Part&#160;3&#151;Transitional provisions

_Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_

10  After Division&#160;707

Insert: 

Division&#160;713&#151;Rules for particular kinds of entities

Table of Subdivisions

713-L	Transitional relief for certain transactions relating to life insurance companies 

Subdivision&#160;713-L&#151;Transitional relief for certain

transactions relating to life insurance companies

Table of sections

713-500	Object of Subdivision
 713-505	When this Subdivision applies (first case)
 713-510	When this Subdivision applies (second case)
 713-515	Entities must choose the relief
 713-520	Conditions
 713-525	Time of transfer
 713-530	What the relief is
 713-535	Subsequent consequences
 713-540	Requirement to notify happening of new event
 713-545	Discount capital gain in certain cases 

713-500  Object of Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The object of this Subdivision is to give an opportunity to a group of

entities that includes a life insurance company to rearrange the assets of the

group for the purposes of one or more of them becoming members of a

consolidated group in a way that does not attract any immediate taxation

consequences.

 </dl></dl>

713-505  When this Subdivision applies (first case)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Subdivision provides for a deferral of the taxation consequences that

would occur because of an event (the _deferral event_) happening

involving an entity (the _originating entity_) and another entity

(the _recipient entity_) if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the event occurs in connection with a life insurance company (the

_member life insurance company_) becoming a member of a

consolidated group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the relevant conditions in section&#160;713-520 are met.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the originating entity is a company, the deferral event referred to in

subsection&#160;(1) is a CGT event referred to in subsection&#160;(4) happening

to a CGT asset (the _original asset_) where, apart from this

Subdivision, the happening of the event would have resulted in:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount (other than a capital gain) being included in the originating

entity's assessable income; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the originating entity making a capital gain.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the originating entity is a trust, the deferral event referred to in

subsection&#160;(1) is a CGT event referred to in subsection&#160;(4) happening

to a CGT asset (also the _original asset_) where, apart from this

Subdivision, the happening of the event would have resulted in:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount (other than a capital gain) being included in the net income of

the trust; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the trustee making a capital gain.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The CGT events are:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>CGT events A1, B1, D1, D2, D3, E2, F1 and F2; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>CGT event C2, but only if the CGT asset that ends is a unit in a unit

trust that is replaced by an equivalent membership interest (the

_replacement interest_) in a company or in another trust.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

713-510  When this Subdivision applies (second case)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Subdivision also provides for a deferral of the taxation consequences

that would occur if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a life insurance company transfers an asset (also the _original asset_) to its virtual PST or from its virtual PST where, apart from

this Subdivision, section&#160;320-200 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ would apply to the transfer; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a life insurance company transfers an asset (also the _original asset_) to its segregated exempt assets where, apart from this

Subdivision, section&#160;320-255 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

would apply to the transfer;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

where the transfer (also the _deferral event_) is made in connection with the life insurance company (also the _member life insurance company_) becoming a member of a consolidated group.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The relevant conditions in section&#160;713-520 must be met.

</dd> </dl></dl>

713-515  Entities must choose the relief

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Subdivision applies only if the originating entity (for a

section&#160;713-505 case) or the life insurance company (for a

section&#160;713-510 case) chooses that it apply.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The choice must be made: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>by the day the originating entity or the life insurance company, or the

head company of the consolidated group of which it is a member, lodges its

income tax return for the income year in which the deferral event happened;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>within a further time allowed by the Commissioner.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

713-520  Conditions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-505 case:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the originating entity must be:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a life insurance company that has virtual PST assets or segregated exempt

assets and that is a member of a consolidatable group; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an entity that is unable to be a member of the same consolidatable group

as a life insurance company because of section&#160;713-510 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>an entity that is, directly or indirectly, a subsidiary of a life

insurance company and is a member of the same consolidated group as the life

insurance company; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the originating entity and the recipient entity must be members of the

same consolidatable group or consolidated group or, if they are not, they would

have been apart from section&#160;713-510 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any asset transferred by the originating entity must be transferred to the

recipient entity at its transfer value.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For both a section&#160;713-505 case and a section&#160;713-510 case:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the total transfer values of the virtual PST assets of the member life

insurance company just before a transfer of assets to which this Subdivision

applies must be the same as the total transfer values of those assets just

after the transfer; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the total transfer values of the segregated exempt assets of the member

life insurance company just before a transfer of assets to which this

Subdivision applies must be the same as the total transfer values of those

assets just after the transfer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Any transfer of an asset under the deferral event must happen on or before

the later of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>30&#160;June 2004; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the head company of the consolidated group of which the member life

insurance company is a member has a substituted accounting period&#151;the end of

the head company's income year in which 30&#160;June 2004 occurs.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

713-525  Time of transfer

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This Act, and the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, apply to the

transfer of an asset to which this Subdivision applies as if the asset had been

transferred just before the member life insurance company became a member of

the consolidated group.

 </dl></dl>

713-530  What the relief is

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-505 case:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the originating entity is a company:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>any amount (other than a capital gain) that would have been included in

the originating entity's assessable income (the _deferred amount_)

as a result of the deferral event is not so included; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any capital gain (the _deferred gain_) that the originating

entity would have made as a result of the deferral event is disregarded; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the originating entity is a trust:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>any amount (other than a capital gain) that would have been included in

the member life insurance company's assessable income (also the _deferred amount_) as a result of the deferral event is not so included; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any capital gain (also the _deferred gain_) that the member

life insurance company would have made as a result of the deferral event is

disregarded.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-510 case:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any amount that would have been included in the member life insurance

company's assessable income (also the _deferred amount_) under

paragraph 320-15(e) or (g) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as a

result of the deferral event is not so included; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any capital gain (also the _deferred gain_) that the member

life insurance company would have made as a result of the deferral event is

disregarded.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

713-535  Subsequent consequences

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if, after the deferral event happens, another event

(the _new event_) happens where the new event is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a CGT event happening to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the original asset; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the deferral event was CGT event C2&#151;the replacement asset; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the recipient entity ceasing to be a member of the consolidated group of

which the member life insurance company is a member; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the recipient entity is a life insurance company:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the original asset being transferred to or from the company's virtual PST

under section&#160;320-180, 320-185 or 320-195 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the original asset being transferred to or from the company's segregated

exempt assets under section&#160;320-235, 320-240 or 320-250 of that Act; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the originating entity is a company&#151;the originating entity ceasing to

exist.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-505 case where the originating entity is a company:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the originating entity must include the deferred amount in its assessable

income for the income year in which the new event happens; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the originating entity is taken, just before the new event happened, to

have made a capital gain equal to the deferred gain.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the originating entity is a subsidiary member of a

consolidated group, the head company of the group will have the amount included

in its assessable income or will make the capital gain.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-505 case where the originating entity is a trust:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the member life insurance company must include the deferred amount in its

assessable income for the income year in which the new event happens; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the member life insurance company is taken, just before the new event

happened, to have made a capital gain equal to the deferred gain.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-505 case where the originating entity is a life

insurance company or a trust and the deferred amount or the deferred gain

relates to an asset that was a virtual PST asset at the time when the deferral

event happened, an amount equal to the deferred amount or deferred gain is

taken to be an amount of assessable income to which subsection 320-205(3) of

the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ applies for the relevant entity.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-510 case: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the member life insurance company must include the deferred amount in its

assessable income for the income year in which the new event happens; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the member life insurance company is taken, just before the new event

happened, to have made a capital gain equal to the deferred gain.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>In addition, if the deferral event involved the transfer of assets from

the member life insurance company's virtual PST, an amount equal to the

deferred amount or deferred gain is taken to be an amount of assessable income

to which subsection 320-205(3) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

applies for the relevant entity.

</dd> </dl></dl>

713-540  Requirement to notify happening of new event

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For a section&#160;713-505 case, the recipient entity must, if it is not a

member of the same consolidated group as the originating entity when the new

event happens, notify the originating entity in the approved form of the

happening of the new event within 60 days after the new event happens.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) does not apply if the new event is the originating entity ceasing to exist. </dd> </dl></dl>

713-545  Discount capital gain in certain cases

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ applies as if the capital gain

referred to in paragraph 713-535(2)(b), (3)(b) or (5)(b) were a discount

capital gain if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the asset to which the deferral event happened is a virtual PST asset;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset was acquired less than 12 months before the deferral event

happened; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the new event happens at least 12 months after the asset was acquired.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Taxation Administration Act 1953_

11  At the end of section&#160;286-75 of Schedule&#160;1

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>You are also liable to an administrative penalty if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>you are required under section&#160;713-540 of the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_ to notify another entity of the

happening of an event by a particular day; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>you do not notify the other entity of the happening of that event by that

day.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

12  At the end of subsection 286-80(2) of Schedule&#160;1

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

	; or (c)	for failing to notify the happening of an event as mentioned in

subsection 286-75(4)&#151;1 penalty unit for each period of 28 days or part of a

period of 28 days starting on the day when the notification is due and ending

when you notify the happening of the event (up to a maximum of 5 penalty units).

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;7&#151;Consolidation: interactions between Consolidation rules and other rules

Part&#160;1&#151;New Division&#160;715 inserted in the Income Tax

Assessment Act 1997

1  After Division&#160;713

Insert: 

Division&#160;715&#151;Interactions between this Part and other areas

of the income tax law

Object

715-15  Object of this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The object of this Subdivision is to give effect to the purposes of

Subdivision&#160;165-CC (about change of ownership or control of a company that

has an unrealised net loss) in these cases:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>on formation of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group, a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset

held directly by the <sup>*</sup>head company is affected by that Subdivision,

and the <sup>*</sup>same business test is failed;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on an entity becoming a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a consolidated

group, an asset consisting of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>membership interest that a <sup>*</sup>member of the group

(including a chosen transitional entity under Division&#160;701 of the

_Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_) holds in the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a liability that the entity owes to such a member;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		is affected by that Subdivision, and the same business test is failed;

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>on a company becoming a subsidiary member:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a CGT asset of the company that becomes an asset of the head company is

affected by that Subdivision; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>because the company is a chosen transitional entity, the asset does not

have its tax cost reset; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the same business test is failed;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>on an entity ceasing to be a subsidiary member, a CGT asset of the head

company that becomes an asset of the entity is affected by that Subdivision,

and the same business test is failed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subdivision&#160;165-CC also affects an entity that has

deferred losses under Subdivision&#160;170-D on assets that it formerly owned.

Subdivision&#160;715-D gives effect to the purposes of Subdivision&#160;165-CC

if such an entity becomes a member of a consolidated group.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This Subdivision achieves its object by supplementing and modifying the

application of Subdivision&#160;165-CC to take account of how the rest of this

Part treats <sup>*</sup>members of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group (in

particular the provisions about entities becoming or ceasing to be members).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-25.]_

Effect on Subdivision&#160;165-CC of a company becoming a member

of a consolidated group

715-25  Subdivision&#160;165-CC stops applying to earlier changeover time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>At and after the time (the _membership time_) when a company

becomes a <sup>*</sup>member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group,

Subdivision&#160;165-CC does not apply to the company in relation to a

<sup>*</sup>changeover time that happened before the membership time, except

for the purposes of section&#160;715-30 (which defines _165-CC tagged asset_).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subdivision&#160;165-CC is about change of ownership or

control of a company that has an unrealised net loss. Note 2:	If the company has 165-CC tagged assets at the membership time, there are further consequences under this Subdivision and Subdivision&#160;715-D. 	Also, Subdivision&#160;165-CC can apply to the head company of the group in relation to a changeover time that happens for it at or after the membership time. See section&#160;715-75\.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) continues to have effect even if the company later

stops being a <sup>*</sup>member of the group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

715-30  Meaning of _165-CC tagged asset_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>CGT asset is a _165-CC tagged asset_ of a company

at a particular time if, and only if:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that time is at or after the most recent <sup>*</sup>changeover time (if

any) for the company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at that changeover time, the company had an unrealised net loss under

section&#160;165-115E; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the asset is covered by subsection 165-115A(1A) as applying to that

changeover time; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the company would not, at that changeover time, satisfy the maximum net

asset value test under section&#160;152-15; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>if the company has chosen under subsection 165-115A(1B) in relation to

that changeover time&#151;the company <sup>*</sup>acquired the asset for $10,000 or

more.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

715-35  Meaning of _final RUNL_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A company's _final RUNL_ at a particular time (the _test time_) is the amount that would have been the company's

<sup>*</sup>residual unrealised net loss at the time of:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if no event that subsection 165-115BB(2) refers to as a relevant event

actually happens at the test time&#151;a notional event of that kind happening at

the test time; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;a notional event of that kind that happens at the test time,

and that the company determines under paragraph 165-115BB(1)(b) to have

happened _later_ than each event that actually happened at that time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This Subdivision reduces a company's final RUNL as amounts

of it are applied for various purposes.

 </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-50.]_

165-CC tagged assets that affect tax cost setting amounts

715-50  Step 1 amount is reduced if membership interest in subsidiary member is 165-CC tagged asset and same business test is failed

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The amount taken into account under subsection 705-65(1) (about the cost

of membership interests in the joining entity) for a <sup>*</sup>membership

interest that a <sup>*</sup>member of the joined group holds in the joining

entity at the joining time is reduced if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apart from this section, the amount would be the membership interest's

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base (if appropriate, as modified by a later provision

of section&#160;705-65); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the membership interest is at that time a <sup>*</sup>165-CC tagged asset

of that member, and that member owned it at the <sup>*</sup>changeover time for

that member; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that member's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL just before the joining time was

greater than nil; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>that member does _not_ satisfy the <sup>*</sup>same business test for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period (the _same business test period_) consisting of the

<sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>trial year; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the time (the _test time_) just before the

<sup>*</sup>changeover time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If at the joining time that <sup>*</sup>member holds:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>2 or <sup>*</sup>more membership interests in the joining entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at least one membership interest in the joining entity, and at least one

membership interest in another member of the joined group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

this section applies to each such membership interest in whichever order that member determines.

_Amount of reduction_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The amount taken into account under subsection 705-65(1) is reduced to the

<sup>*</sup>membership interest's <sup>*</sup>market value at the joining

time.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, if that member's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL (as reduced by any previous reductions under this section) is _less than_ the difference between: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a);

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>market value referred to in subsection&#160;(3);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the amount taken into account under subsection 705-65(1) is instead reduced by that final RUNL.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>That <sup>*</sup>final RUNL is reduced by the amount of the reduction

under subsection&#160;(3) or (4).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Rights and options to acquire membership interests_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>Subsection 705-65(6) (which treats rights and options as membership

interests) also applies for the purposes of this section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

715-55  Step 2 amount is affected if liability of subsidiary member is 165-CC tagged asset of another group member and same business test is failed

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The amount (the _comparison amount_) applicable under the

table in subsection 705-75(2) (about reduction of the step 2 amount) for an

accounting liability of the joining entity that is owed to a <sup>*</sup>member

of the joined group at the joining time is reduced if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apart from this section, the comparison amount would be the

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base (if appropriate, as modified by a later provision

of section&#160;705-75) of the asset of that member that is constituted by the

accounting liability; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset is at that time a <sup>*</sup>165-CC tagged asset of that

member, and that member owned it at the <sup>*</sup>changeover time; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that member's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL just before the joining time (as

reduced by any reductions under section&#160;715-50) was greater than nil;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>that member does _not_ satisfy the <sup>*</sup>same business test for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period (the _same business test period_) consisting of the

<sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>trial year; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the time (the _test time_) just before the

<sup>*</sup>changeover time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph&#160;(1)(c) has the effect that if both this

section and section&#160;715-50 apply to the same member of the joined group,

section&#160;715-50 is applied before this section.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If at the joining time that <sup>*</sup>member holds:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>2 or <sup>*</sup>more assets constituted by accounting liabilities of the

joining entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at least one asset constituted by an accounting liability of the joining

entity, and at least one asset constituted by an accounting liability of

another member of the group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

this section applies to each such asset in whichever order that member determines.

_Amount of reduction_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The comparison amount is reduced to the asset's <sup>*</sup>market value

at the joining time.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, if that member's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL (as reduced by any previous reductions under section&#160;715-50 or this section) is _less than_ the difference between: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a);

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset's <sup>*</sup>market value at the joining time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

the comparison amount is instead reduced by that final RUNL.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>That <sup>*</sup>final RUNL is reduced by the amount of the reduction

under subsection&#160;(3) or (4).

</dd> </dl></dl>

165-CC tagged assets that form loss denial pools of head company

when consolidated group is formed

715-60  Assets that the head company already owns

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>At the time (the _formation time_) when a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group comes into existence under paragraph

703-5(1)(a), a _loss denial pool_ of the <sup>*</sup>head company

is created if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the formation time is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the

head company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the formation time, the head company owns a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that is a <sup>*</sup>165-CC tagged asset of the head company at that

time; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>that it owned at the <sup>*</sup>changeover time; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>that is not a <sup>*</sup>membership interest in a <sup>*</sup>member of

the group; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>that is not a right or option (including a contingent right or option),

created or issued by a member of the group, to acquire such a membership

interest; and</dd>

<dt>(v)</dt><dd>that is not constituted by a liability owed to the head company by a

member of the group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		or 2 or more such assets; and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the head company's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL just before the formation time

(as reduced by any reductions under section&#160;715-50 or 715-55) was greater

than nil; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the head company does _not_ satisfy the <sup>*</sup>same business

test for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period (the _same business test period_) consisting of the

head company's <sup>*</sup>trial year; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the time (the _test time_) just before the

<sup>*</sup>changeover time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph&#160;(1)(c) has the effect that if the head

company has 165-CC tagged assets that are affected by section&#160;715-50 or

715-55 (because they are membership interests in, or accounting liabilities

owed by, another group member), those sections are applied before this section.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>When it is created, the pool consists of the one or more <sup>*</sup>CGT

assets referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(b), and its _loss denial balance_ is equal to the <sup>*</sup>final RUNL referred to in

paragraph&#160;(1)(c).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The pool is distinct from any other loss denial pool of

the head company, for example, one created at the formation time under

section&#160;715-70\. Note 2:	170-D deferred losses on 165-CC tagged assets of the head company may be added to the pool by subsection 715-355(1).  </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-70.]_

715-70  Assets of subsidiary member that become those of head company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>At the time (the _formation time_) when an entity becomes a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group, a _loss denial pool_ of the <sup>*</sup>head company of the group is created if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the formation time is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the

head company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity is a chosen transitional entity under Division&#160;701 of the

_Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>subsection&#160;(2) or (4) of this section is satisfied.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	If the entity is a chosen transitional entity,

section&#160;701-15 of the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_

prevents:

 </dl></dl>

*	section&#160;701-10 (cost to head company of assets that entity brings into group); and
 *	subsection 701-35(4) (setting value of trading stock at tax-neutral amount);

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

	of this Act from applying to the entity's assets in relation to

the formation time. Note 2:	The pool is distinct from any other loss denial pool of the head company, for example, one created under this section because another entity becomes a subsidiary member of the group at the formation time.  </dl></dl>

_Joining entity has 165-CC tagged assets_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This subsection is satisfied if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset of the entity, or each of 2 or more CGT assets of

the entity:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is a <sup>*</sup>165-CC tagged asset of the entity at the formation time;

and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>was owned by the entity at the <sup>*</sup>changeover time; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>is not a <sup>*</sup>membership interest in a <sup>*</sup>member of the

group; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>is not a right or option (including a contingent right or option),

created or issued by a member of the group, to acquire such a membership

interest; and</dd>

<dt>(v)</dt><dd>is not constituted by a liability owed to the entity by a member of the

group at the formation time; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL just before the formation time (as

reduced by any reductions under section&#160;715-50 or 715-55) was greater than

nil; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity does _not_ satisfy the <sup>*</sup>same business test for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period (the _same business test period_) consisting of the

entity's <sup>*</sup>trial year; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the time (the _test time_) just before the

<sup>*</sup>changeover time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph&#160;(2)(b) has the effect that if the entity has

165-CC tagged assets that are affected by section&#160;715-50 or 715-55

(because they are membership interests in, or accounting liabilities owed by,

another group member), those sections are applied before this section.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>When it is created because of subsection&#160;(2), the pool consists of

the one or more <sup>*</sup>CGT assets referred to in paragraph&#160;(2)(a),

and its _loss denial balance_ is equal to the <sup>*</sup>final

RUNL referred to in paragraph&#160;(2)(b).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	170-D deferred losses on 165-CC tagged assets of the head

company may be added to the pool by subsection 715-355(2).

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Entity has loss denial pool_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>This subsection is satisfied if, just before the formation time, the

entity had a <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>When it is created because of subsection&#160;(4), the <sup>*</sup>head company's loss denial pool: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>consists of the one or more <sup>*</sup>CGT assets of which the entity's

loss <sup>*</sup>denial pool consisted; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>has a _loss denial balance_ equal to the <sup>*</sup>loss

denial balance of the entity's loss denial pool;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

just before the formation time. 

How Subdivision&#160;165-CC applies to consolidated groups

715-75  Extension of single entity rule and entry history rule

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subsection 701-1(1) (Single entity rule) and section&#160;701-5 (Entry

history rule) also have effect for all the purposes of Subdivision&#160;165-CC

(about change of ownership or control of a company that has an unrealised net

loss).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	One consequence of this is that the head company is the

only member of a consolidated group that can have a changeover time and be

subject to consequences under Subdivision&#160;165-CC. The head company is

treated as owning all CGT assets owned by group members, and as making relevant

losses.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section is not intended to limit the effect that subsection 701-1(1)

and section&#160;701-5 have apart from this section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Effect on Subdivision&#160;165-CC of entity leaving consolidated group

715-80  Application of sections&#160;715-85 to 715-110

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Sections&#160;715-85 to 715-110 apply if, at a particular time (the

_leaving time_), an entity (the _leaving entity_)

ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated

group.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	If a changeover time happened to the head company at or

after the group came into existence and before the leaving time,

Subdivision&#160;165-CC does _not_ apply to the head company at and after

the leaving time, in respect of assets that leave with the leaving entity, in

relation to the changeover time. 	This is because the head company can no longer make a capital loss, or become entitled to a deduction, in respect of a CGT event happening to any of those assets. Note 2:	If, just before the leaving time, the head company had a loss denial pool, see section&#160;715-120\.  </dl></dl>

715-85  First changeover time for leaving company at or after leaving time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If the leaving entity is a company, its first <sup>*</sup>changeover time at

or after the leaving time is determined:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>on the basis that the reference time under subsection 165-115A(2A) is the

one that would be used in determining whether the leaving time was a changeover

time for the _head company_; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>making the additional assumptions in section&#160;715-290.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the leaving entity is a trust, it cannot have a

changeover time (because Subdivision&#160;165-CC applies only to companies), so

section&#160;715-95 applies to it instead: see subsection 715-95(2).

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

715-90  How same business test applies if leaving time is changeover time for leaving company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the leaving entity is a company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the leaving time is a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the leaving entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The continuity period referred to in subsection 165-115B(3), as applying

to the leaving time as a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the leaving entity, is

taken to have ended just _after_ that time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This ensures that the same business test is applied to the

business that the leaving entity carries on at the leaving time: see subsection

165-13(3).

 </dl></dl>

715-95  If ownership and control of leaving entity have _not_ changed since head company's last changeover time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the leaving entity is a company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the leaving time is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the

leaving entity; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>just before the leaving time, the <sup>*</sup>head company owned at least

one <sup>*</sup>CGT asset:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that was a <sup>*</sup>165-CC tagged asset just before the leaving time;

and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>that it owned at the latest changeover time for the head company at or

after the group came into existence and before the leaving time; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>at least one asset covered by paragraph&#160;(c) is an asset (a

_leaving asset_) that becomes an asset of the leaving entity at the

leaving time because subsection 701-1(1) (Single entity rule) ceases to apply

to the entity; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the head company's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL at the leaving time is greater

than nil.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section also applies if the leaving entity is a trust.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>head company does _not_ satisfy the <sup>*</sup>same business test for: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the period (the _same business test period_) starting at the

_earlier_ of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the time 12 months before the leaving time; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>when the head company came into existence;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		and ending just before the leaving time; and

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the time (the _test time_) just before the

<sup>*</sup>changeover time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the head company must make one of the choices for which sections&#160;715-100, 715-105 and 715-110 provide.

For provisions about making one of these choices, 
see sections&#160;715-175 to 715-185\. 

715-100  First choice: adjustable values of leaving assets reduced to nil

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The first choice is to reduce the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each

leaving asset to nil. The choice has effect accordingly, just before the

leaving time. The <sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL is

_not_ reduced because of it.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The consequences of the choice are worked out under

section&#160;715-145.

 </dl></dl>

715-105  Second choice: head company's final RUNL applied in reducing adjustable values of leaving assets that are loss assets

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The second choice is to reduce under this section the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each leaving asset (a _loss asset_)

for which the <sup>*</sup>head company would have had a notional capital loss,

or notional revenue loss, under section&#160;165-115F at the time (the

_test time_) just before the leaving time if the test time had been

a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the head company. The choice has effect

accordingly.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The consequences of the choice are worked out under this

section and section&#160;715-145.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>2 or more entities cease to be <sup>*</sup>subsidiary members of the

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group at the leaving time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>2 or more of them make the second choice;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the choices have effect in whichever order the <sup>*</sup>head company determines.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>This section applies to each of the loss assets in order, according to

their respective <sup>*</sup>adjustable values (apart from this section) at the

test time: from largest to smallest. (If an asset has more than one such

adjustable value, use the greater or greatest of them.)</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>At the test time, the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the loss asset is reduced to the asset's <sup>*</sup>market value at that time.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>However, if the <sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL at the leaving time (as reduced by any previous reductions under this section) is _less than_ the difference between: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the loss asset (apart from this

section) at the test time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset's <sup>*</sup>market value at the test time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the adjustable value is instead reduced at the test time by that final RUNL.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>That <sup>*</sup>final RUNL is reduced by the amount of the reduction

under subsection&#160;(4) or (5). If 2 or more such reductions are made for the

same asset (because it has 2 or more different characters), that final RUNL is

reduced by the greater or greatest of the reductions.

</dd> </dl></dl>

715-110  Third choice: loss denial pool of leaving entity created

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The third choice can be made only if every asset covered by paragraph

715-95(1)(c) is a leaving asset. The choice is to have a _loss denial pool_ of the leaving entity created at the leaving time, consisting of

every leaving asset. (To avoid doubt, the choice can be made even if the

leaving entity is not a company.)</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A choice under this section has effect accordingly. The pool is distinct from any other loss denial pool of the leaving entity.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>When the pool is created, its _loss denial balance_ is equal to the <sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL at the leaving time. </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the head company makes this choice, the leaving entity

can choose to cancel the loss denial pool by reducing reduced cost bases of

assets in the pool: see section&#160;715-185.

 </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-120.] Back to Top_

Effect of assets in loss denial pool of head company becoming

assets of leaving entity

715-120  What happens

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at a particular time (the _leaving time_), an entity (the

_leaving entity_) ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>just before the leaving time, the <sup>*</sup>head company had a

<sup>*</sup>loss denial pool; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>at the leaving time, at least one <sup>*</sup>CGT asset (a _leaving asset_) that was in the pool just before that time becomes a CGT asset

of the leaving entity because subsection 701-1(1) (Single entity rule) ceases

to apply to the entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Each leaving asset leaves the <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool at the leaving

time.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the leaving entity is a company and the leaving time is _not_ a

<sup>*</sup>changeover time for the leaving entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the leaving entity is a trust;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the <sup>*</sup>head company must make one of the choices for which sections&#160;715-125, 715-130 and 715-135 provide.

For provisions about making one of these choices, 
see sections&#160;715-175 to 715-185\. 

715-125  First choice: adjustable values of leaving assets reduced to nil

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The first choice is to reduce the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each

leaving asset to nil. The choice has effect accordingly, just before the

leaving time. The <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance of the <sup>*</sup>head

company's <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool is _not_ reduced because of it.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The consequences of the choice are worked out under

section&#160;715-145.

 </dl></dl>

715-130  Second choice: pool's loss denial balance applied in reducing adjustable values of leaving assets that are loss assets

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The second choice is to reduce under this section the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each leaving asset (a _loss asset_)

for which the <sup>*</sup>head company would have had a notional capital loss,

or notional revenue loss, under section&#160;165-115F at the time (the

_test time_) just before the leaving time if the test time had been

a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the head company. The choice has effect

accordingly.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The consequences of the choice are worked out under this

section and section&#160;715-145.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>2 or more entities cease to be <sup>*</sup>subsidiary members of the

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>2 or more of them make the second choice;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the choices have effect in the same order as the entities cease being subsidiary members. If 2 or more of the entities ceased at the same time, their choices have effect in whichever order the <sup>*</sup>head company determines.

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>This section applies to each of the loss assets in order, according to

their respective <sup>*</sup>adjustable values (apart from this section) at the

test time: from largest to smallest. (If an asset has more than one such

adjustable value, use the greater or greatest of them.)</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>At the test time, the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the loss asset is reduced to the asset's <sup>*</sup>market value at that time.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>However, if the <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance (as reduced by any previous reductions under this section or section&#160;715-160) of the <sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool<sup> </sup>is _less than_ the difference between: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the loss asset (apart from this

section) at the test time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset's <sup>*</sup>market value at the test time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the adjustable value is instead reduced at the test time by that loss denial balance.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>That <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance is reduced at the leaving time by the

amount of the reduction under subsection&#160;(3) or (4). If 2 or more such

reductions are made for the same asset (because it has 2 or more different

characters), that loss denial balance is reduced by the greater or greatest of

the reductions.

</dd> </dl></dl>

715-135  Third choice: loss denial pool of leaving entity created

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The third choice can be made only if every asset that was in the

<sup>*</sup>loss denial pool just before the leaving time is a leaving asset.

The choice is to have a _loss denial pool_ of the leaving entity

created at the leaving time, consisting of every leaving asset. (To avoid

doubt, the choice can be made even if the leaving entity is not a company.)</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A choice under this section has effect accordingly. The pool is distinct from any other loss denial pool of the leaving entity.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>When the leaving entity's loss denial pool is created, its _loss denial balance_ equals the loss denial balance of the head company's loss denial pool (as reduced by any previous reductions under section&#160;715-130 or 715-160). </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the head company makes this choice, the leaving entity

can choose to cancel the loss denial pool by reducing reduced cost bases of

assets in the pool: see section&#160;715-185.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The head company's <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool ceases to exist when the

leaving entity's loss denial pool is created.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-145.]_

Effect of first and second choices on various kinds of assets

715-145  Effect of choice on adjustable value of leaving asset

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section has effect for the purposes of determining the consequences

of a choice under any of sections&#160;715-100, 715-105, 715-125, 715-130 and

715-185 (the _choice provisions_) for a leaving asset.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The asset's _adjustable value_ at the time (the _test time_) just before the leaving time is worked out under this table. (If the asset is covered by 2 or more items, there are consequences for it under the choice provisions and this section in respect of each of the items.) </dd> </dl></dl>
