<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If any of the choice provisions reduces at the test time the asset's

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value, the thing identified for the asset under the

table in subsection&#160;(2) of this section is reduced by the same amount.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(3) has effect for the purposes of working out under section&#160;711-30 the <sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>terminating value for the asset at the leaving time. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_\[The next section is section 715-155.]_

General provisions about loss denial pools

715-155  When asset leaves pool

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>CGT asset leaves a <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>just after a <sup>*</sup>realisation event happens to the asset, unless

the realisation event is the ending of an income year (in the case of an item

of <sup>*</sup>trading stock); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>as mentioned in subsection 715-120(2) (when it becomes an asset of the

leaving entity).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

715-160  How loss denial balance is applied to losses realised on assets in pool

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If, apart from this section, a loss would be <sup>*</sup>realised for

income tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to a

<sup>*</sup>CGT asset when it is in a <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool of an

entity, the loss is reduced by the lesser of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount of the loss; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the pool's <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance (as reduced by any previous

reductions under section&#160;715-130 or this subsection);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

and the loss denial balance is reduced by the same amount.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) applies to <sup>*</sup>realisation events in the order

in which they happen. If 2 or more happen at the same time, it applies to them

in whichever order the entity determines.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) reduces a <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance after section&#160;715-130 does, unless the <sup>*</sup>realisation event happens _before_ the leaving time referred to in that section. </dd> </dl></dl>

715-165  When pool ceases to exist

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool of a company ceases to exist when there is

a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the company.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The CGT assets in the pool then become subject to the

application of Subdivision&#160;165-CC (about change of ownership or control of

a company that has an unrealised net loss).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool of any entity ceases to exist:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>when there are no <sup>*</sup>CGT assets, and no <sup>*</sup>170-D

deferred losses, in the pool; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>just after the <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance becomes nil; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>when the entity becomes a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>as mentioned in subsection 715-135(4).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-175.]_

Choices under this Subdivision

715-175  When choice must be made

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A choice under section&#160;715-95 or 715-120 must be made within 6 months

after the leaving time, or within a further period allowed by the

Commissioner.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>After that 6 months, or that further period, the head company is taken to have made the first choice under section&#160;715-100 or 715-125 unless it is established that the head company made a different choice within that 6 months or further period. </dd> </dl></dl>

715-180  Head company to notify leaving entity of choice

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Within one month after making a choice under section&#160;715-95 or

715-120, or within a further period allowed by the Commissioner, the head

company must give the leaving entity written notice of the choice.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the choice is to have a <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool of the leaving entity created at the leaving time, the notice must also specify the pool's <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance at that time. </dd> </dl></dl>

715-185  Leaving entity may choose to cancel loss denial pool by reducing adjustable values of assets in the pool

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Within 6 months after a <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool is created under

section&#160;715-110 or 715-135, or within a further period allowed by the

Commissioner, the leaving entity may choose to be treated as if the

<sup>*</sup>head company had instead made:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first choice under section&#160;715-100 or 715-125; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the second choice under section&#160;715-105 or 715-130;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as specified by the leaving entity in its choice.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the leaving entity makes a choice under subsection&#160;(1):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool ceases to exist just after the leaving

time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the leaving time, the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each

<sup>*</sup>CGT asset in the pool is reduced to what it would have been at that

time if the head company had instead made the choice specified by the leaving

entity in its choice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The choice by the leaving entity does not affect how subsection 715-135(4)

applies to the <sup>*</sup>head company.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This means that the head company's loss denial pool still

ceases to exist.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;715-B&#151;How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to

consolidated groups and leaving entities

Table of sections

How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to consolidated groups

715-215	Extension of single entity rule and entry history rule
 715-225	Working out adjusted unrealised loss using individual asset method
 715-230	No reductions or other consequences for interests subject to loss cancellation under Subdivision&#160;715-H

How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to leaving entity that is a company

715-240	Application of sections&#160;715-245 to 715-260
 715-245	If ownership or control of leaving entity has altered since head company's last alteration time or formation of group
 715-250	If head company has had an alteration time but ownership and control of leaving entity have not altered since
 715-255	Consequences if leaving entity is a loss company at the leaving time
 715-260	If neither of sections&#160;715-245 and 715-250 applies

How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to leaving entity that is a trust

715-270	Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies 

How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to consolidated groups

715-215  Extension of single entity rule and entry history rule

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subsection 701-1(1) (Single entity rule) and section&#160;701-5 (Entry

history rule) also have effect for all the purposes of Subdivision&#160;165-CD

(about reductions after alterations in ownership or control of loss company).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	One consequence of this is that the head company is the

only member of a consolidated group that can have an alteration time and be

subject to reductions or other consequences under Subdivision&#160;165-CD. The

head company is treated as owning all CGT assets owned by group members, and as

making relevant losses. 	Another consequence is for working out who has a relevant equity interest or relevant debt interest in a company that has an alteration time at which it is a loss company but not a member of a consolidated group. Interests in the loss company that are owned by subsidiary members of the group are treated as being owned by the head company.  </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section is not intended to limit the effect that subsection 701-1(1)

and section&#160;701-5 have apart from this section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-225.]_

715-225  Working out adjusted unrealised loss using individual asset method

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For the purposes of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>using the <sup>*</sup>individual asset method to work out whether the

<sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group has an adjusted

unrealised loss under section&#160;165-115U at an <sup>*</sup>alteration time;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>working out under section&#160;165-115W whether the head company of a

consolidated group has a trading stock decrease at an alteration time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

step 1 of the method statement in subsection 165-115U(1), or step 2 of the method statement in subsection 165-115W(1), does _not_ apply to an amount that was counted in respect of a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset at an earlier time if:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>at the time (the _joining time_) when an entity became a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of the group, the asset became an asset of the

head company because of subsection 701-1(1) (Single entity rule); and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the earlier time is an <sup>*</sup>alteration time that happened in

respect of the entity before the joining time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

unless the entity is a chosen transitional entity under Division&#160;701 of the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the joining entity is a chosen transitional entity,

section&#160;701-15 of the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_

prevents:

 </dl></dl>

*	section&#160;701-10 (cost to head company of assets that entity brings into group); and
 *	subsection 701-35(4) (setting value of trading stock at tax-neutral amount);

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

	of this Act from applying to the assets of the joining entity in

relation to the joining time. 	If the joining entity is _not_ a chosen transitional entity, it is assumed that the process of resetting the tax costs of its assets will bring their tax costs into closer alignment to their market values, and so remove the need to consider unrealised losses on those assets that existed before the joining time.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section has effect despite section&#160;701-5 (Entry history rule).

</dd> </dl></dl>

715-230  No reductions or other consequences for interests subject to loss cancellation under Subdivision&#160;715-H

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If section&#160;715-610 reduces a loss that would otherwise be

<sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event

that happens to an interest in, or a debt owed by, a company,

sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB do not apply (and are taken never to have

applied) to the interest or debt, in relation to an <sup>*</sup>alteration time

that happened for the company during the ownership period referred to in

subsection 715-610(2).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section&#160;715-610 is about cancelling a loss on a

realisation event for a direct or indirect interest in a subsidiary member of a

consolidated group. Note 2:	Sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB are about the consequences that an alteration time for a loss company has for relevant equity interests and relevant debt interests in the company.  </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-240.] Back to Top_

How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to leaving entity that is a company

715-240  Application of sections&#160;715-245 to 715-260

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Sections&#160;715-245 to 715-260 affect how Subdivision&#160;165-CD (about

reductions after alterations in ownership or control of loss company) applies

to a company (the _leaving entity_) at and after the time (the

_leaving time_) when it ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary

member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group that came into existence at a

particular time (the _formation time_).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If a trust ceases to be a subsidiary member of a

consolidated group: see section&#160;715-270.

 </dl></dl>

715-245  If ownership or control of leaving entity has altered since head company's last alteration time or formation of group

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if the leaving time would be an

<sup>*</sup>alteration time for the leaving entity if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the reference time under subsection 165-115L(2) or 165-115M(2) were:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if at least one alteration time has occurred in relation to the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group since the

formation time and before the leaving time&#151;the time just after the most recent

such alteration time; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;the formation time; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the additional assumptions in section&#160;715-290 were made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The leaving time is an _alteration time_ for the leaving

entity.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	One consequence of this is that the reference time for

working out the leaving entity's _next_ alteration time is the time just

after the leaving time.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The leaving entity is a _loss company_ at that

<sup>*</sup>alteration time if, and only if, it has an <sup>*</sup>adjusted

unrealised loss at that time. If so, that adjusted unrealised loss is the

leaving entity's _overall loss_ at that time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection&#160;(4) affects how the leaving entity works

out its adjusted unrealised loss at the leaving time in some cases. Note 2:	If the leaving entity is a loss company at the leaving time, section&#160;715-255 provides for the consequences.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the leaving entity uses the <sup>*</sup>individual asset method of

working out its <sup>*</sup>adjusted unrealised loss at that

<sup>*</sup>alteration time, then for the purposes of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>step 1 of the method statement in subsection 165-115U(1); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the method statement in subsection 165-115W(1);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the leaving entity is taken to have had no earlier alteration time. 

715-250  If head company has had an alteration time but ownership and control of leaving entity have not altered since

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at least one <sup>*</sup>alteration time has occurred in relation to the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group since the

formation time and before the leaving time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the leaving time is _not_ an <sup>*</sup>alteration time for the

leaving entity under subsection 715-245(2).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The leaving time is an _alteration time_ for the leaving

entity.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>However, for the purposes of determining when the leaving entity's _next_ <sup>*</sup>alteration time happens, the reference time under subsection 165-115L(2) or 165-115M(2) is the time just after the most recent alteration time for the <sup>*</sup>head company _before_ the leaving time.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The leaving entity is a _loss company_ at the leaving time if, and only if, the <sup>*</sup>head company would have had an <sup>*</sup>adjusted unrealised loss at the most recent <sup>*</sup>alteration time (the _head company alteration time_) for the head company before the leaving time if that adjusted unrealised loss (if any) were worked out on the basis that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the head company chooses whether the <sup>*</sup>individual asset method

or the <sup>*</sup>global method is used; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset is taken into account only if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the head company owned it at the head company alteration time; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>it becomes a CGT asset of the leaving entity at the leaving time because

subsection 701-1(1) (the single entity rule) ceases to apply to the entity; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the individual asset method is used, then for the purposes of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>step 1 of the method statement in subsection 165-115U(1); and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the method statement in subsection 165-115W(1);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		the head company had no earlier alteration time.

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the leaving entity is a <sup>*</sup>loss company at the leaving time,

its _overall loss_ at that time is the <sup>*</sup>adjusted

unrealised loss worked out under subsection&#160;(4).

</dd> </dl></dl>

715-255  Consequences if leaving entity is a loss company at the leaving time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;715-245 or 715-250 applies; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the leaving entity is a <sup>*</sup>loss company at the leaving time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the head company must choose whether subsection&#160;(2) or (3) of this section has effect for the purposes of applying, to each <sup>*</sup>membership interest in the leaving entity, in relation to the time just before the leaving time, whichever of these provisions is appropriate:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>subsection 701-55(3) (about trading stock);</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>subsection 701-55(5), but only so far as it relates to working out the

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a <sup>*</sup>membership interest that was

<sup>*</sup>acquired on or after 20&#160;September 1985;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>subsection 701-55(6) (about revenue assets).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;701-55 is about setting the tax cost of an

asset.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>head company chooses this subsection, the interest's

<sup>*</sup>tax cost setting amount (apart from this section) just before the

leaving time is reduced to nil.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>head company chooses this subsection, the interest's <sup>*</sup>tax cost setting amount (apart from this section) just before the leaving time is reduced by the adjustment amount under section&#160;165-115ZB, which is calculated on the basis that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>just before the leaving time, all the <sup>*</sup>membership interests in

the leaving entity constituted a single relevant equity interest under

section&#160;165-115X that the head company had in the leaving entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the adjustment amount is worked out and applied in accordance with

subsection 165-115ZB(6), but disregarding the paragraphs of that subsection

except paragraphs 165-115ZB(6)(a) and (d).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>head company's choice must be made within 6 months after

the leaving time, or within a further period allowed by the Commissioner.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>After that 6 months, or that further period, the head company is taken to have chosen subsection&#160;(2) unless it is established that the head company made a different choice within that 6 months or further period. </dd> </dl></dl>

_Rights and options to acquire membership interests_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>Subsection 711-15(2) (which treats rights and options as membership

interests) also applies for the purposes of this section, on the basis that the

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group referred to in section&#160;715-240 is the old

group referred to in that subsection.

</dd> </dl></dl>

715-260  If neither of sections&#160;715-245 and 715-250 applies

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>no <sup>*</sup>alteration time has occurred in relation to the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group since the

formation time and before the leaving time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the leaving time is _not_ an <sup>*</sup>alteration time for the

leaving entity under subsection 715-245(2).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The leaving entity's first <sup>*</sup>alteration time after the leaving

time is determined:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>on the basis that the reference time under subsection 165-115L(2) or

165-115M(2) is the time just after the formation time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>making the additional assumptions in section&#160;715-290.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the leaving entity uses the <sup>*</sup>individual asset method of

working out its <sup>*</sup>adjusted unrealised loss at that first

<sup>*</sup>alteration time, then for the purposes of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>step 1 of the method statement in subsection 165-115U(1); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the method statement in subsection 165-115W(1);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the leaving entity is taken to have had no earlier alteration time.

_\[The next section is section 715-270.]_

How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to leaving entity that is a trust

715-270  Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>At and after the time (the _leaving time_) when a trust ceases

to be a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group,

Subdivision&#160;165-CD (about reductions after alterations in ownership or

control of loss company) applies to the trust on the basis set out in this

section.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The trust is taken to be a company.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The leaving time is the only _alteration time_ in respect of the trust.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The trust is a _loss company_ at that time if, and only if, it has an <sup>*</sup>adjusted unrealised loss at that time. If so, that adjusted unrealised loss is its _overall loss_ at that time.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the trust is a <sup>*</sup>loss company at the leaving time, the <sup>*</sup>head company must choose whether subsection&#160;(6) or (7) of this section has effect for the purposes of applying, to each <sup>*</sup>membership interest in the trust, in relation to the time just before the leaving time, whichever of these provisions is appropriate: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>subsection 701-55(3) (about trading stock);</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>subsection 701-55(5), but only so far as it relates to working out the

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a <sup>*</sup>membership interest that was

<sup>*</sup>acquired on or after 20&#160;September 1985;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>subsection 701-55(6) (about revenue assets).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;701-55 is about setting the tax cost of an

asset.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>head company chooses this subsection, the interest's

<sup>*</sup>tax cost setting amount (apart from this section) just before the

leaving time is reduced to nil.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>head company chooses this subsection, the interest's <sup>*</sup>tax cost setting amount (apart from this section) just before the leaving time is reduced by the adjustment amount under section&#160;165-115ZB, which is calculated on the basis that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>just before the leaving time:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>all the <sup>*</sup>membership interests in the leaving entity constituted

a single relevant equity interest under section&#160;165-115X that the

<sup>*</sup>head company had in the leaving entity; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>each of those interests was an equity under section&#160;165-115X that

the <sup>*</sup>head company had in the leaving entity; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the adjustment amount is worked out and applied in accordance with

subsection 165-115ZB(6), but disregarding the paragraphs of that subsection

except paragraphs 165-115ZB(6)(a) and (d).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>head company's choice must be made within 6 months after

the leaving time, or within a further period allowed by the Commissioner.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>After that 6 months, or that further period, the head company is taken to have chosen subsection&#160;(6) unless it is established that the head company made a different choice within that 6 months or further period. </dd> </dl></dl>

_Rights and options to acquire membership interests_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(10)</dt><dd>Subsection 711-15(2) (which treats rights and options as membership

interests) also applies for the purposes of this section, on the basis that the

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group is the old group referred to in that subsection.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;715-C&#151;Common rules for the purposes of

Subdivisions&#160;715-A and 715-B

715-290  Additional assumptions to be made when using reference time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The additional assumptions to be made are that, throughout the period

starting at the reference time and ending just before the leaving time:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the leaving entity was in existence; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>head company held and beneficially owned all the

<sup>*</sup>membership interests in the leaving entity (instead of whoever

actually did); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>those membership interests remained the same; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the head company directly controlled the voting power in the leaving entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;715-D&#151;Treatment of company's deferred losses

under Subdivision&#160;170-D on joining a consolidated group

Table of sections

Key terminology

715-310	What is a _170-D deferred loss_, and when it _revives_

Deferred loss on 165-CC tagged asset

<center>Back to Top</center>

715-355	Head company's own deferred losses at formation time
 715-360	Deferred losses brought in by subsidiary member
 715-365	How loss denial balance is applied when 170-D deferred loss revives 

Key terminology

715-310  What is a _170-D deferred loss_, and when it _revives_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>capital loss, deduction, or partner's share of a deduction,

that section&#160;170-270 (about transactions within linked groups) requires to

be disregarded is a _170-D deferred loss_ made:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>by the company that paragraph 170-255(1)(a) refers to as the originating

company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the time of the event that paragraph refers to as the deferral event;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>on the <sup>*</sup>CGT asset <sup>*</sup>acquired by the other entity

referred to in that paragraph.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>170-D deferred loss _revives_ at the time when

section&#160;170-275 (as applying in relation to the deferral event) treats the

originating company as having made a <sup>*</sup>capital loss, or having become

entitled to a deduction, in respect of that asset.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-355.]_

Deferred loss on 165-CC tagged asset

715-355  Head company's own deferred losses at formation time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if, at the time (the _formation time_)

when a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group comes into existence, the

<sup>*</sup>head company has (otherwise than because of section&#160;701-5

(Entry history rule)) a <sup>*</sup>170-D deferred loss that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it made on a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset that is a <sup>*</sup>165-CC tagged

asset of the head company because of paragraph 165-115A(1A)(b) (which covers

CGT assets on which it has 170-D deferred losses); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>has not <sup>*</sup>revived.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool of the <sup>*</sup>head company is

created under section&#160;715-60 at the formation time, each <sup>*</sup>170-D

deferred loss of that kind that the head company has at that time is added to

the loss denial pool at that time.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Otherwise, a _loss denial pool_ of the <sup>*</sup>head company is created at the formation time if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the formation time is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the

head company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the head company's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL just before the formation time

(as reduced by any reductions under section&#160;715-50 or 715-55) was greater

than nil; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the head company does _not_ satisfy the <sup>*</sup>same business

test for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period (the _same business test period_) consisting of the

head company's <sup>*</sup>trial year; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the time (the _test time_) just before the

<sup>*</sup>changeover time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph&#160;(3)(b) has the effect that if the head

company has 165-CC tagged assets that are affected by section&#160;715-50 or

715-55 (because they are membership interests in, or accounting liabilities

owed by, another group member), those sections are applied before this section.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>When it is created because of subsection&#160;(3), the pool consists of

each <sup>*</sup>170-D deferred loss covered by subsection&#160;(2), and its

_loss denial balance_ is equal to the <sup>*</sup>final RUNL

referred to in paragraph&#160;(3)(b).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The pool is distinct from any other loss denial pool of the

head company, for example, one created at the formation time under

section&#160;715-360.

 </dl></dl>

715-360  Deferred losses brought in by subsidiary member

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if, just before the time (the _membership time_) when a company (the _deferred loss company_) becomes

a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group, it had a

<sup>*</sup>170-D deferred loss that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it made on a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset that is a <sup>*</sup>165-CC tagged

asset of the company at the membership time because of paragraph

165-115A(1A)(b) (which covers CGT assets on which it has 170-D deferred

losses); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>as at the membership time has not <sup>*</sup>revived.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a <sup>*</sup>loss denial pool of the <sup>*</sup>head company is

created under subsection 715-70(2) because of the deferred loss company

becoming a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of the group, each <sup>*</sup>170-D

deferred loss of that kind that the deferred loss company had just before the

membership time is added to the loss denial pool at that time.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Otherwise, a _loss denial pool_ of the <sup>*</sup>head company is created at the membership time if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the membership time is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>changeover time for the

head company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the deferred loss company's <sup>*</sup>final RUNL just before the

membership time (as reduced by any reductions under section&#160;715-50 or

715-55) was greater than nil; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the deferred loss company does _not_ satisfy the <sup>*</sup>same

business test for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period (the _same business test period_) consisting of the

deferred loss company's <sup>*</sup>trial year; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the time (the _test time_) just before the

<sup>*</sup>changeover time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The 170-D deferred losses become those of the head

company at the formation time because of section&#160;701-5 (Entry history

rule). Note 2:	Paragraph&#160;(3)(b) has the effect that if the deferred loss company has other 165-CC tagged assets affected by section&#160;715-50 or 715-55 (because the membership time is when the group comes into existence, and the other 165-CC tagged assets are membership interests in, or accounting liabilities owed by, another group member), those sections are applied before this section.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>When it is created because of subsection&#160;(3), the pool consists of

each 170-D deferred loss covered by subsection&#160;(2), and its _loss denial balance_ is equal to the <sup>*</sup>final RUNL referred to in

paragraph&#160;(3)(b).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The pool is distinct from any other loss denial pool of the

head company, for example, one created under this section because another

entity becomes a subsidiary member of the group at the membership time.

 </dl></dl>

715-365  How loss denial balance is applied when 170-D deferred loss revives

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a <sup>*</sup>170-D deferred loss on a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset is in a

<sup>*</sup>loss denial pool of an entity when the loss <sup>*</sup>revives,

the <sup>*</sup>capital loss or deduction that section&#160;170-275 would,

apart from this section, treat the entity as having made or become entitled to

at that time in respect of the asset is reduced by the lesser of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount of the capital loss or deduction; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the pool's <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance (as reduced by any previous

reductions under section&#160;715-130, subsection 715-160(1) or this

subsection);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

and the loss denial balance is reduced by the same amount.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) applies to <sup>*</sup>170-D deferred losses in the

order in which they <sup>*</sup>revive. If 2 or more revive at the same time,

it applies to them in whichever order the entity determines.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) reduces a <sup>*</sup>loss denial balance before section&#160;715-130 does, unless the <sup>*</sup>realisation event happens _after_ the leaving time referred to in that section. </dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next Subdivision is Subdivision 715-G.]_

Subdivision&#160;715-G&#151;How value shifting rules apply to a

consolidated group

Table of sections

715-410	Extension of single entity rule and entry history rule
 715-450	No reductions or other consequences for interests subject to loss cancellation under Subdivision&#160;715-H 

715-410  Extension of single entity rule and entry history rule

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subsection 701-1(1) (Single entity rule) and section&#160;701-5 (Entry

history rule) also have effect for all the purposes of Part&#160;3-95 (Value

shifting).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	One consequence of this for the operation of

Division&#160;727 (about indirect value shifting affecting interests in

companies and trusts, and arising from non-arm's length dealings) is that

economic benefits provided by or to a subsidiary member of a consolidated group

are treated as provided by or to the head company of the group. As a result:

 </dl></dl>

*	the head company is the only group member that can be a losing entity or gaining entity for an indirect value shift; and
 *	economic benefits provided by one group member to another are treated as provided by the head company to itself, and so have no relevance to Division&#160;727.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

	Another consequence is that the head company is treated as

owning all interests owned by group members in a losing entity or gaining

entity that is not a group member.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section is not intended to limit the effect that subsection 701-1(1)

and section&#160;701-5 have apart from this section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 715-450.]_

715-450  No reductions or other consequences for interests subject to loss cancellation under Subdivision&#160;715-H

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If section&#160;715-610 reduces a loss that would otherwise be

<sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event

that happens to an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an entity:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the loss is not subject to reduction under Division&#160;723 (Direct value

shifting by creating right over non-depreciating asset) or 727 (Indirect value

shifting); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is not, and is taken never to

have been, reduced under Division&#160;725 because of a <sup>*</sup>direct

value shift during the ownership period referred to in subsection 715-610(2);

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is not, and is taken never to

have been, reduced under Division&#160;727 because of an <sup>*</sup>indirect

value shift during that period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;715-610 is about cancelling a loss on a

realisation event for a direct or indirect interest in a subsidiary member of a

consolidated group.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Subdivision&#160;715-H&#151;Cancelling loss on realisation event for

direct or indirect interest in a subsidiary member of a consolidated group

Table of sections

715-610	Cancellation of loss
 715-615	Exception for interests in entity leaving consolidated group
 715-620	Exception if loss attributable to certain matters 

715-610  Cancellation of loss

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section reduces to nil a loss that would otherwise be

<sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event

that happens to an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest (the _realised interest_) in an entity (the _first entity_) when it is

owned by another entity (the _owner_), if the conditions in

subsections&#160;(2) and (4) are met.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The first condition is that, at some time during the period (the _ownership period_) when the owner owned the realised interest: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first entity was a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group, and the owner was _not_ a

<sup>*</sup>member of the group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an <sup>*</sup>external indirect equity or loan

interest in a subsidiary member of a consolidated group; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an

entity that, at that time:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>owned an equity or loan interest in a subsidiary member of a consolidated

group; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>was _not_ a member of the group; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an

entity that owned at that time an external indirect equity or loan interest in

a subsidiary member of a consolidated group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an entity (the _test entity_) is an _external indirect equity or loan interest_

in a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group if, and

only if, neither the owner of the interest nor the test entity is a member of

the group and:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the test entity owns an equity or loan interest in the subsidiary member;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the test entity owns an equity or loan interest that is an external

indirect equity or loan interest in the subsidiary member because of one or

more other applications of this subsection.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The second condition is that, at the same or a different time during the

ownership period:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the owner was, or <sup>*</sup>controlled (for value shifting purposes),

the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group because of

which the first condition is satisfied; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the owner was an <sup>*</sup>associate of an entity that, at the same or a

different time during the ownership period, was, or controlled (for value

shifting purposes), the head company of such a consolidated group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

715-615  Exception for interests in entity leaving consolidated group

_Membership interests in leaving entity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the realised interest is a <sup>*</sup>membership interest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>during the ownership period the first entity ceased to be a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

the first condition in section&#160;715-610 cannot be satisfied, because of that consolidated group, at a time when the first entity was a member of the group, unless the interest needed to be disregarded under section&#160;703-35 (about employee shares) in order for the first entity to be a member of the group at that time.

_Liabilities owed by leaving entity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the realised interest:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>consists of a liability owed by the first entity to the owner; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>became an asset of the owner because subsection 701-1(1) (the single

entity rule) ceased to apply to the first entity when it ceased to be a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the first condition in section&#160;715-610 cannot be satisfied, because of that consolidated group, at a time when the first entity was a member of the group. 

715-620  Exception if loss attributable to certain matters

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The loss is not reduced if all of it can be shown to be attributable to

things other than these:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>something that would be reflected in what would, apart from this Part, be

an overall loss under section&#160;165-115R or 165-115S, of a

<sup>*</sup>member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group (an _excluded group_) because of which the first condition in section&#160;715-610 is

satisfied, at an <sup>*</sup>alteration time for that member;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift for which, apart from this Part, a

member of an excluded group would be the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If only part of the loss can be shown to be attributable to things other

than the ones listed in subsection&#160;(1), the loss is reduced to the amount

of that part.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Assessment Act 1997

Subdivision&#160;719-T&#151;Interactions between this Part and other

areas of the income tax law: special rules for MEC groups

How Subdivision&#160;165-CC applies to MEC groups

719-700  Changeover times under section&#160;165-115C or 165-115D

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section has effect for the purposes of determining whether a time

(the _test time_) is a <sup>*</sup>changeover time under

section&#160;165-115C (about changes in ownership) or 165-115D (about changes

in control) in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Modified meaning of reference time_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The _reference time_ is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if no <sup>*</sup>changeover time has occurred in respect of the head

company since the group came into existence and before the test time&#151;when the

group came into existence; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;the time just after the last such changeover time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(2) of this section has effect despite subsection

165-115A(2A).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Assumptions to make_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Assume that, while the <sup>*</sup>MEC group exists:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>top company for the group holds and beneficially owns all

the <sup>*</sup>membership interests in the <sup>*</sup>head company (instead

of whoever actually does); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>those membership interests remain the same; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the top company directly controls the voting power in the head company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

719-705  Additional changeover times for head company of MEC group

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The time when a <sup>*</sup>potential MEC group ceases to exist is a

_changeover time_ in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group if, just before that time, the potential MEC group's

membership was the same as the membership of the MEC group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The changeover times in subsections&#160;(1), (2) and (3)

are based on the events described in subsections 719-280(2), (3) and (4), each

of which causes the test company referred to in section&#160;719-280 to be

assumed to fail the continuity of ownership test in section&#160;165-12.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If something:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>happens at a time in relation to <sup>*</sup>membership interests in one

or more of these entities:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a company that was just before that time a <sup>*</sup>member of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group and an <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 company of the

<sup>*</sup>top company for the MEC group;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an entity interposed between a company described in subparagraph&#160;(i)

and the company that was the top company for the group just before that time;

and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>does not cause the <sup>*</sup>potential MEC group whose membership is the

same as the membership of the MEC group to cease to exist, but does cause a

change in the identity of the top company for the potential MEC group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

that time is a _changeover time_ in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>MEC group.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The time when a <sup>*</sup>MEC group ceases to exist because there ceases

to be a <sup>*</sup>provisional head company of the group is a _changeover time_ in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>MEC

group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 719-720.]_

<center>Back to Top</center>

How Subdivision&#160;165-CD applies to MEC groups

719-720  Alteration times under section&#160;165-115L or 165-115M

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section has effect for the purposes of determining whether a time

(the _test time_) is an <sup>*</sup>alteration time under

section&#160;165-115L (about alterations in ownership) or 165-115M (about

alterations in control) in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Modified meaning of reference time_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The _reference time_ is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if no <sup>*</sup>alteration time has occurred in respect of the head

company since the group came into existence and before the test time&#151;when the

group came into existence; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;the time just after the last such alteration time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In applying subsection&#160;(2), disregard an <sup>*</sup>alteration time

arising under subsection 719-725(4).</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(2) of this section has effect despite subsections 165-115L(2) and 165-115M(2). </dd> </dl></dl>

_Assumptions to make_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>Assume that, while the <sup>*</sup>MEC group exists:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>top company for the group holds and beneficially owns all

the <sup>*</sup>membership interests in the <sup>*</sup>head company (instead

of whoever actually does); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>those membership interests remain the same; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the top company directly controls the voting power in the head company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

719-725  Additional alteration times for head company of MEC group

_Additional alteration times based on section 719-280_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The time when a <sup>*</sup>potential MEC group ceases to exist is an

_alteration time_ in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group if, just before that time, the potential MEC group's

membership was the same as the membership of the MEC group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The alteration times in subsections&#160;(1), (2) and (3)

are based on the events described in subsections 719-280(2), (3) and (4), each

of which causes the test company referred to in section&#160;719-280 to be

assumed to fail the continuity of ownership test in section&#160;165-12.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If something:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>happens at a time in relation to <sup>*</sup>membership interests in one

or more of these entities:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a company that was just before that time a <sup>*</sup>member of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group and an <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 company of the

<sup>*</sup>top company for the MEC group;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an entity interposed between a company described in subparagraph&#160;(i)

and the company that was the top company for the group just before that time;

and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>does not cause the <sup>*</sup>potential MEC group whose membership is the

same as the membership of the MEC group to cease to exist, but does cause a

change in the identity of the top company for the potential MEC group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

that time is an _alteration time_ in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>MEC group.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The time when a <sup>*</sup>MEC group ceases to exist because there ceases

to be a <sup>*</sup>provisional head company of the group is an

_alteration time_ in respect of the <sup>*</sup>head company of the

<sup>*</sup>MEC group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Additional alteration times based on Subdivision 719-K_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If Subdivision&#160;719-K (MEC group cost setting rules: pooling cases)

applies, the time just before the trigger time referred to in paragraph

719-555(1)(a) is an _alteration time_ in respect of the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>MEC group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

719-730  Some alteration times only affect interests in top company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if an <sup>*</sup>alteration time (except one arising

under subsection 719-725(4)) happens for the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB apply, in relation to the alteration time, to an interest or debt that is, or is part of, a relevant equity interest or relevant debt interest that an entity has in the <sup>*</sup>head company just before the <sup>*</sup>alteration time, _only if_ the interest or debt is: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the <sup>*</sup>top company for

the MEC group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest in the top company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB are about the

consequences that an alteration time for a loss company has for relevant equity

interests and relevant debt interests in the company.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In determining what is a relevant equity interest or relevant debt

interest that an entity has in the <sup>*</sup>head company just before the

<sup>*</sup>alteration time, make the assumptions in subsection 719-720(5).

</dd> </dl></dl>

719-735  Some alteration times affect only pooled interests

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB do not apply in relation to an

<sup>*</sup>alteration time that happens for the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group because of subsection 719-725(4) (trigger time for MEC

group cost setting rules: pooling cases).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Instead, Subdivision&#160;719-K applies to the <sup>*</sup>MEC group, in relation to the trigger time, on the basis that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>what would, apart from this section, be the pooled cost amount for the

purposes of the formulas in subsections 719-570(1) and (2) is reduced by the

amount of the <sup>*</sup>head company's overall loss under

section&#160;165-115R or 165-115S at that alteration time; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>paragraph&#160;(a) of this subsection _only_ affects the application

of those formulas because of subsection 719-570(3) (to work out the

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a <sup>*</sup>membership interest).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 719-755.]_

How indirect value shifting rules apply to a MEC group

719-755  Effect on MEC group cost setting rules if head company is losing entity or gaining entity for indirect value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section has effect for the purposes of working out the consequences

(if any) of an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift if the <sup>*</sup>losing

entity or <sup>*</sup>gaining entity is the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group. (Subsection&#160;(3) has effect in addition to

section&#160;727-455.)</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest can be an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>head company only if it is: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the <sup>*</sup>top company for

the MEC group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest in the top company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;719-K (MEC group cost setting rules: pooling cases)

applies to the <sup>*</sup>MEC group, in relation to the first time referred to

in that Subdivision as a trigger time that happens at or after the

<sup>*</sup>IVS time, on the basis that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>what would, apart from this section, be the pooled cost amount for the

purposes of the formulas in subsections 719-570(1) and (2) is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the <sup>*</sup>head company is the <sup>*</sup>losing entity&#151;reduced;

or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the head company is the gaining entity&#151;increased;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		by the amount of the indirect value shift; and

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>paragraph&#160;(a) of this subsection also affects the application of

those formulas because of subsection 719-570(3) (to work out the

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a <sup>*</sup>membership interest).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_\[The next section is section 719-775.]_

Cancelling loss on realisation event for direct or indirect

interest in a subsidiary member of a MEC group

719-775  Cancellation of loss

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section reduces to nil a loss that would otherwise be

<sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event

that happens to an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest (the _realised interest_) in an entity (the _first entity_) when it is

owned by another entity (the _owner_), if the conditions in

subsections&#160;(2) and (4) are met.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The first condition is that, at some time during the period (the _ownership period_) when the owner owned the realised interest: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first entity was a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group (except an <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 company), and the owner was

_not_ a <sup>*</sup>member of the group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an <sup>*</sup>external indirect equity or loan

interest in a subsidiary member of a MEC group (except an eligible tier-1

company); or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an

entity that, at that time:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>owned an equity or loan interest in a subsidiary member of a MEC group

(except an eligible tier-1 company); and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>was _not_ a member of the group; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an equity or loan interest in an entity that

owned at that time an external indirect equity or loan interest in a subsidiary

member of a MEC group (except an eligible tier-1 company); or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an equity or loan interest, or an

<sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest, in an eligible tier-1 company

that was a member of a MEC group at that time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an entity (the _test entity_) is an _external indirect equity or loan interest_

in a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group if, and only if,

neither the owner of the interest nor the test entity is a member of the group

and:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the test entity owns an equity or loan interest in the subsidiary member;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the test entity owns an equity or loan interest that is an external

indirect equity or loan interest in the subsidiary member because of one or

more other applications of this subsection.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The second condition is that, at the same or a different time during the

ownership period:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the owner was, or <sup>*</sup>controlled (for value shifting purposes),

the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group because of which the

first condition is satisfied; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the owner was an <sup>*</sup>associate of an entity that, at the same or a

different time during the ownership period, was, or controlled (for value

shifting purposes), the head company of such a MEC group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

719-780  Exception for pooled interests in eligible tier-1 companies

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The first condition in section&#160;719-775 cannot be satisfied, because of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group, at a time when the realised interest was a

<sup>*</sup>pooled interest in an <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 company that is a

member of the group.

 </dl></dl>

719-785  Exception for interests in top company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The first condition in section&#160;719-775 cannot be satisfied, because of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group, at a time when:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first entity was the <sup>*</sup>top company for the MEC group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the realised interest was an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest

in the top company for the MEC group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

719-790  Exception for interests in entity leaving MEC group

_Membership interests in leaving entity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the realised interest is a <sup>*</sup>membership interest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>during the ownership period the first entity ceased to be a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the first condition in section&#160;719-775 cannot be satisfied, because of that MEC group, at a time when the first entity was a member of the group, unless the interest needed to be disregarded under section&#160;719-30 (about employee shares) in order for the first entity to be a member of the group at that time.

_Liabilities owed by leaving entity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the realised interest:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>consists of a liability owed by the first entity to the owner; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>became an asset of the owner because subsection 701-1(1) (the single

entity rule) ceased to apply to the first entity when it ceased to be a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the first condition in section&#160;719-775 cannot be satisfied, because of that MEC group, at a time when the first entity was a member of the group. 

719-795  Exception if loss attributable to certain matters

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The loss is not reduced if all of it can be shown to be attributable to

things other than these:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>something that would be reflected in what would, apart from this Part, be

an overall loss under section&#160;165-115R or 165-115S, of a

<sup>*</sup>member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group (an _excluded group_)

because of which the first condition in section&#160;719-775 is satisfied, at

an <sup>*</sup>alteration time for that member;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift for which, apart from this Part, a

member of an excluded group would be the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If only part of the loss can be shown to be attributable to things other

than the ones listed in subsection&#160;(1), the loss is reduced to the amount

of that part.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next Subdivision is Subdivision 719-X.]_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

(the _leaving time_); and</dd>

later time for an attribution account entity in relation to the
