9  At the end of Division&#160;717

Add: 

Subdivision&#160;717-F&#151;Elections etc. relating to CFCs, FIFs and

FLPs: entry rules

<center>Back to Top</center>

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;717-F 717-270  What this Subdivision is about
 This Subdivision deals with the effect upon certain elections etc. relating to CFCs, FIFs and FLPs when an entity becomes a subsidiary member of a consolidated group.

Table of sections

Application and object

717-275	Application
 717-280	Object of this Subdivision

Elections etc.

717-285	Pre-joining-time irrevocable elections etc. by joining entity not inherited by head company
 717-290	Pre-joining-time actions of joining entity do not prevent head company from electing to apply the calculation method

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Application and object

717-275  Application

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This Subdivision operates for the purposes of Part&#160;X and Part&#160;X1 of

the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ if an entity (the _joining entity_) becomes a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group at a time (the _joining time_).

 </dl></dl>

717-280  Object of this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The object of this Subdivision is to provide:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that the <sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group

does not inherit the joining entity's irrevocable declarations, elections,

choices or selections; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that pre-joining-time actions of the joining entity do not prevent the

head company from electing to apply the calculation method to determine whether

foreign investment fund income accrued from a FIF.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Elections etc.

717-285  Pre-joining-time irrevocable elections etc. by joining entity not inherited by head company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If at the joining time an irrevocable declaration, election, choice or

selection made by the joining entity under Part&#160;X or XI of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ is in force, then, for the head company core

purposes, the <sup>*</sup>head company of the group is _not_ taken to have

made the declaration, election, choice or selection.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The entry history rule in section&#160;701-5 would

otherwise have had the effect that the head company is taken to have made the

declaration etc. Note 2:	Declarations etc. actually made by the head company would apply to interests in CFCs, FIFs or FLPs of which the head company becomes the holder under the single entity rule as a result of the joining entity becoming a subsidiary member.  </dl></dl>

717-290  Pre-joining-time actions of joining entity do not prevent head company from electing to apply the calculation method

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Any entitlement of the <sup>*</sup>head company of the group to make an

election under subsection 535(3) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_

for the head company core purposes is not affected by anything done by the

joining entity before the joining time.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The entry history rule in section&#160;701-5 would

otherwise have had the effect that actions of the joining entity would be

treated as those of the head company. Depending on the nature of the actions,

this could have prevented the head company from making the election mentioned

above.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;717-G&#151;Elections etc. relating to CFCs, FIFs and

FLPs: exit rules

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;717-G

<center>Back to Top</center>
 717-295  What this Subdivision is about
 This Subdivision deals with the effect upon certain elections etc. relating to CFCs, FIFs and FLPs when an entity ceases to be a subsidiary member of a consolidated group.

Table of sections

Application and object

717-300	Application
 717-305	Object of this Subdivision

Elections etc.

717-310	Pre-leaving-time irrevocable declarations, elections, choices and selections by head company not inherited by leaving entity
 717-315	Pre-leaving-time actions of head company do not prevent leaving entity from electing to apply the calculation method

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Application and object

717-300  Application

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This Subdivision operates for the purposes of Part&#160;X and Part&#160;X1 of

the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ if an entity (the _leaving entity_) ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group at a time (the _leaving time_).

 </dl></dl>

717-305  Object of this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The object of this Subdivision is to provide:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that the leaving entity does not inherit the <sup>*</sup>head company's

irrevocable declarations, elections, choices or selections; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that pre-leaving-time actions of the head company do not prevent the

leaving entity from electing to apply the calculation method to determine

whether foreign investment fund income accrued from a FIF.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Elections etc.

717-310  Pre-leaving-time irrevocable declarations, elections, choices and selections by head company not inherited by leaving entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If at the leaving time an irrevocable declaration, election, choice or

selection made by the <sup>*</sup>head company of the group under Part&#160;X

or XI of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ is in force, then, for the

entity core purposes, so far as they relate to the leaving entity after the

leaving time, the leaving entity is _not_ taken to have made the election.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The exit history rule in section&#160;701-40 would

otherwise have had the effect that the leaving entity is taken to have made the

declaration etc.

 </dl></dl>

717-315  Pre-leaving-time actions of head company do not prevent leaving entity from electing to apply the calculation method

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Any entitlement of the leaving entity to make an election under subsection

535(3) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ for the entity core

purposes, so far as they relate to the leaving entity after the leaving time,

is not affected by anything done by the <sup>*</sup>head company before that

time.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The exit history rule in section&#160;701-40 would

otherwise have had the effect that actions of the head company would be treated

as those of the leaving entity. Depending on the nature of the actions, this

could have prevented the leaving entity from making the election mentioned

above.

 </dl></dl>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;9&#151;Consolidation: foreign dividend accounts  
**</center>

Part&#160;1&#151;Basic amendments

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

1  At the end of Division&#160;717

Add: 

<center>Back to Top</center>

Subdivision&#160;717-J&#151;Foreign dividend accounts

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;717-J 717-500  What this Subdivision is about
 Only the head company of a consolidated group has an operating foreign dividend account, so only the head company can make an FDA declaration to relieve from withholding tax a dividend paid by a member of the group to a foreign resident. The balance of the account reflects what has happened to all members of the group.

Table of sections

Object

717-505	Object of this Subdivision

Treatment of foreign dividend accounts around joining time

717-510	No FDA surplus for joining company

Single entity rule for foreign dividend accounts

717-515	Single entity rule for FDA credits and FDA debits

FDA declaration for dividend paid by subsidiary member

717-520	Head company may make FDA declaration
 717-525	Multiple FDA declarations for dividends paid on same day
 717-530	Extended operation of sections&#160;717-520 and 717-525

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Object

717-505  Object of this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The object of this Subdivision is to affect the operation of Subdivision B

of Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ so that each <sup>*</sup>consolidated group operates a single

<sup>*</sup>foreign dividend account, by ensuring that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>FDA credit and an <sup>*</sup>FDA debit arise so that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the balance of the foreign dividend account of the <sup>*</sup>head

company of the group reflects the balance of the foreign dividend account of a

company that becomes a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of the group; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the balance of the foreign dividend account of the subsidiary member of

the group is nil; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the head company is the only <sup>*</sup>member of the group that can have

an <sup>*</sup>FDA surplus; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the head company can make an <sup>*</sup>FDA declaration relating to a

dividend (within the meaning of that Subdivision) or <sup>*</sup>non-share

dividend paid by any member of the group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In this Act:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_FDA credit_ has the same meaning as in Subdivision B of

Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_. _FDA debit_ has the same meaning as in Subdivision B of Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_. _FDA declaration_ has the same meaning as in Subdivision B of Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_. _FDA surplus_ has the same meaning as in Subdivision B of Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_. _foreign dividend account_ has the same meaning as in Subdivision B of Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_.  </dl></dl>

Treatment of foreign dividend accounts around joining time

717-510  No FDA surplus for joining company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates for the purposes of Subdivision B of

Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_

if a company (the _joining company_) becomes a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group at a time

(the _joining time_) just after another time (the _balance time_).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the joining company has an <sup>*</sup>FDA surplus at the balance time: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>FDA debit equal to the FDA surplus arises for the joining

company at the balance time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>FDA credit equal to the FDA surplus arises for the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the group at the joining time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the joining company's total <sup>*</sup>FDA debits arising before the

balance time exceed its total <sup>*</sup>FDA credits arising before the

balance time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an FDA credit equal to the excess arises for the joining company at the

balance time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an FDA debit equal to the excess arises for the <sup>*</sup>head company

of the group at the joining time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsections&#160;(2) and (3) of this section, work out

whether, when, and how much (if any) of, an <sup>*</sup>FDA debit arises for

the joining company under paragraph 128TB(1)(d) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ in relation to the income year that actually includes the balance

time as if that income year:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>started at:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the start of that income year; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the joining company ceased to be a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group after the start of that income year but before

the balance time&#151;the time the joining company last ceased to be a subsidiary

member of a consolidated group before the balance time; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ended just before the balance time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This ensures that the FDA debit (if any) for the joining

company under paragraph 128TB(1)(d) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ arises just before the balance time, so that it is taken into account

for the purposes of subsections&#160;(2) and (3) of this section.

 </dl></dl>

Single entity rule for foreign dividend accounts

717-515  Single entity rule for FDA credits and FDA debits

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If a company is a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated

group for any period, it and any other subsidiary member of the group are taken

for the purposes of sections&#160;128TA and 128TB of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ to be parts of the <sup>*</sup>head company of the

group, rather than separate entities, during that period.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	This has the effect that:

 </dl></dl>

(a)	FDA credits and FDA debits arise under sections&#160;128TA and 128TB (respectively) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ for the head company of a consolidated group but not for a subsidiary member of the group; and
 (b)	the shareholdings of all members of a consolidated group are aggregated to work out whether dividends paid to a member are non-portfolio dividends for the purposes of those sections.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 2:	Section&#160;717-10 may also affect FDA credits and FDA

debits for the head company of a consolidated group. It treats the head company

as having paid and been personally liable for foreign tax on foreign income

included in its assessable income if a subsidiary member of the group actually

paid and was personally liable for the tax.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

FDA declaration for dividend paid by subsidiary member

717-520  Head company may make FDA declaration

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>on a day, a company that is a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group pays dividends (within the meaning of

Subdivision B of Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_) to shareholders (within the meaning of that Act) in

respect of <sup>*</sup>shares in the company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on the day, there is an <sup>*</sup>FDA surplus for the <sup>*</sup>head

company of the consolidated group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>head company may make an <sup>*</sup>FDA declaration

specifying an <sup>*</sup>FDA declaration percentage under subsection 128TC(1)

of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ as if the head company were paying

the dividends.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the head company makes an FDA declaration:

 </dl></dl>

(a)	an FDA debit equal to the sum of the FDA declaration amounts worked out for the dividends by reference to the FDA declaration percentage will arise for the head company just after the start of the day under section&#160;128TB of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_; and
 (b)	foreign resident shareholders in the subsidiary member will be relieved from withholding tax on amounts of the dividends not exceeding the FDA declaration amounts.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In this Act:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_FDA declaration percentage_ has the same meaning as in Subdivision

B of Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, subsection 128TC(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_

operates in relation to the <sup>*</sup>FDA declaration percentage on the basis

that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company mentioned in that subsection is the <sup>*</sup>subsidiary

member; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the dividends were paid to shareholders in respect of <sup>*</sup>shares

in the subsidiary member.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, subsection 128TC(5) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ operates in relation to the <sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>FDA

declaration by reference to amounts worked out on the basis described in

subsection&#160;(4) of this section.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, sections&#160;128TD and 128TE of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ apply to the <sup>*</sup>head company in relation to an <sup>*</sup>FDA declaration made because of subsection&#160;(2) of this section, even though the shareholders and dividends mentioned in those sections applying in relation to the declaration are shareholders in, and dividends paid by, the <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member. </dd> </dl></dl>

717-525  Multiple FDA declarations for dividends paid on same day

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group makes 2 or more <sup>*</sup>FDA declarations

relating to dividends (within the meaning of Subdivision B of Division&#160;11A

of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_) paid by

<sup>*</sup>members of the group on a single day.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	It does not matter whether all those FDA declarations are

made under section&#160;128TC of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ as

affected by section&#160;717-520 of this Act or whether one of the declarations

relates to dividends actually paid by the head company.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_FDA declaration percentage in each FDA declaration_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>FDA declaration percentage for each <sup>*</sup>FDA

declaration must be such that the sum of the amounts worked out under

subsection 128TC(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ in relation to

the FDA declarations is not greater than the <sup>*</sup>head company's

<sup>*</sup>FDA surplus at the beginning of the day.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If (apart from this subsection) that sum _is_ greater than the <sup>*</sup>head company's <sup>*</sup>FDA surplus at the beginning of the day, each of the <sup>*</sup>FDA declarations is valid but is taken always to have effect as if the <sup>*</sup>FDA declaration percentage specified in the declaration were the percentage worked out using the formula: </dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1214.gif)</sub>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Subsection 128TC(5) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ does not

operate in relation to any of the <sup>*</sup>FDA declarations.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Penalty for statement reflecting wrong percentage_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>Subsection 128TE(1) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ operates

as if it referred to subsection&#160;(3) of this section instead of subsection

128TC(5) of that Act.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, subsection&#160;(3) of this section does not prevent subsection 128TE(1) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ from making the <sup>*</sup>head company liable to pay additional tax by way of penalty. </dd> </dl></dl>

717-530  Extended operation of sections&#160;717-520 and 717-525

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;128AAA (the _applied section_) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies to sections&#160;717-520 and 717-525 of this

Act in the same way as the applied section applies to Division&#160;11A of

Part&#160;III of that Act.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;128AAA of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies Division&#160;11A of Part&#160;III of that Act to non-share

dividends in the same way as that Division applies to dividends.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;719-X&#151;International tax rules

Table of sections

 719-905	Transfer of balance of foreign dividend accounts on change in identity of provisional head company 

Foreign dividend accounts

719-900  General rules about foreign dividend accounts

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section modifies the effect that Subdivision&#160;717-J has in

relation to a <sup>*</sup>MEC group because of section&#160;719-2.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Except as provided by this section, section&#160;719-2

gives Subdivision&#160;717-J effect in relation to a MEC group in a way

corresponding to the way in which that Subdivision has effect in relation to a

consolidated group.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;717-J has effect in relation to the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of the <sup>*</sup>MEC group in a way

corresponding to the way in which that Subdivision has effect in relation to

the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;717-J has effect as if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<sup>*</sup>MEC group at a time were not a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of the

group at the time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each company that is a <sup>*</sup>member of the MEC group at the time and

is not the provisional head company at the time were a subsidiary member of the

group at the time.

</dd>

<center>Back to Top</center>

719-905  Transfer of balance of foreign dividend accounts on change in identity of provisional head company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>cessation event happens to the <sup>*</sup>provisional head

company (the _old company_) of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>another company (the _new company_) is appointed as the

provisional head company of the group under subsection 719-60(3).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The appointment of the new company as the provisional head

company of a MEC group under subsection 719-60(3) is taken to have come into

force immediately after the cessation event.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If there was an <sup>*</sup>FDA surplus for the old company at the time of

the <sup>*</sup>cessation event:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>FDA debit equal to the FDA surplus arises for the old

company at the time of the cessation event; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>FDA credit equal to the FDA surplus arises for the new

company when it is appointed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the old company's total <sup>*</sup>FDA debits arising before the time

of the <sup>*</sup>cessation event exceeded its total <sup>*</sup>FDA credits

arising before that time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an FDA credit equal to the excess arises for the old company at the time

of the cessation event; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an FDA debit equal to the excess arises for the new company when it is

appointed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

12  Application of amendments

(1)	The amendments of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ made by this Schedule apply in relation to a dividend or non-share dividend paid after 30&#160;June 2003 by a company, except a company to which subitem&#160;(2) applies.
 (2)	This subitem and subitem&#160;(3) apply to a company if:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company becomes a member of a consolidated group or MEC group on the

day (the _consolidation day_) the group comes into existence; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the consolidation day either is before 1&#160;July 2003 or is both:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the first day of the first income year starting after 30&#160;June 2003 of

the group's head company (for a consolidated group) or provisional head company

(for a MEC group) on the consolidation day; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>before 1&#160;July 2004; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the company was not a member of a consolidated group or MEC group before

the consolidation day.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

(3)	The amendments of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ made by this Schedule apply in relation to a dividend or non-share dividend paid by a company on or after the consolidation day.
 (4)	A term used in subitem&#160;(2) and defined in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ has the same meaning in that subitem as it has in that Act.
 (5)	The amendments of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ made by this Schedule apply to a dividend or a non-share dividend that:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is paid by a company (the _paying company_) after 30&#160;June

2002; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is paid to a company that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is related (within the meaning of subsection 51AE(16) of that Act) to the

paying company; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is a member of a consolidated group or MEC group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

(6)	A term used in paragraph&#160;(5)(a) or (b) and defined in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ has the same meaning in that paragraph as it has in that Act.
 (7)	To avoid doubt, the amendments of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ made by this Schedule apply to a dividend or a non-share dividend if they apply to it under subitem&#160;(5), even if they would not apply to it under subitem&#160;(1) or (3).

20  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_foreign dividend account_ has the meaning given by

section&#160;717-505.

 </dl></dl>

21  Application of amendments of subsection 995-1(1)

The amendments of subsection 995-1(1) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ made by this Part apply on and after 1&#160;July 2002.

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;10&#151;Consolidation: offshore banking units 
**</center>

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_

1  Section&#160;121C (at the end of the definition of _OBU_)

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	In this Division, the head company of a consolidated group

or MEC group may be treated for certain purposes as an OBU at a time when a

subsidiary member of the group is an OBU (see Subdivision&#160;717-O of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_).

 </dl></dl>

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

2  At the end of Division&#160;717

Add: 

Subdivision&#160;717-O&#151;Offshore banking units

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;717-O 717-700  What this Subdivision is about
 The head company of a consolidated group is treated for certain purposes as an offshore banking unit at a time when a subsidiary member of the group is an offshore banking unit.

Table of sections

717-705	Object of this Subdivision
 717-710	Head company treated as OBU

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

717-705  Object of this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The object of this Subdivision is to ensure that certain rules in the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ relating to offshore banking units

interact properly with the consolidation regime in this Part.

 </dl></dl>

717-710  Head company treated as OBU

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Division&#160;9A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies to the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated

group as if the head company were an OBU (within the meaning of that Division)

at a time when a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of the group is an OBU (within

the meaning of that Division).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) operates for the head company core purposes mentioned in subsection 701-1(2)_._ </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;11&#151;Consolidation: application of rules to MEC groups 
**</center>

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

1  Before Subdivision&#160;719-B

Insert: 

Subdivision&#160;719-A&#151;Modified application of Part&#160;3-90 to

MEC groups

719-2  Modified application of Part&#160;3-90 to MEC groups

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Part (other than Division&#160;703 and this Division) has effect in

relation to a <sup>*</sup>MEC group in the same way in which it has effect in

relation to a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	A provision in this Part (other than in Division&#160;703

or in this Division) mentioning 2 separate consolidated groups will, under

subsection&#160;(1), have an additional operation when the groups are both MEC

groups or when one is a MEC group and the other is a consolidated group.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, that effect is subject to the modifications set out in this

Division.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection&#160;(1), a reference in this Part (other than in Division&#160;703 or this Division) to a provision in Division&#160;703 applies as if it referred instead to that provision or the corresponding provision in Subdivision&#160;719-B (as appropriate). </dd> </dl></dl>

2  Subsection 995-1(1) (at the end of the definition of _consolidated group_)

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Part&#160;3-90 contains rules relating to the tax

treatment of consolidated groups. Division&#160;719 (of that Part) applies

those rules to MEC groups with modifications (see section&#160;719-2). Note 2:	Provisions in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ and in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ (other than in Part&#160;3-90) referring only to consolidated groups do _not_ apply to MEC groups.  </dl></dl>

3  Subsection 995-1(1) (at the end of the definition of _MEC group_)

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Part&#160;3-90 contains rules relating to the tax

treatment of consolidated groups. Division&#160;719 (of that Part) applies

those rules to MEC groups with modifications (see section&#160;719-2). Note 2:	Provisions in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ and in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ (other than in Part&#160;3-90) referring only to consolidated groups do _not_ apply to MEC groups.  </dl></dl>

_Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_

4  Before Subdivision&#160;719-C

Insert: 

Subdivision&#160;719-A&#151;Modified application of Part&#160;3-90 to

MEC groups

719-2  Modified application of Part&#160;3-90 to MEC groups

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Part (other than Division&#160;703 and this Division) has effect in

relation to a MEC group in the same way in which it has effect in relation to a

consolidated group.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, that effect is subject to the modifications set out in this Division. </dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;719-B&#151;MEC groups and their members

719-5  Debt interests that are not membership interests

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;703-30 of this Act has effect in relation to a MEC group in the

same way in which it has effect in relation to a consolidated group.

 </dl></dl>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;12&#151;Consolidation: MEC group cost setting rules 
**</center>

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

1  Section&#160;719-155

Repeal the section, substitute: 

719-155  Object of this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The object of this Subdivision is to modify the tax cost setting rules in

Divisions&#160;701 and 705 so that they take account of the special

characteristics of <sup>*</sup>MEC groups.

 </dl></dl>

2  Before subsection 719-160(1)

Insert:

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1A)</dt><dd>This section applies if an entity (the _MEC joining entity_)

becomes a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at a time

(the _MEC joining time_).

</dd> </dl></dl>

3  Section&#160;719-165

Repeal the section, substitute: 

719-165  Trading stock value not set for assets of eligible tier-1 companies

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if an entity (the _MEC joining entity_)

becomes a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at a time

(the _MEC joining time_).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection 701-35(4) (setting value of trading stock at tax-neutral amount) does not apply to the assets of the MEC joining entity if it is an <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 company at the MEC joining time. </dd> </dl></dl>

4  At the end of Subdivision&#160;719-C

Add: 

719-170  Modified effect of subsections 705-175(1) and 705-185(1)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if all of the <sup>*</sup>members of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group (the _acquired group_) become members of

another MEC group, or of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group, at a particular time

(the _acquisition time_) as a result of the <sup>*</sup>acquisition

of <sup>*</sup>membership interests in:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>head company of the acquired group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>other entities that were <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 companies of the

acquired group just before the acquisition time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsections 705-175(1) and 705-185(1) have effect as if a

<sup>*</sup>membership interest in an entity mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b)

of this section were a membership interest in the <sup>*</sup>head company of

the acquired group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	If the _acquiring_ group is a MEC group, and the

head company of the acquired group becomes an eligible tier-1 company of the

_acquiring_ group, the assets of the members of the acquired group do

_not_ have their tax cost reset at the acquisition time. This is because:

 </dl></dl>

(a)	section&#160;719-160 treats an entity becoming an eligible tier-1 company of the _acquiring_ group as if it were a part of the head company of that group; and
 (b)	section&#160;705-185 treats the subsidiary members of the acquired group as part of the head company of the acquired group.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 2:	If:

 </dl></dl>

(a)	the _acquiring_ group is a MEC group, but the head company of the acquired group does _not_ become an eligible tier-1 company of the _acquiring_ group; or
 (b)	the _acquiring_ group is a consolidated group and the acquired group is a MEC group;

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

	the assets of the members of the acquired group have their tax

cost reset at the acquisition time (section&#160;719-160 does not preclude tax

cost resetting in these cases). For the purposes of resetting the tax cost of

those assets, section&#160;705-185 treats the subsidiary members of the

acquired group as part of the head company of the acquired group.

 </dl></dl>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;13&#151;Consolidation: MEC groups and losses  
**</center>

Part&#160;1&#151;Basic amendments

1  Before section&#160;719-300

<center>Back to Top</center>

Insert: 

Guide to Subdivision&#160;719-F

719-250  What this Subdivision is about

This Subdivision modifies the rules about transferring and utilising losses so the rules operate appropriately in relation to MEC groups, taking account of the special characteristics of those groups. The modifications mainly affect:

	(a)	rules about maintaining the same ownership to be able to utilise a loss; and
 	(b)	rules for working out how much of a loss can be utilised by reference to bundles of losses and their available fractions.

Table of sections

Maintaining the same ownership to be able to utilise loss

719-255	Special rules
 719-260	Special test for utilising a loss because a company maintains the same owners
 719-265	What is the test company?
 719-270	Assumptions about the test company having made the loss for an income year
 719-275	Assumptions about nothing happening to affect direct and indirect ownership of the test company
 719-280	Assumptions about the test company failing to meet the conditions in section&#160;165-12

Same business test and change of head company

719-285	Same business test and change of head company

Bundles of losses and their available fractions

719-300	Application
 719-305	Subdivision&#160;707-C affects utilisation of losses made by ongoing head company while it was head company
 719-310	Adjustment of available fractions for bundles of losses previously transferred to ongoing head company
 719-315	Further adjustment of available fractions for all bundles
 719-320	Limit on utilising losses other than the prior group losses
 719-325	Cancellation of all losses in a bundle

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Maintaining the same ownership to be able to utilise loss

719-255  Special rules

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section and section&#160;719-260 have effect for the purposes of

working out whether a loss can be <sup>*</sup>utilised for an income year (the

_claim year_) by a company (the _focal company_) that

made the loss if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;165-12 is relevant to the question whether the focal company

can utilise the loss; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the focal company is the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group at any time in its <sup>*</sup>ownership test period for the loss (as

affected by section&#160;707-205, if relevant).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the focal company made the loss because of a transfer

under Subdivision&#160;707-A, section&#160;707-205 has the effect that the

ownership test period starts for the focal company at the time of the transfer.

 </dl></dl>

_Section 707-210 does not have effect_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Section&#160;707-210 does not have effect for the purposes of working out

whether the focal company can <sup>*</sup>utilise the loss for the claim year.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;707-210 is about whether a company can utilise

a loss it made because the loss was transferred to it under

Subdivision&#160;707-A because the transferor met the conditions in

section&#160;165-12.

 </dl></dl>

719-260  Special test for utilising a loss because a company maintains the same owners

_Meeting the conditions in section 165-12_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The focal company is taken to meet the conditions in section&#160;165-12

for the claim year and the loss if and only if the company (the _test company_) identified in relation to the focal company in accordance with

section&#160;719-265 would have met those conditions for that year on the

relevant assumptions in:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;719-270 (which is about assuming the test company made the

loss for a particular income year); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;719-275 (which is about assuming that nothing happened in

relation to certain things that would affect whether the test company would

meet those conditions); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>section&#160;719-280 (which is about assuming that the test company would

have failed to meet those conditions in certain circumstances).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Focal company&apos;s failure to meet conditions in section 165-12_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The focal company is taken to fail to meet a condition in

section&#160;165-12 only at:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first time the test company would have failed to meet the condition on

the relevant assumptions mentioned in subsection&#160;(1); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>test time described in subsection 166-5(5) for the test

company, if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>Division&#160;166 is relevant to working out whether the test company

could have <sup>*</sup>utilised the loss for the claim year on the relevant

assumptions mentioned in paragraphs&#160;(1)(a) and (b); and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the test company is not assumed under section&#160;719-280 to fail to

meet the condition before the test time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the focal company is taken to fail to meet a condition

in section&#160;165-12, the focal company will not be able to utilise the loss

for the claim year unless the focal company meets the conditions in

section&#160;165-13 by satisfying the same business test. That test applies to

the focal company (and not the test company).

 </dl></dl>

_Same business test for focal company under Division 166_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If subsection 166-5(4) affects whether the focal company can

<sup>*</sup>utilise the loss for the claim year because the focal company is a

<sup>*</sup>listed public company or a <sup>*</sup>100% subsidiary of one for

the year, subsection 166-5(5) operates as if it required the <sup>*</sup>same

business test to be applied to the <sup>*</sup>business the focal company

carried on just before the time described in subsection&#160;(2) of this

section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Same business test for focal company to transfer loss_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If subsection 707-125(4) is relevant to working out whether the focal

company can transfer the loss to a company under Subdivision&#160;707-A, that

subsection:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>has effect as if subsection 707-125(5) described the focal company's

income year containing the time at which the focal company is taken under

subsection&#160;(2) of this section to fail to meet a condition in

section&#160;165-12; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>has effect despite subsection&#160;(3) of this section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For working out whether certain losses can be transferred

under Subdivision&#160;707-A, subsection 707-125(4) modifies the operation of

subsection 166-5(5) by extending the same business test period to include the

income year described in subsection 707-125(5).

 </dl></dl>

719-265  What is the test company?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>To identify for the purposes of section&#160;719-260 the company that is

the test company for the focal company for the loss:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>first, identify the test company for the focal company by applying

whichever one of subsections&#160;(2), (3), (4) and (6) is relevant; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>then, if the condition in column 1 of an item of the table is met, apply

this section again to identify the test company as if the company described in

column 2 of the item were the focal company, taking account only of things that

happened before the event described in column 3 of the item.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Change of head company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If, under section&#160;719-90, the focal company is taken to have made the

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>was the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at any time

during the income year for which it made the loss; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>became the head company of a MEC group after that income year (without

having been a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of the group before becoming the

head company); and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the focal company was later the head company of the MEC group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the test company for the focal company is the company that is the test company for the first head company.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;719-90 applies if there is a change in the

head company of a MEC group, treating the later head company as if what had

happened to the earlier head company had happened to the later head company.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>Subsections&#160;(2), (3) and (4) and section&#160;719-90 have effect

subject to subsection&#160;(6) of this section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the time the loss is transferred to the company under that Subdivision,

if the company makes the loss because of that transfer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for an income year starting after the transfer, another company was the

head company of the group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

719-280  Assumptions about the test company failing to meet the conditions in section&#160;165-12

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Assume that the test company fails to meet the conditions in

section&#160;165-12 at the time an event described in subsection&#160;(2), (3)

or (4) happens after the start of the <sup>*</sup>ownership test period for the

focal company in relation to:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>MEC group whose <sup>*</sup>head company was the focal

company; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>potential MEC group whose membership was the same as the

membership of that MEC group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the test company is assumed to fail to meet the

conditions in section&#160;165-12 for the claim year and the loss, the focal

company is taken (under section&#160;719-260) to have failed to meet those

conditions.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>One event is the <sup>*</sup>potential MEC group ceasing to exist.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Another event is something happening that meets these conditions: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the thing happens at a time in relation to <sup>*</sup>membership

interests in one or more of these entities:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a company that was just before that time a <sup>*</sup>member of the

<sup>*</sup>MEC group and an <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 company of the

<sup>*</sup>top company for the MEC group;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an entity interposed between a company described in subparagraph&#160;(i)

and the company that was the top company for the group just before that time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the thing does not cause the <sup>*</sup>potential MEC group to cease to

exist but does cause a change in the identity of the top company for the

potential MEC group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Another event is the <sup>*</sup>MEC group ceasing to exist because there

ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>provisional head company of the group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Other causes of failure to meet conditions in section 165-12_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, this section does not limit the circumstances in which the

test company would have failed to meet the conditions in section&#160;165-12 on

the relevant assumptions set out in sections&#160;719-270 and 719-275.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Same business test and change of head company

719-285  Same business test and change of head company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In working out whether the <sup>*</sup>same business test is satisfied by a

company that, after the <sup>*</sup>test time, became the <sup>*</sup>head

company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group that existed before that time, disregard

what happened in relation to the company before it became a <sup>*</sup>member

of the group. Section&#160;719-90 has effect subject to this section.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The same business test is to be applied on the basis that

the company's business at the test time was the business that

section&#160;719-90 treats the company as having carried on at that time,

except to the extent that section&#160;719-90 attributes to the company its

actual history before it became a member of the MEC group. Note 2:	Section&#160;719-90 applies if there is a change in the head company of a MEC group, treating the later head company as if what had happened to the earlier head company had happened to the later head company.  </dl></dl>

year a loss it made because of a <sup>*</sup>COT transfer from a company (the

_latest transferor_).</dd> <dt>(1A)</dt><dd>A transfer of a loss under Subdivision&#160;707-A from a company to a company is a _COT transfer_ of the loss if the transfer occurs because: </dd> </dl></dl>

not exist in relation to the transferor.

</dd>

1  At the end of Subdivision&#160;709-A

Add: 

Payment of group liability by former subsidiary member

709-95  Payment of group liability by former subsidiary member

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an entity (the _former subsidiary_) ceases to be a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group (the

_old group_) at a particular time (the _leaving time_);

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at or after the leaving time, the former subsidiary:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>pays a PAYG instalment for which it was jointly and severally

liable under subsection 721-15(1) because it was a subsidiary member of the old

group; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>pays income tax for which it was jointly and severally liable

under that subsection because it was a subsidiary member of the old group; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>apart from this section, a <sup>*</sup>franking credit would arise under

section&#160;205-15 in the <sup>*</sup>franking account of the former

subsidiary at a time (the _crediting time_) because of that payment.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The credit:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>does not arise at the crediting time in the <sup>*</sup>franking account

of the former subsidiary; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>instead, arises at the crediting time in the franking account of the

entity that was the <sup>*</sup>head company of the old group at the leaving

time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

709-100  Refund of income tax to former subsidiary member

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an entity (the _former subsidiary_) ceases to be a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group (the

_old group_) at a particular time (the _leaving time_);

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at or after the leaving time, the former subsidiary <sup>*</sup>receives a

refund of income tax for which it was jointly and severally liable under

subsection 721-15(1) because it was a subsidiary member of the old group; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>apart from this section, a <sup>*</sup>franking debit would arise under

section&#160;205-30 in the <sup>*</sup>franking account of the former

subsidiary at a time (the _debiting time_) because of that payment.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The debit:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>does not arise at the debiting time in the <sup>*</sup>franking account of

the former subsidiary; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>instead, arises at the debiting time in the franking account of the entity

that was the <sup>*</sup>head company of the old group at the leaving time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

4  After section&#160;721-15

Insert: 

721-17  Notice of joint and several liability for general interest charge

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the group liability is <sup>*</sup>general interest charge for a day in

relation to another liability (the _primary liability_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Commissioner gives a particular contributing member written notice

under subsection 721-15(5) of the group liability; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>general interest charge arises for a subsequent day in relation to the

primary liability; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the general interest charge for the subsequent day has not been paid or

otherwise discharged in full by the time it became due and payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commissioner is taken to have given the contributing member written

notice under subsection 721-15(5) of the <sup>*</sup>general interest charge

for the subsequent day. The notice is taken to have been given on that day.

</dd> </dl></dl>

5  After subsection 721-30(5)

Insert:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5A)</dt><dd>Despite subsection&#160;(5), if the group liability is

<sup>*</sup>general interest charge for a day, the liability of a TSA

contributing member under subsection&#160;(2) becomes due and payable by the

member at the end of the day on which the Commissioner gives the member written

notice of the liability under subsection&#160;(5).

</dd> </dl></dl>

721-32  Notice of general interest charge liability under TSA

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section operates if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the group liability is <sup>*</sup>general interest charge for a day in

relation to another liability (the _primary liability_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Commissioner gives a particular TSA contributing member written notice

under subsection 721-30(5) of its liability under subsection 721-30(2) in

relation to the general interest charge for that day; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>general interest charge arises for a subsequent day in relation to the

primary liability; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the TSA contributing member is liable under subsection 721-30(2) for an

amount in relation to the general interest charge for the subsequent day.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commissioner is taken to have given the TSA contributing member

written notice under subsection 721-30(5) of the amount in relation to the

<sup>*</sup>general interest charge for the subsequent day. The notice is taken

to have been given on that day.

</dd> </dl></dl>

7  After section&#160;721-35

Insert: 

721-40  TSA liability and group liability are linked

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The liability of a TSA contributing member under subsection 721-30(2) (the

_TSA liability_) is separate and distinct for all purposes from the

group liability to which it relates (the _linked group liability_).

For example, the Commissioner may take proceedings to recover the unpaid amount

of the TSA liability, proceedings to recover the unpaid amount of the linked

group liability, or both.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The TSA contributing member will not be jointly and

severally liable for the linked group liability under section&#160;721-15 (see

subsection 721-15(3)). However, the head company of the group remains liable

for the linked group liability.

 </dl></dl>

_Payment or discharge of TSA liability_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an amount is paid or applied at a particular time towards discharging

the TSA liability, the linked group liability is discharged at that time to the

extent of the same amount.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Payment or discharge of linked group liability_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an amount is paid or applied at a particular time towards discharging the

linked group liability; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>as a result, the amount unpaid on the TSA liability at that time (apart

from this section) exceeds the amount unpaid on the linked group liability at

that time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the TSA liability is discharged at that time to the extent of the excess.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Subsections&#160;(2) and (3) operate in relation to a liability under a

judgment (the _judgment liability_):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the judgment liability is for the entire amount unpaid on the TSA

liability&#151;as if the judgment liability were the TSA liability; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the judgment liability is for the entire amount unpaid on the linked

group liability&#151;as if the judgment liability were the linked group liability.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>This section does not discharge a liability to a greater extent than the

amount of the liability.

</dd> </dl></dl>

703-45  Subsidiary members or nominees interposed between the head company and a subsidiary member of a consolidated group or a consolidatable group

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group or a <sup>*</sup>consolidatable group at a

Insert: 

Division&#160;701C&#151;Modified application etc. of provisions of

<center>Back to Top</center>

Income Tax Assessment Act 1997: transitional foreign-held membership

structures

Table of Subdivisions

701C-A	Overview
 701C-B	Membership rules allowing foreign holding
 701C-C	Modifications of tax cost setting rules 

Subdivision&#160;701C-A&#151;Overview

Table of sections

701C-1	Overview 

701C-1  Overview

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This Division:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>sets out, for the purposes of item&#160;2, column 4 of the table in

subsection 703-15(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, rules that

allow certain entities to be subsidiary members of consolidatable groups or

consolidated groups where other entities are interposed between them and the

head company of the group (see Subdivision&#160;701C-B); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>modifies certain rules in Part&#160;3-90 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ relating to setting the tax cost of assets to take account of

those membership rules (see Subdivision&#160;701C-C).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_\[The next section is 701C-10.]_

Subdivision&#160;701C-B&#151;Membership rules allowing foreign

holding

Table of sections

701C-10	Additional membership rules where entities are interposed between the head company and a subsidiary member&#151;case where an interposed entity is a non-resident and the subsidiary member is a company
 701C-15	Additional membership rules where entities are interposed between the head company and a subsidiary member&#151;case where an interposed entity is a non-resident and the subsidiary member is a trust or partnership
 701C-20	Transitional foreign-held subsidiaries and transitional foreign-held indirect subsidiaries 

701C-10  Additional membership rules where entities are interposed between the head company and a subsidiary member&#151;case where an interposed entity is a non-resident and the subsidiary member is a company
<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section describes, for the purposes of item&#160;2, column 4 of the

table in subsection 703-15(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, a

set of requirements that must be met for an entity (the _test entity_) to be a subsidiary member of a consolidated group or a

consolidatable group at a particular time (the _test time_).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Test entity must be company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>At the test time, the test entity must be a company.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_At least one interposed entity must be a non-resident company or non-resident trust_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>At the test time, at least one of the interposed entities must be:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a company (a _non-resident company_) that is a foreign

resident; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a trust (a _non-resident trust_) that does not meet the

requirements in any item of the table in section&#160;703-25 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_The interposed entities must all be of a particular kind_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>At the test time, each of the interposed entities must be:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a subsidiary member of the group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a non-resident company; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a non-resident trust; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an entity that holds membership interests in an entity interposed between

it and the test entity, or in the test entity, only as a nominee of one or more

entities each of which is a member of the group, a non-resident company or a

non-resident trust; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a partnership, each of the partners in which is a non-resident company or

a non-resident trust.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Test entity must be a subsidiary member on assumption that non-resident companies and non-resident trusts were subsidiary members_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>At the test time, it must be the case that the test entity would be a

subsidiary member of the group if each interposed entity that is a non-resident

company or non-resident trust were a subsidiary member of the group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Additional requirement for consolidatable groups_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the group is a consolidatable group, the test time must be before

1&#160;July 2004.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Additional requirement for consolidated groups at formation_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>If the group is a consolidated group and the test time is the time at

which the group comes into existence as a consolidated group, the test time

must be before 1&#160;July 2004.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Additional requirement for consolidated groups after formation_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the group is a consolidated group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the test time is after the group comes into existence; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>at the test time, one or more of the membership interests in the test

entity are held by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a non-resident company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a non-resident trust; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>an entity that holds the membership interests only as a nominee of one

or more entities each of which is a non-resident company or a non-resident

trust; or</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>a partnership, each of the partners in which is a non-resident company or

a non-resident trust;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

then:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>from the time the group came into existence as a consolidated group until

the test time, the test entity must have been a subsidiary member of the group;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>at the time the group came into existence as a consolidated group, one or

more of the membership interests in the test entity must have been held by an

entity of a kind mentioned in subparagraph&#160;(c)(i), (ii), (iii) or (iv).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

701C-15  Additional membership rules where entities are interposed between the head company and a subsidiary member&#151;case where an interposed entity is a non-resident and the subsidiary member is a trust or partnership

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section describes, for the purposes of item&#160;2, column 4 of the

table in subsection 703-15(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, a

set of requirements that must be met for an entity (the _test entity_) to be a subsidiary member of a consolidated group or a

consolidatable group at a particular time (the _test time_).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Test entity must be a trust or partnership_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>At the test time, the test entity must be a trust or partnership.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_At least one interposed entity must be a company that is a subsidiary member because of section 701C-10_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>At the test time, one or more of the interposed entities must be companies

that are subsidiary members of the group because the set of requirements in

section&#160;701C-10 are met.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Test entity must be a subsidiary member on assumption that head company beneficially owned all membership interests beneficially owned by subsection (3) companies_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>At the test time, it must be the case that the test entity would be a

subsidiary member of the group if the head company beneficially owned all the

membership interests beneficially owned by each company described in

subsection&#160;(3).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

701C-20  Transitional foreign-held subsidiaries and transitional foreign-held indirect subsidiaries

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an entity is a subsidiary member of a consolidated group in a case where

the set of requirements described in section&#160;701C-10 are met; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>one or more of the membership interests in the entity are held by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a non-resident company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a non-resident trust; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>an entity that holds the membership interests only as a nominee of one

or more entities each of which is a non-resident company or a non-resident

trust; or</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>a partnership, each of the partners in which is a non-resident company or

a non-resident trust;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

then:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity is a _transitional foreign-held subsidiary_ of the

group; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the transitional foreign-held subsidiary; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an entity that is a transitional foreign-held indirect subsidiary of the

group because of another application of this paragraph;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		holds one or more membership interests in another entity that:

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>is a subsidiary member of the group; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>is not a transitional foreign-held subsidiary of the group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		that other member is a _transitional foreign-held indirect subsidiary_ of the group.

</dl></dl></dl>

Note:	In order to be a subsidiary member of the group as required by subparagraph&#160;(d)(iii), the transitional foreign-held indirect subsidiary would need to have satisfied the set of requirements in either section&#160;701C-10 or 701C-15 

Subdivision&#160;701C-C&#151;Modifications of tax cost setting

rules

Table of sections

Application and object

701C-25	Application and object of this Subdivision

Basic modification

701C-30	Transitional foreign-held subsidiary to be treated as part of head company

Other modifications

701C-35	Trading stock value not set for assets of transitional foreign-held subsidiaries
 701C-40	Cost setting rules for exit cases&#151;modification of core rules
 701C-50	Cost setting rules for exit cases&#151;reference to modification of core rule 

Application and object

701C-25  Application and object of this Subdivision

_Application_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Subdivision applies if an entity (the _transitional foreign-held joining entity_) that is a transitional foreign-held subsidiary or a

transitional foreign-held indirect subsidiary becomes a subsidiary member of a

consolidated group at the time (the _formation time_) the group

comes into existence.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Object_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The object of this Subdivision is to ensure that, on becoming a subsidiary

member at the formation time, the tax cost of the assets of any transitional

foreign-held subsidiary is not set and that the tax cost setting amount for

assets of any transitional foreign-held indirect subsidiary that becomes a

subsidiary member at that time takes account of this.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Basic modification

701C-30  Transitional foreign-held subsidiary to be treated as part of head company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The following provisions:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;701-10 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_(about

setting the tax cost of assets that an entity brings into the group);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;705-A of that Act, in its application in accordance with

Subdivision&#160;705-B of that Act;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

apply, for the purposes of setting the tax cost of an asset of the transitional foreign-held entity at the formation time, as if each subsidiary member of the group that is a transitional foreign-held subsidiary at the formation time were a part of the head company of the group, rather than a separate entity.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	This section means that references in those provisions to

matters internal to the group operate as if transitional foreign-held

subsidiaries in the group were parts of the head company of the group. For

example:

 </dl></dl>

(a)	provisions operating if the head company holds (whether directly or indirectly) membership interests in another entity operate even if a transitional foreign-held subsidiary actually holds those interests; and
 (b)	provisions operating if the head company owns or controls another entity operate even if one or more transitional foreign-held subsidiaries actually own or control that other entity; and
 (c)	provisions operating if an entity is interposed between the head company and another entity operate even if the first entity is actually interposed between a transitional foreign-held subsidiary and the other entity.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 2:	If the transitional foreign-held entity is a transitional

foreign-held subsidiary, this section means the assets of the entity do not

have their tax cost reset at the formation time. This is because

Subdivision&#160;705-A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, in its

application in accordance with Subdivision&#160;705-B of that Act, resets the

tax cost of assets of _subsidiary_ members of a group, but not assets of

the head company.

 </dl></dl>

Other modifications

701C-35  Trading stock value not set for assets of transitional foreign-held subsidiaries

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Subsection 701-35(4) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_(setting

value of trading stock at tax-neutral amount) does not apply to the assets of

the transitional foreign-held entity if it is a transitional foreign-held

subsidiary.

 </dl></dl>

701C-40  Cost setting rules for exit cases&#151;modification of core rules

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;701-15 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ applies as

if the following subsection were added at the end of the section:

 </dl></dl>

_Application to transitional foreign-held subsidiaries_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If an entity that ceases to be a subsidiary member is a transitional

foreign-held subsidiary when it does so:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>this section applies to each membership interest in the transitional

foreign-held subsidiary that is held by an entity (an _eligible non-resident_) of a kind mentioned in subparagraph 701C-20(b)(i), (ii),

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>or (iv) of the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_ in

the same way as it applies to a membership interest in the transitional

foreign-held subsidiary that is held by the head company; and</dd></dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for that purpose, the definition of _head company core purposes_ in subsection 701-1(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ applies to the eligible non-resident in the same way as it applies to

the head company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

701C-50  Cost setting rules for exit cases&#151;reference to modification of core rule

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;711-5 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ applies as if

the following note were added at the end of the section:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the leaving entity is a transitional foreign-held

subsidiary (within the meaning of section&#160;701C-20 of the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997)_, this Division will, in accordance with

subsection 701-15(4) of this Act (see section&#160;701C-40 of the

first-mentioned Act), apply to membership interests that an eligible

non-resident mentioned in that subsection holds in the entity in the same way

as it applies to membership interests that the head company holds in the entity.

 </dl></dl>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;17&#151;Consolidation: transitional cost setting rule relating to roll-overs 
**</center>

_Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_

1  Section&#160;701-35

Omit "Part&#160;3-90 of the _Income Tax Assessment 1997_ applies", substitute "the provisions mentioned in subsection&#160;(2) apply".

2  At the end of section&#160;701-35

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The provisions are:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>Division&#160;705 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>provisions  of this Act modifying the effect of that Division.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(1) does not apply if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the asset mentioned in subsection&#160;(1) is a membership interest in an

entity (the _test entity_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>when the CGT event happened:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the originating company in relation to the roll-over, or the transferor in

relation to the roll-over relief, was a foreign resident; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the recipient company, or the transferee in relation to the roll-over

relief, was an Australian resident; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>when the transitional group came into existence, the test entity was a

subsidiary member of the group, other than as a transitional foreign-held

subsidiary of the group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

3  After section&#160;719-160

Insert: 

719-163  Modified effect of section&#160;701-35

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies if the transitional group mentioned in

section&#160;701-35 of this Act is a MEC group.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>That section has effect as if paragraph 701-35(3)(c) were repealed and the following paragraph were substituted: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>when the transitional group came into existence, the test entity was a

subsidiary member of the group, other than as:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a transitional foreign-held subsidiary of the group (see

section&#160;701C-20); or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an eligible tier-1 company of the group.

</dd>
