###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;18&#151;Consolidation: extra transitional provision for foreign tax credits 
**</center>

_New Business Tax System (Consolidation, Value Shifting, Demergers and Other Measures) Act 2002_

1  At the end of Schedule&#160;10

Add:

11  Transitional provision for section&#160;160AF

(1)	This item applies if:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>because of item&#160;5, 6 or 7, old section&#160;160AFE applies to a

taxpayer as if a period were an income year (the _notional income year_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the taxpayer has an initial excess credit (within the meaning of old

section&#160;160AFE) in relation to the notional income year; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the taxpayer transfers all or part (the extent of the transfer being the

_transfer amount_) of that initial excess credit under old

section&#160;160AFE for utilisation by another company in the notional income

year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

(2)	Section&#160;160AF of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies to the taxpayer for the year of income in which the notional income year ends as if the amount of foreign tax paid by the taxpayer mentioned in paragraph 160AF(1)(b) of that Act were reduced by the transfer amount.
 (3)	This item operates separately in relation to each class of foreign income identified in subsection 160AF(7) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_, as if the taxpayer's foreign income of that class for a year of income were the whole of the taxpayer's foreign income for that year.

4  After section&#160;707-325

Insert: 

707-326  Events involving only value donor and real loss-maker not covered by rule against inflation of modified market value

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section affects the calculation of the modified market value of the

real loss-maker mentioned in subsection 707-315(1) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ for a bundle of losses. This section affects the

calculation:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>only if section&#160;707-325 of this Act applies for the purposes of

working out the available fraction for the bundle; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>only for the purposes of working out the available fraction for the bundle

to affect the utilisation of tax losses, film losses and net capital losses in

the bundle (and not any overall foreign losses, as defined in

section&#160;160AFD of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_, in the

bundle).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This section does not affect the calculation of the real

loss-maker's modified market value for other purposes (such as the real

loss-maker being a value donor for the purposes of another application of

section&#160;707-325 of this Act).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Disregard for the purposes of subsection 707-325(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ an event:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that is described in subsection 707-325(4) of that Act; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that meets the condition in subsection&#160;(3) or (4) of this section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>One condition is that the event was an injection of capital directly into

the real loss-maker by the value donor mentioned in section&#160;707-325 of

this Act.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The other condition is that the event was a transaction: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that did not take place at arm's length; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that involved only the real loss-maker and the value donor mentioned in

section&#160;707-325 of this Act; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that would have caused subsection 707-325(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ to operate in working out the real loss-maker's

modified market value (even if no other events described in subsection

707-325(4) of that Act had occurred), apart from this section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(2) of this section does not apply if subsection

707-325(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>operates for the purposes of working out the value donor's modified market

value because of an event that involved an entity other than the value donor

and the real loss-maker (whether or not the event also involved either the

value donor or the real loss-maker); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>would operate for those purposes because of such an event apart from

another application of this section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

5  After section&#160;707-328

Insert: 
<center>Back to Top</center>

707-328A  Some events involving only group members not covered by rule against inflation of modified market value

_Overview_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(3) of this section affects the calculation, under

section&#160;707-325 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ and

section&#160;707-325 of this Act, of the modified market value of the real

loss-maker mentioned in subsection 707-315(1) of that Act for a bundle of

losses, but only if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the requirement in subsection&#160;(2) of this section is met in relation

to each other company that became a member of the group mentioned in subsection

707-315(1) of that Act in connection with the bundle at the time (the

_formation time_) the group became a consolidated group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the provisions described in subsection 707-327(4) of this Act operate

(because of that subsection) in relation to each loss of such a company that is

covered by paragraphs 707-327(1)(b) and (c) of this Act as if the bundle

included the loss; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>all members of the group at the formation time were companies; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>subsection 707-325(2) of that Act does not operate, for the purposes of

working out the modified market value of an entity that became a member of the

group at the formation time, because of an event that involved an entity that

did not become a member of the group then; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the transferee mentioned in subsection 707-325(1) of this Act chooses that

this section apply in relation to the real loss-maker.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Section&#160;707-325 of this Act must apply in relation to the other

company (as value donor) so that the available fraction for the bundle is to be

worked out as if there were added to the real loss-maker's modified market

value an amount worked out by reference to the other company's modified market

value at the initial transfer time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Disregarding events for purposes of anti-inflation rule_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Disregard for the purposes of subsection 707-325(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ an event that is described in subsection 707-325(4) of

that Act and was either:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an injection of capital into an entity that became a member of the group

at the formation time by another such entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a transaction that involved only entities that became members of the group

at the formation time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Disregarding such an event could have a direct or indirect

effect on the real loss-maker's modified market value for the purposes of

working out the available fraction for the bundle in one of these ways:

 </dl></dl>

(a)	it could directly affect the real loss-maker's modified market value calculated under section&#160;707-325 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, if the real loss-maker was involved in the event;
 (b)	it could have an indirect effect by affecting the value donor's modified market value calculated under that section and used under section&#160;707-325 of this Act to add an amount to the real loss-maker's modified market value for those purposes.

_Choice_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A choice for the purposes of paragraph&#160;(1)(e):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>may be made only by the day on which the transferee lodges its income tax

return for the first income year for which it utilises (except in accordance

with section&#160;707-350) losses transferred to it under

Subdivision&#160;707-A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>cannot be amended or revoked.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Scope of this section_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>This section affects the modified market value of an entity that became a

member of the group at the formation time only for the purposes of calculating

the real loss-maker's modified market value for the purposes of working out the

available fraction for the bundle.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>This section has effect for working out the available fraction of the bundle only so far as it affects the utilisation of a tax loss, film loss or net capital loss. It does not affect the utilisation of an overall foreign loss (as defined in section&#160;160AFD of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_) that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is included in the bundle; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>was transferred under Subdivision&#160;707-A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ from an entity other than the real loss-maker.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the bundle includes an overall foreign loss and a loss

of another sort:

 </dl></dl>

(a)	utilisation of the overall foreign loss is limited by the available fraction for the bundle worked out apart from this section; and
 (b)	utilisation of the loss of the other sort is limited by the available fraction for the bundle as affected by this section, if applicable.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>This section can operate in relation to only one bundle of losses

transferred to the transferee under Subdivision&#160;707-A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997._

</dd> </dl></dl>

section&#160;73BF of this Act or section&#160;40-292 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>In working out the amount of a balancing adjustment under section&#160;73BF of this Act or section&#160;40-292 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ for the asset, the asset's adjustable value (see section&#160;40-85 of that Act) is reduced by so much of a reduction amount (see section&#160;73BAF of this Act) for the asset that has not been applied in reducing a notional Division&#160;40 deduction for the head company. </dd> </dl></dl>

5  Section&#160;45-705 in Schedule&#160;1

45-705  Application of Subdivision to head company

_Period during which Subdivision applies to head company_

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subject to sections&#160;45-880 and 45-885, this Subdivision applies to a

during the period:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>starting at the start of the <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter of the company

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ending:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>at the end of the instalment quarter of the company determined under

paragraph&#160;(5)(a) or (b); or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>just before the instalment quarter of the company determined under

paragraph&#160;(5)(c) or (d).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_When the period beginsinitial head company instalment rate_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This Subdivision starts to apply to a company as the <sup>*</sup>head

company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group at the start of an

<sup>*</sup>instalment quarter under this subsection if, during that quarter,

the Commissioner gives the company (as that head company) the

<sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment rate.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The operation of this subsection may be affected by

section&#160;45-885.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>This Subdivision starts to apply to a company as the <sup>*</sup>head

<sup>*</sup>instalment quarter (the _starting quarter_) under this

subsection if all of the following conditions are satisfied:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the consolidated group is <sup>*</sup>created from a <sup>*</sup>MEC group

during the starting quarter;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>either of the following applies:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>this Subdivision applied, in accordance with Subdivision&#160;45-S, to the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of the MEC group at the end of the

previous instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the Commissioner gives the <sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment

rate to the provisional head company of the MEC group during the starting

quarter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For the application of this Subdivision to a provisional

head company of a MEC group: see section&#160;45-915.

 </dl></dl>

_When the period beginsnew head company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>This Subdivision starts to apply to a company as the <sup>*</sup>head

company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group at the start of an

<sup>*</sup>instalment quarter (the _starting quarter_) under this

subsection if all of the following conditions are satisfied:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company is an interposed company mentioned in subsection 124-380(5) of

the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company chooses under that subsection that the consolidated group is

to continue in existence at and after the completion time mentioned in that

subsection;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the completion time occurs during the starting quarter;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>one of the following subparagraphs applies:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>this Subdivision applied to the original company mentioned in that

subsection&#160;(as the head company of the consolidated group) at the end of

the previous instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the Commissioner gives the <sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment

rate to the original company mentioned in that subsection&#160;(as the head

company of the consolidated group) during the starting quarter;</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the consolidated group is <sup>*</sup>created from a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group during the starting quarter and this Subdivision applied to the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of the MEC group at the end of the

previous instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>the consolidated group is created from a MEC group during the starting

quarter and the Commissioner gives the initial head company instalment rate to

the provisional head company of the MEC group during the starting quarter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_When the period ends_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>This Subdivision stops applying to a company as the <sup>*</sup>head

company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group at the earliest of the following

times after the company becomes the head company:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the end of the <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter during which the

consolidated group ceases to exist (other than because a <sup>*</sup>MEC group

is <sup>*</sup>created from the consolidated group);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the end of the instalment quarter during which the Commissioner is

notified of the creation of a MEC group from the consolidated group if the MEC

group is created during that instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>just before the instalment quarter during which the Commissioner is

notified of the creation of a MEC group from the consolidated group if the MEC

group was created before that instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>just before the instalment quarter that includes the completion time

mentioned in subsection 124-380(5) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

where an interposed company mentioned in that subsection chooses under that

subsection that the consolidated group is to continue in existence.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The operation of this subsection because of

paragraph&#160;(a) may be affected by section&#160;45-880.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection&#160;(5), the Commissioner is notified of

the creation of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group from a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group

when the Commissioner receives a notice of the consolidation of the MEC group

under subsection 719-40(1) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>If this Subdivision stops applying to a company as the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group just before an <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter under paragraph&#160;(5)(c), then, for the purposes of this Part, this Act has effect for the company and other <sup>*</sup>members of the group as if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the consolidated group had continued to exist until just before the start

of that quarter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company were the head company of the group until just before the start

of that quarter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, this Subdivision does not apply to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group for any time at

all if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>subsection&#160;(2), (3) or (4), and subsection&#160;(5), would, apart

from this subsection, apply to the company; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the time at which this Subdivision would stop applying to the company

under subsection&#160;(5) is before the time at which this Subdivision would

start to apply to the company under subsection&#160;(2), (3) or (4).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, and apart from the operation of subsection&#160;(7), this

Subdivision may apply to a company as the <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group at a time when the company is not in fact the

head company of the group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	An example of this is when an interposed company becomes

the new head company of a consolidated group. Under this section and

section&#160;45-740, this Subdivision may start applying to the company as if

it had already become the head company when it is not yet such a company.

 </dl></dl>

6  Section&#160;45-720 in Schedule&#160;1 (link note)

Repeal the link note, substitute:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	You stop being an annual payer when this Subdivision starts

applying to you as the head company of a consolidated group: see

section&#160;45-160.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

7  Before section&#160;45-755 in Schedule&#160;1

Insert (after the group heading): 

45-740  Change of head company

_Object_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The object of this section (except subsection&#160;(8)) is to ensure that,

for the purposes of this Part, when a company becomes the new <sup>*</sup>head

company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company inherits the history of the former head company of the group;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the history of the new head company is effectively ignored.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section applies to a <sup>*</sup>head company of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company is an interposed company mentioned in subsection 45-705(4) (an

interposed company that chooses under subsection 124-380(5) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ that the consolidated group is to continue in

existence at and after the completion time mentioned in that subsection); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the conditions in subsection 45-705(4) are satisfied in relation to the

interposed company (whether or not this Subdivision applies to the company as

the head company of the group for any period of time).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Everything that happened before the completion time in relation to the

company (the _original company_) that was the <sup>*</sup>head

company of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group immediately before the completion

time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is taken to have happened in relation to the interposed company instead of

in relation to the original company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is taken to have happened in relation to the interposed company instead of

what would (apart from this section) be taken to have happened in relation to

the interposed company before the completion time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

just as if, at all times before the completion time:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the interposed company had been the original company; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the original company had been the interposed company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, subsection&#160;(3) also covers everything that,

immediately before the completion time, was taken to have happened in relation

to the original company because of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;701-1 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_(single

entity rule); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;701-5 of that Act (entry history rule); or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>section&#160;703-75 of that Act (effects of an interposed company becoming

the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group); or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>section&#160;719-90 of that Act (effects of a change of head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group); or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>section&#160;45-710 in this Schedule (single entity rule for the purposes

of this Part), including an application of that section under

Subdivision&#160;45-S in this Schedule; or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>this section; or</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>section&#160;45-920 in this Schedule (effects of a change of

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a MEC group for the purposes of this

Part); or</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>one or more previous applications of any of the provisions covered by

paragraphs&#160;(a) to (g).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>In addition, and without affecting subsection&#160;(3):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an assessment of the original company for an income year that ends before

the income year that includes the completion time; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an amendment of the assessment;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is taken to be something that had happened to the interposed company, whether or not the assessment or amendment is made before the completion time.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>This section has effect for the purposes of applying this Part to

<sup>*</sup>members of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group in relation to an

<sup>*</sup>instalment quarter of the interposed company that ends after the

completion time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	An assessment mentioned in subsection&#160;(5) may

therefore be taken to be the base assessment of the interposed company for the

purposes of this Part.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>Subsections&#160;(1) to (6) are to be disregarded in applying

section&#160;45-705 (about the application of this Subdivision to a company as

the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, if the Commissioner has given an initial head

company instalment rate to the original company during an earlier instalment

quarter, the rate is not, despite this section, treated as if it had been given

to the interposed company for the purposes of section&#160;45-705\. Subject to

the other provisions in that section, this Subdivision therefore starts

applying to the interposed company under subsection 45-705(4).

 </dl></dl>

_Special rule for the original company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>A provision of this Part that applies on an entity becoming a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group does not

apply to the original company when it is taken to have become such a member at

the completion time as a result of section&#160;703-70 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;45-755 (the entry rule) therefore does not

apply to the original company on the company becoming a subsidiary member of

the consolidated group.

 </dl></dl>

8  Subsection 45-760(1) in Schedule&#160;1

Repeal the subsection, substitute:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies to an entity if all of the following conditions are

satisfied:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group during an <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter of the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the group;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>this Subdivision applies to the head company of the group during that

instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity does not, at the time it ceases to be a subsidiary member of

the group, become:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a subsidiary member of another consolidated group the head company of

which is one to which this Subdivision applies at that time; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a member (other than the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company) of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group the provisional head company of which is one to which

this Subdivision applies, in accordance with Subdivision&#160;45-S, at that

time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>this Part applies to the entity under section&#160;45-10.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

9  At the end of section&#160;45-775 in Schedule&#160;1

_Additional applications of subsection (2)_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If, after exercising the power in relation to the membership change under

subsection&#160;(2) for the first time, and on the basis of an assessment

(including an amendment) of the <sup>*</sup>head company for the income year in

which the change occurs, or for an earlier year, the Commissioner has worked

out:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>another instalment rate under section&#160;45-320 for the company (whether

or not the Commissioner has given that rate to the company); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>another amount of <sup>*</sup>GDP-adjusted notional tax under

section&#160;45-405 for the company (whether or not the Commissioner has

notified the company an amount of instalment based on that other amount);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner may again exercise the power under subsection&#160;(2) in relation to the membership change, as if:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the rate mentioned in paragraph&#160;(a) were the most recent instalment

rate mentioned in paragraph&#160;(2)(a); and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the amount of GDP-adjusted notional tax mentioned in paragraph&#160;(b)

were the amount of GDP-adjusted notional tax worked out for the purposes of the

most recent amount of instalment that is mentioned in paragraph&#160;(2)(b).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, in relation to the membership change, the Commissioner:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>may exercise the power under subsection&#160;(2) by applying

subsection&#160;(4) more than once; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>must not exercise that power more than once in relation to a particular

instalment rate mentioned in paragraph&#160;(4)(a) or a particular amount of

<sup>*</sup>GDP-adjusted notional tax mentioned in paragraph&#160;(4)(b).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

10  Subdivision&#160;45-R in Schedule&#160;1 (heading)

Repeal the heading, substitute: 

Subdivision&#160;45-R&#151;Special rules for consolidated groups

11  Section&#160;45-850 in Schedule&#160;1

Repeal the section, substitute: 

45-850  What this Subdivision is about

This Subdivision deals with the application of this Part to members of a consolidated group after the group has come into existence but before the members are treated as a single entity for the purposes of this Part.
 This Subdivision also contains special rules in relation to the application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to members of a consolidated group in these circumstances:

	(a)	a group whose members were treated as a single entity under that Subdivision (a _mature group_) is acquired by another group (see section&#160;45-880); or
 	(b)	a member of a mature group ceases to be such a member and becomes the head company of a new group (see section&#160;45-885).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subdivision&#160;45-S extends the operation of this

Subdivision so that it can apply to members of a MEC group. It contains

modifications of this Subdivision for the purposes of that extended operation.

 </dl></dl>

12  Paragraph 45-855(b) in Schedule&#160;1

Repeal the paragraph, substitute:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the period ends before Subdivision&#160;45-Q starts to apply, because of

subsection 45-705(2) or subparagraph 45-705(3)(c)(ii), (4)(d)(ii) or (iv), to

the <sup>*</sup>head company of the group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

13  Paragraphs 45-860(1)(a) and (2)(a) in Schedule&#160;1

Omit "during which Subdivision&#160;45-Q starts to apply to the <sup>*</sup>head company of the group", substitute "that includes the starting time".

14  Paragraphs 45-860(1)(b) and (2)(b) in Schedule&#160;1

 head company", substitute "the <sup>*</sup>head company of the group that includes the starting time".

company of the group because of subsection 45-705(2) or subparagraph

45-705(3)(c)(ii), (4)(d)(ii) or (iv).

</dd> </dl></dl>

17  At the end of section&#160;45-865 in Schedule&#160;1

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>during the <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter or the <sup>*</sup>consolidation

transitional year mentioned in paragraph&#160;(2)(a), the entity is a

<sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of:

</dd>

and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

company of one of the groups is entitled under subsection&#160;(1);

</dd>

18  At the end of Subdivision&#160;45-R in Schedule&#160;1

Add: 

45-880  Continued application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to the head company of an acquired group

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies to a company for which all of the following

conditions are satisfied in relation to a particular time (the _takeover time_):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>just before the takeover time, Subdivision&#160;45-Q applied to the

company as the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the takeover time, the company becomes a <sup>*</sup>wholly-owned

subsidiary of a <sup>*</sup>member of another consolidated group or

<sup>*</sup>MEC group;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that other group is consolidated at or before the takeover time under

section&#160;703-50 or 719-50 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the Commissioner receives the choice (or notice) under that section for

the consolidation of that other group not later than 28 days after the takeover

time, or within such further period (if any) as the Commissioner allows;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>at the takeover time, Subdivision&#160;45-Q (including that Subdivision as

applied under Subdivision&#160;45-S) does not apply to the head company or the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of that other group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this Part only, this Act has effect in relation to the

company and the other <sup>*</sup>members of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group

mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(a) (the _preserved group_) as if,

during the period covered by subsection&#160;(5):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the preserved group had continued to exist as a consolidated group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company were still the <sup>*</sup>head company of the preserved

group; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q had continued to apply to the company as the head

company of the preserved group; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an entity, while being a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of the preserved

group, were not treated as a member of the group mentioned in

paragraph&#160;(1)(b) (the _new group_).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(2) does not stop the company from being a member of the

new group for the purposes of this Part during the period covered by

subsection&#160;(5).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This means, for example, sections&#160;45-855 and 45-860

apply to the head company as a member of the new group.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, for the purposes of applying section&#160;45-855 to the company,

a reference in that section to an application of section&#160;701-1 of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ to the company in relation to the period

mentioned in section&#160;45-855 is taken to be:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a reference only to an application of section&#160;701-1 of that Act to

the company as a member of the new group during that period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>not a reference to an application (because of subsection&#160;(2) of this

section) of section&#160;701-1 of that Act to the company as the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the preserved group during that period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>This subsection covers the period that starts from the start of the

<sup>*</sup>instalment quarter of the company that includes the takeover time

and ends at the earlier of the following times:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the end of the instalment quarter of the company during which the company

ceases to be a member of the new group;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>just before the instalment quarter of the company during which the

Commissioner gives the <sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment rate to the

<sup>*</sup>head company, or the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company, of the

new group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may, on the application of the company made not later

than 28 days after the takeover time, allow such extension of time for the

purposes of paragraph&#160;(1)(d) as he or she considers appropriate.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, nothing in this section prevents the operation of section&#160;45-755 or 45-760 to <sup>*</sup>members of the preserved group while it continues to exist under subsection&#160;(2). </dd> </dl></dl>

45-885  Early application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to the head company of a new group

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies to a company for which all of the following

conditions are satisfied in relation to a particular time (the _starting time_):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>just before the starting time, the company was a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary

member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group, or a member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>just before the starting time, the consolidated group or MEC group was a

mature group (see subsection&#160;(4));</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>at the starting time, either of the following applies:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the company ceases to be a subsidiary member of the consolidated group, or

a member of the MEC group;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the group ceases to exist (otherwise than because a MEC group or

consolidated group is <sup>*</sup>created from the group, or because its

<sup>*</sup>head company or <sup>*</sup>provisional head company becomes a

<sup>*</sup>wholly-owned subsidiary of a member of another mature group);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>at the starting time, the company is the head company of another

consolidated group;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>within 28 days after the starting time, or within such further period (if

any) as the Commissioner allows, the Commissioner receives the choice to

consolidate, at and after the starting time, that other consolidated group

under section&#160;703-50 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this Part:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the instalment rate that the Commissioner is taken to have given to the

company under paragraph 45-760(2)(a) has effect as if it were the

<sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment rate for the company as the

<sup>*</sup>head company of the <sup>*</sup>consolidated group mentioned in

paragraph&#160;(1)(d); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an instalment rate that would otherwise be the initial head company

instalment rate for the company as the head company of that consolidated group

is not to be treated as that initial head company instalment rate.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This means, subject to the provisions in

section&#160;45-705, Subdivision&#160;45-Q starts applying to the company as

the head company of the consolidated group at the start of the instalment

quarter that includes the starting time: see subsection&#160;(2) of that

section and paragraph 45-760(2)(a).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may, on the application of the company made within 28

days after the starting time, allow such extension of time for the purposes of

paragraph&#160;(1)(e) as he or she considers appropriate.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Mature group_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group or a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group is a _mature group_ at a particular time if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>for a consolidated group&#151;Subdivision&#160;45-Q applies to its

<sup>*</sup>head company at that time; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a MEC group&#151;Subdivision&#160;45-Q, as applied under

Subdivision&#160;45-S, applies to its <sup>*</sup>provisional head company at

that time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;45-S&#151;MEC groups

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;45-S
 45-900  What this Subdivision is about
 This Subdivision sets out how this Part applies in relation to MEC groups and their members.

Table of sections

Preliminary

45-905	Objects of Subdivision

General modification rules

45-910	Extended operation of Part to cover MEC groups

Extended operation of Subdivision&#160;45-Q

45-913	Sections&#160;45-705 and 45-740 do not apply to members of MEC groups
 45-915	Application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to provisional head company
 45-917	Assumption for applying section&#160;45-710 (single entity rule)
 45-920	Change of provisional head company
 45-922	Life insurance company

Extended operation of Subdivision&#160;45-R

45-925	Additional modifications of sections&#160;45-855 and 45-860
 45-930	Modifications of sections&#160;45-865 and 45-870 and a related provision
 45-935	Additional modifications of section&#160;45-885

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Preliminary

45-905  Objects of Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The objects of this Subdivision are to:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>extend the operation of this Part (except sections&#160;45-705 and 45-740

and this Subdivision) so that it can apply in relation to <sup>*</sup>MEC

groups and their members; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>modify the rules in this Part for that extended operation so that they

take account of the special characteristics of MEC groups.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

General modification rules

45-910  Extended operation of Part to cover MEC groups

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Part (except sections&#160;45-705 and 45-740 and this Subdivision)

has effect in relation to members of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group in the same way in

which it has effect in relation to <sup>*</sup>members of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, that effect is subject to the modifications set out in the following table and elsewhere in this Subdivision. </dd> </dl></dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Modifications of this Part</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Item</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>A reference in this Part to:</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Is taken to be a reference to:</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a <sup>*</sup>MEC group</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary member of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a member (other than the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company) of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>_Exceptions_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The modifications set out in the table do not apply to the following

provisions:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>this Subdivision;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>subsection 45-30(4) (see section&#160;45-930);</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the note at the end of subsection 45-330(5);</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>note 2 at the end of section&#160;45-700;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>sections&#160;45-705 and 45-740 (see sections&#160;45-913, 45-915 and

45-920);</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>subparagraphs 45-760(1)(c)(i) and (ii);</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the note at the end of section&#160;45-850;</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>sections&#160;45-865 and 45-870 (see section&#160;45-930);</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>paragraphs&#160;(1)(b), (c), (d) and (e), and subsection&#160;(5), of

section&#160;45-880;</dd>

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>paragraphs&#160;(1)(a), (b) and (c), and subsection&#160;(4), of

section&#160;45-885.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The provisions covered by paragraphs&#160;(c), (d), (f),

(g), (i) and (j) apply to members of a MEC group without any modifications.

 </dl></dl>

Extended operation of Subdivision&#160;45-Q

45-913  Sections&#160;45-705 and 45-740 do not apply to members of MEC groups

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In applying Subdivision&#160;45-Q to members of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group, the

Subdivision has effect as if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;45-705 had no effect and section&#160;45-915 had effect

instead; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;45-740 had no effect and section&#160;45-920 had effect

instead.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

45-915  Application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to provisional head company

_Period during which Subdivision applies to provisional head company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subject to sections&#160;45-880 and 45-885 (as applied under this

Subdivision), Subdivision&#160;45-Q applies to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group during the

period:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>starting at the start of the <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter of the company

determined under subsection&#160;(2), (3) or (4); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ending:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>at the end of the instalment quarter of the company determined under

paragraph&#160;(6)(a) or (b); or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>just before the instalment quarter of the company determined under

paragraph&#160;(6)(c).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to the provisional

head company is subject to the modifications set out in this section and

elsewhere in this Subdivision.

 </dl></dl>

_When the period beginsinitial head company instalment rate_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q starts to apply to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at the start of

an <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter under this subsection if, during that

quarter, the Commissioner gives the company (as that provisional head company)

the <sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment rate.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The operation of this subsection may be affected by

section&#160;45-885 (as applied under this Subdivision).

 </dl></dl>

_When the period beginsgroup created from consolidated group_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q starts to apply to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at the start of

an <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter (the _starting quarter_) under

this subsection if all of the following conditions are satisfied:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>during the starting quarter, the Commissioner is notified of the creation

of the MEC group from a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group (see

subsection&#160;(5));</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company is the provisional head company of the MEC group when the

Commissioner is so notified;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>either of the following applies:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q applied to the <sup>*</sup>head company of the

consolidated group at the end of the previous instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the Commissioner gives the <sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment

rate to the head company of the consolidated group during the starting quarter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For the application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to a head

company of a consolidated group: see section&#160;45-705.

 </dl></dl>

_When the period beginsnew provisional head company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q starts to apply to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at the start of

an <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter (the _starting quarter_) under

this subsection if both of the following conditions are satisfied:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company is appointed as the provisional head company of the MEC group

under subsection 719-60(3) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ during

the starting quarter;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>one of the following applies:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q applied to the former provisional head company of

the MEC group at the end of the previous instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the Commissioner gives the <sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment

rate to the former provisional head company of the MEC group during the

starting quarter;</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is notified during the starting quarter of the creation

of the MEC group from a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group and

Subdivision&#160;45-Q applied to the <sup>*</sup>head company of the

consolidated group at the end of the previous instalment quarter;</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is notified during the starting quarter of the creation

of the MEC group from a consolidated group and the Commissioner gives the

initial head company instalment rate to the head company of the consolidated

group during the starting quarter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Notification of creation of MEC group from consolidated group_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsections&#160;(3) and (4), the Commissioner is

notified of the creation of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group from a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group when the Commissioner receives a notice of the

consolidation of the MEC group under subsection 719-40(1) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_When the period ends_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q stops applying to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at the earliest

of the following times after the company becomes the provisional head company:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the end of the <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter during which the MEC group

ceases to exist (other than because a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group is

<sup>*</sup>created from the MEC group);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the end of the instalment quarter during which a consolidated group is

created from the MEC group;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>just before the instalment quarter during which another company is

appointed as the provisional head company of the MEC group under subsection

719-60(3) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The operation of this subsection because of

paragraph&#160;(a) may be affected by section&#160;45-880 (as applied under

this Subdivision).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, Subdivision&#160;45-Q does not apply to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group for any time at

all if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>subsection&#160;(2), (3) or (4), and subsection&#160;(6), would, apart

from this subsection, apply to the company; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the time at which Subdivision&#160;45-Q would stop applying to the company

under subsection&#160;(6) is before the time at which that Subdivision would

start to apply to the company under subsection&#160;(2), (3) or (4).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, Subdivision&#160;45-Q may apply to a company as the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at a time when

the company is not in fact the provisional head company of the group.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	An example of this is when a company replaces another

company as the provisional head company of a MEC group. Under this section and

section&#160;45-920, Subdivision&#160;45-Q may start applying to the company as

if it had already become the provisional head company when it is not yet such a

company.

 </dl></dl>

45-917  Assumption for applying section&#160;45-710 (single entity rule)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In applying section&#160;45-710 to members of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group at a

particular time, the company that is the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company

of the group at that time must be assumed to be the <sup>*</sup>head company of

the group at all times during the period:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>throughout which the group is in existence; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that is all or a part of the income year of the company that includes that

particular time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

45-920  Change of provisional head company

_Object_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The object of this section (except subsection&#160;(9)) is to ensure that,

for the purposes of this Part, when a company becomes the new

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company inherits the history of the former provisional head company;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the history of the new provisional head company is effectively ignored.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section applies to a <sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group (the _new provisional head company_) that is

appointed under subsection 719-60(3) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ if one of the following conditions is satisfied:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the conditions in subsection 45-915(4) are satisfied in relation to the

new provisional head company (whether or not Subdivision&#160;45-Q applies to

the company as the provisional head company of the group for any period of

time);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the new provisional head company is so appointed during the

<sup>*</sup>instalment quarter of the company in which the MEC group is

<sup>*</sup>created from a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group and either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the Commissioner gives the <sup>*</sup>initial head company instalment

rate to the <sup>*</sup>head company of the consolidated group during that

instalment quarter; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q applied to the head company of the consolidated

group at the end of the previous instalment quarter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Everything that happened before the starting time in relation to the

company (the _former company_) that was the <sup>*</sup>provisional

head company of the <sup>*</sup>MEC group immediately before the starting time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is taken to have happened in relation to the new provisional head company

instead of in relation to the former company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is taken to have happened in relation to the new provisional head company

instead of what would (apart from this section) be taken to have happened in

relation to the new provisional head company before the starting time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

just as if, at all times before the starting time:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the new provisional head company had been the former company; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the former company had been the new provisional head company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, the _starting time_ is the

time at which the <sup>*</sup>cessation event happened to the former company

(the event that results in the appointment of the new provisional head

company).</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, subsection&#160;(3) also covers everything that, immediately before the starting time, was taken to have happened in relation to the former company because of: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;701-1 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_(single

entity rule); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;701-5 of that Act (entry history rule); or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>section&#160;703-75 of that Act (effects of an interposed company becoming

the <sup>*</sup>head company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group); or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>section&#160;719-90 of that Act (effects of a change of head company of a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group); or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>section&#160;45-710 in this Schedule (single entity rule for the purposes

of this Part), including an application of that section under this Subdivision;

or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>section&#160;45-740 in this Schedule (effects of an interposed company

becoming the head company of a consolidated group for the purposes of this

Part); or</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>this section; or</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>one or more previous applications of any of the provisions covered by

paragraphs&#160;(a) to (g).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>In addition, and without affecting subsection&#160;(3):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an assessment of the former company for an income year that ends before

the income year that includes the starting time; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an amendment of the assessment;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is taken to be something that had happened to the new provisional head company, whether or not the assessment or amendment is made before the starting time.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>This section has effect for the purposes of applying this Part to members

of the <sup>*</sup>MEC group in relation to an <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter

of the new provisional head company that ends after the starting time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	An assessment mentioned in subsection&#160;(6) may

therefore be taken to be the base assessment of the new provisional head

company for the purposes of this Part.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>Subsections&#160;(1) to (7) are to be disregarded in applying

section&#160;45-915 (about the application of Subdivision&#160;45-Q to a

company as the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, if the Commissioner has given an initial head

company instalment rate to the former company during an earlier instalment

quarter, the rate is not, despite this section, treated as if it had been given

to the new provisional head company for the purposes of section&#160;45-915.

Subject to the other provisions in that section, Subdivision&#160;45-Q

therefore starts applying to the new provisional head company under subsection

45-915(4).

 </dl></dl>

_Special rule for the former company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>A provision of this Part that applies on an entity becoming a member

(other than the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company) of a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group does not apply to the former company when it becomes such a member at the

starting time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;45-755 (the entry rule, as applied under this

Subdivision) therefore does not apply to the former company on the company

becoming such a member of the MEC group.

 </dl></dl>

45-922  Life insurance company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In applying Subdivision&#160;45-Q to members of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group for

an <sup>*</sup>instalment quarter of the <sup>*</sup>provisional head company

of the group in an income year of the provisional head company, the company is

taken to be a <sup>*</sup>life insurance company for that quarter if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>one or more life insurance companies are members of the group at any time

during that quarter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>one or more life insurance companies were members of the group at any time

during a previous instalment quarter of the company in that year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Extended operation of Subdivision&#160;45-R

45-925  Additional modifications of sections&#160;45-855 and 45-860

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In applying sections&#160;45-855 and 45-860 to members of a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group, those sections have effect as if, in addition to the modifications set

out in the table in section&#160;45-910:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a reference in those sections to subsection 45-705(2) were a reference to

subsection 45-915(2); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a reference in those sections to subparagraph 45-705(3)(c)(ii), (4)(d)(ii)

or (iv) were a reference to subparagraph 45-915(3)(c)(ii), (4)(b)(ii) or (iv).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

45-930  Modifications of sections&#160;45-865 and 45-870 and a related provision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>In applying sections&#160;45-865 and 45-870, and subsection 45-30(4)

(which is related to section&#160;45-865), to members of a <sup>*</sup>MEC

group, those provisions have effect as if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a reference in those provisions to a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group were a

reference to a <sup>*</sup>MEC group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a reference in those provisions to a MEC group were a reference to a

consolidated group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This means a reference in those provisions to the head

company of a consolidated group has effect as if it were a reference to the

head company of a MEC group. Similarly, a reference in those provisions to a

subsidiary member of a consolidated group has effect as if it were a reference

to a subsidiary member of a MEC group.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, the modifications in subsection&#160;(1) do not apply to

subsection 45-865(4) and the note at the end of section&#160;45-865.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This means subsection 45-865(4) and the note apply to

members of a MEC group without any modifications.

 </dl></dl>

45-935  Additional modifications of section&#160;45-885

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In applying section&#160;45-885 to members of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group, that

section has effect as if, in addition to the modifications set out in the table

in section&#160;45-910, it had been modified as set out in the following table:

 </dl></dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>

19  Application of amendments

(1)	The amendment made by item&#160;1 applies only in relation to an income year that begins on or after 1&#160;July 2003.
 (2)	The amendments made by items&#160;2 to 18 apply on and after 1&#160;July 2002.

Part&#160;2&#151;Amendment of the Income Tax Assessment Act 1997

20  Subsection 995-1(1) (definition of _consolidation transitional year_)

Repeal the definition, substitute:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_consolidation transitional year_ for a <sup>*</sup>member of a

<sup>*</sup>consolidated group or a member of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group, is an

income year for that member that satisfies both of the following conditions:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the group is in existence during all or any part of that year;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;45-Q in Schedule&#160;1 to the _Taxation Administration Act 1953_ (including that Subdivision as applied under Subdivision&#160;45-S

in that Schedule):

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>does not apply at all to the <sup>*</sup>head company or the

<sup>*</sup>provisional head company of the group during that year; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>starts to apply at any time during that year to the head company or the

provisional head company of the group because of subsection 45-705(2) or

subparagraph 45-705(3)(c)(ii), (4)(d)(ii) or (iv), or subsection 45-915(2) or

subparagraph 45-915(3)(c)(ii), (4)(b)(ii) or (iv), in that Schedule.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

21  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_created_:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group is _created_ from a

<sup>*</sup>MEC group if the consolidated group comes into existence under

section&#160;703-55 at the time the MEC group ceases to exist (as mentioned in

that section); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a MEC group is _created_ from a consolidated group if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the MEC group comes into existence under section&#160;719-40 when a

<sup>*</sup>special conversion event happens to a <sup>*</sup>potential MEC

group derived from an <sup>*</sup>eligible tier-1 company of a <sup>*</sup>top

company; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the eligible tier-1 company was the <sup>*</sup>head company of the

consolidated group (as mentioned in paragraph 719-40(1)(b)).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

22  Subsection 995-1(1) (definition of _initial head company instalment rate_)

Repeal the definition, substitute:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_initial head company instalment rate_, for a <sup>*</sup>head

company of a <sup>*</sup>consolidated group, or a <sup>*</sup>provisional head

company of a <sup>*</sup>MEC group, is an <sup>*</sup>instalment rate worked

out on the basis of:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>for a group that comes into existence in an income year under

section&#160;703-50 or 719-50&#151;the first <sup>*</sup>base assessment of a

company as the head company of that group for which the <sup>*</sup>base year

is that income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a group (the _later group_) for which either of the

following conditions is satisfied:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the later group is <sup>*</sup>created from a group (the _first group_) that comes into existence under section&#160;703-50 or 719-50;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>starting from the first group, consolidated groups or MEC groups are

successively created, ending in the creation of the later group;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		the first base assessment of a company as the head company of the first

group, the later group or any other group covered by subparagraph&#160;(ii),

for which the base year is the income year in which the first group comes into

existence.

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, subparagraph&#160;(b)(ii) covers a

consolidated group that is created from a MEC group, which was in turn created

from a consolidated group that came into existence under section&#160;703-50.

 </dl></dl>

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;26&#151;Loss integrity rules: global method of valuing assets

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

1  Subsection 165-115ZD(1)

After ", a loss", insert "(the _realised loss_)".

2  Subsection 165-115ZD(4)

Repeal the subsection, substitute:

_Adjusted unrealised loss worked out under this section_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The adjusted unrealised loss referred to in paragraph&#160;(2)(a) is

worked out using this method statement:

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Method statement_

_Step 1._	Add up the amount or value of each thing covered by subsection&#160;(5). (If the total exceeds the realised loss, reduce the total by the excess.)
 _Step 2._	Reduce the step 1 amount by so much of the realised loss as it is reasonable to conclude is attributable to _none_ of these:

	(a)	a notional capital loss, or a notional revenue loss, that the company has at that last alteration time in respect of a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset;
 	(b)	a trading stock decrease in relation to that time for a CGT asset that was <sup>*</sup>trading stock of the company at that time.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the equity or debt is a revenue asset, the realised loss

is different from the loss referred to in subsection&#160;(1): see

subsection&#160;(9).

<sup>*</sup>changeover time for the company, be a notional capital gain or

notional revenue gain that the company had under section&#160;165-115F at that

changeover time in respect of a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset; or

</dd>

Division&#160;210&#151;Venture capital franking

Table of Subdivisions

	Guide to Division&#160;210
 210-A	Franking a distribution with a venture capital credit
 210-B	Participating PDFs
 210-C	Distributions that are frankable with a venture capital credit
 210-D	Amount of the venture capital credit on a distribution
 210-E	Distribution statements
 210-F	Rules affecting the allocation of venture capital credits
 210-G	Venture capital sub-account

<center>Back to Top</center>
 210-H	Effect of receiving a distribution franked with a venture capital credit 

Guide to Division&#160;210

Table of sections

210-1	Purpose of venture capital franking
 210-5	How is this achieved?
 210-10	What is a venture capital credit?
 210-15	What does the PDF have to do to distribute the credits?
 210-20	Limits on venture capital franking 

210-1  Purpose of venture capital franking

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The purpose of these rules is to encourage venture capital investment by

superannuation funds and other entities that deal with superannuation.

 </dl></dl>

210-5  How is this achieved?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This is done by giving tax benefits to those entities when they invest in

PDFs, which are the vehicles for venture capital investment. If the PDF makes a

distribution franked with a venture capital credit, the relevant venture

capital investor receives a certain part of a distribution from the PDF as

exempt income and, in addition, is entitled to a tax offset equal to the

venture capital credit.

 </dl></dl>

210-10  What is a venture capital credit?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>There is a venture capital franking sub-account in the franking account of

each PDF.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Venture capital credits arise in the sub-account if the PDF pays income tax that is reasonably attributable to capital gains from venture capital investments. </dd> </dl></dl>

210-15  What does the PDF have to do to distribute the credits?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Only a participating PDF can distribute venture capital credits. A PDF elects

to participate by keeping a record of its venture capital sub-account.

 </dl></dl>

210-20  Limits on venture capital franking

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The venture capital credit on a distribution cannot exceed the franking

credit on the distribution. It is, in this sense, a species of franking

credit.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A PDF can only distribute venture capital credits if it does it so that all members of the PDF receive venture capital credits in proportion to their holdings.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a PDF has a venture capital surplus when it makes a distribution, it must frank the distribution with venture capital credits.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>There are measures to ensure that a PDF does not maintain a venture capital deficit over a prolonged period. </dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;210-A&#151;Franking a distribution with a venture

capital credit

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-A
 210-25  What this Subdivision is about
 A PDF can only frank a distribution with a venture capital credit if certain conditions are met. These conditions are set out in this Subdivision.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

210-30	Franking a distribution with a venture capital credit

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

210-30  Franking a distribution with a venture capital credit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An entity _franks_ a <sup>*</sup>distribution _with a venture capital credit_ if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity is a <sup>*</sup>participating PDF at the time the distribution

is made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the distribution is <sup>*</sup>frankable with a venture capital credit;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity allocates a <sup>*</sup>venture capital credit to the

distribution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Subdivision&#160;210-B&#151;Participating PDFs

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-B
 210-35  What this Subdivision is about
 A PDF may participate if it elects to keep a record of its venture capital sub-account.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

210-40	What is a participating PDF

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

210-40  What is a participating PDF

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>PDF is a _participating PDF_ at a particular time

if it keeps a record of its <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account at that time.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;210-C&#151;Distributions that are frankable with a

venture capital credit

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-C
 210-45  What this Subdivision is about
 A distribution can only be franked with a venture capital credit if all members of the PDF receive distributions in proportion to their holdings.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

210-50	Which distributions can be franked with a venture capital credit?

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

210-50  Which distributions can be franked with a venture capital credit?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>distribution by a <sup>*</sup>participating PDF is

_frankable with a venture capital credit_ if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the distribution is a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the distribution is made under a resolution under which:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>distributions are made to all members of the PDF; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the amount of the distribution per <sup>*</sup>membership interest is the

same for each of those distributions.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;210-D&#151;Amount of the venture capital credit on a

distribution

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-D
 210-55  What this Subdivision is about
 The amount of the venture capital credit on a distribution is that stated in the distribution statement, unless the amount exceeds the franking credit on the distribution.
 In that case, the amount of the venture capital credit on the distribution is taken to be the same as the franking credit.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

210-60	Amount of the venture capital credit on a distribution

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

210-60  Amount of the venture capital credit on a distribution

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The amount of the <sup>*</sup>venture capital credit on a

<sup>*</sup>distribution is that stated in the <sup>*</sup>distribution

statement for the distribution, unless that amount exceeds the

<sup>*</sup>franking credit on the distribution.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the amount of the <sup>*</sup>venture capital credit stated in the <sup>*</sup>distribution statement for a <sup>*</sup>distribution exceeds the <sup>*</sup>franking credit on the distribution, the amount of the venture capital credit is taken to be the same as the amount of the franking credit, and not the amount stated in the distribution statement. </dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;210-E&#151;Distribution statements

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-E

<center>Back to Top</center>

 A participating PDF that makes a distribution franked with a venture capital credit must provide additional information in the distribution statement given to the recipient.
