<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>participating PDF that makes a <sup>*</sup>distribution

<sup>*</sup>franked with a venture capital credit must include in the

<sup>*</sup>distribution statement given to the recipient:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a statement that there is a <sup>*</sup>venture capital credit of a

specified amount on the distribution; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a statement to the effect that the venture capital credit is only relevant

for a taxpayer who is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the trustee of a fund that is a <sup>*</sup>complying superannuation fund

in relation to the income year in which the distribution is made and is not a

self managed superannuation fund (within the meaning of the _Superannuation Industry Supervision Act 1993_); or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the trustee of a fund that is a <sup>*</sup>complying approved deposit

fund  in relation to the income year in which the distribution is made

and is not a self managed superannuation fund (within the meaning of the

_Superannuation Industry Supervision Act 1993_); or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the trustee of a unit trust that is a <sup>*</sup>pooled superannuation

trust  in relation to the income year in which the distribution is made;

or</dd>

	(iv) a <sup>*</sup>life insurance company.

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If, under subsection&#160;(1), a statement must be included in a

<sup>*</sup>distribution statement, the distribution statement is taken not to

have been given unless the statement is included.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;210-F&#151;Rules affecting the allocation of venture

capital credits

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-F
 210-75  What this Subdivision is about
 If a PDF has a venture capital surplus when it makes a distribution frankable with venture capital credits, it must frank the distribution with venture capital credits.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

210-80	Draining the venture capital surplus when a distribution frankable with venture capital credits is made
 210-81	Distributions to be franked with venture capital credits to the same extent
 210-82	Consequences of breaching the rule in section&#160;210-81

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

210-80  Draining the venture capital surplus when a distribution frankable with venture capital credits is made

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a <sup>*</sup>participating PDF would otherwise have a

<sup>*</sup>venture capital surplus at the time a <sup>*</sup>distribution that

is <sup>*</sup>frankable with a venture capital credit is made, the PDF must

either:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>allocate a <sup>*</sup>venture capital credit to the distribution that is

equal to the <sup>*</sup>franking credit on the distribution; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>allocate a venture capital credit to the distribution that either alone or

when added to venture capital credits allocated to other distributions made

under the resolution of the PDF under which the distribution in question is

made, reduces the surplus to nil, or creates a <sup>*</sup>venture capital

deficit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>venture capital debit arises for a <sup>*</sup>participating

PDF when a <sup>*</sup>distribution is made if the PDF does not allocate a

<sup>*</sup>venture capital credit in accordance with subsection&#160;(1). The

amount of the debit is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1215.gif)</sub>

where:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_actual franked amount_ is the amount of the <sup>*</sup>venture

capital credit that is allocated to the <sup>*</sup>distribution by the PDF

(this may be nil). _subsection (1) franked amount_ is the amount of the <sup>*</sup>venture capital credit that would have been allocated to the <sup>*</sup>distribution if the PDF had made the smallest allocation needed to satisfy subsection&#160;(1).  </dl></dl>

210-81  Distributions to be franked with venture capital credits to the same extent

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a <sup>*</sup>PDF <sup>*</sup>franks a <sup>*</sup>distribution with a

venture capital credit, it must frank each other distribution made under the

same resolution with a venture capital credit worked out using the same venture

capital percentage.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The _venture capital percentage_ for a <sup>*</sup>distribution is worked out using the formula: </dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1216.gif)</sub>

210-82  Consequences of breaching the rule in section&#160;210-81

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If a <sup>*</sup>PDF <sup>*</sup>franks a <sup>*</sup>distribution with a

venture capital credit in breach of section&#160;210-81:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the distribution is taken not to have been franked with a venture capital

credit; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each other distribution made under the same resolution is taken not to

have been franked with a venture capital credit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;210-G&#151;Venture capital sub-account

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-G
 210-85  What this Subdivision is about
 This Subdivision:

*	creates a venture capital sub-account for each PDF; and

*	identifies when venture capital credits and debits arise in the sub-account and the amount of those credits and debits; and

*	identifies when there is a venture capital surplus or deficit in the sub-account; and

*	creates a liability to pay venture capital deficit tax if the account is in deficit at certain times.

 210-95	Venture capital deficit tax

 210-150	Deferring venture capital deficit 

210-90  The venture capital sub-account

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Each PDF has a venture capital sub-account in its franking account. The

sub-account exists even if the PDF does not elect to become a participating PDF

by keeping a record of it.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>To the extent that income tax is reasonably attributable to capital gains from venture capital investments, it generates a venture capital credit in the sub-account. There are other circumstances in which a venture capital credit arises.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a PDF receives a refund of that tax, a venture capital debit will arise for the PDF. There are other circumstances in which a venture capital debit will arise, such as on the payment of a distribution franked with a venture capital credit. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

210-95  Venture capital deficit tax

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Venture capital deficit tax is payable if a PDF's venture capital

sub-account is in deficit at the end of the PDF's income year, or immediately

before it ceases to be a PDF.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A PDF's venture capital sub-account may be in deficit, even if its franking account is not. This can happen because only income tax on income of a particular kind (capital gains on venture capital investments) gives rise to venture capital credits. This means that when a PDF anticipates a venture capital credit, it is not only anticipating that income tax will be paid, but that income tax on income of that kind will be paid. Although income tax may, in fact, later be paid, it will not necessarily be income of the kind that would give rise to a venture capital credit. This results in franking credits arising even while the venture capital sub-account remains in deficit.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The discrepancy between the franking account balance and the venture capital sub-account balance can also arise because venture capital credits do not necessarily arise at the same time as the relevant franking credits and debits (see item&#160;1 of the table in section&#160;210-105 and item&#160;2 of the table in section&#160;210-120). </dd> </dl></dl>

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

210-100  Venture capital sub-account

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Each <sup>*</sup>PDF has a _venture capital sub-account_ within

its <sup>*</sup>franking account.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The balance in the venture capital sub-account on

1&#160;July 2002 will be either nil or, if the entity has a venture capital

surplus or deficit immediately before 1&#160;July 2002 under the imputation

scheme existing at that time, an amount calculated under the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

210-110  Determining the extent to which a franking credit is reasonably attributable to a particular payment of tax

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In determining the extent to which a <sup>*</sup>franking credit is

reasonably attributable to a <sup>*</sup>CGT event in relation to a

<sup>*</sup>qualifying SME investment of the <sup>*</sup>PDF, have regard to:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the extent to which the credit can reasonably be attributed to the

<sup>*</sup>payment of a PAYG instalment or the payment of income tax by the

PDF in relation to its <sup>*</sup>section&#160;124ZZB SME assessable income

for an income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the extent to which the section&#160;124ZZB SME assessable income can

reasonably be attributed to the CGT event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

210-115  Participating PDF may elect to have venture capital credits arise on its assessment day

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Before a <sup>*</sup>PDF's assessment day for an income year, the PDF may

elect to have the <sup>*</sup>venture capital credits that arise because of the

<sup>*</sup>payment of PAYG instalments and income tax during that income year

arise on the assessment day.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>PDF's _assessment day_ for an income year is the earlier of: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the day on which the PDF furnishes its return of income for the income

year; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the day on which the Commissioner makes an assessment of the amount of the

PDF's taxable income for that year under section&#160;166 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

210-125  Venture capital debit where CGT limit is exceeded

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>venture capital debit arises for a <sup>*</sup>PDF where the

PDF's net venture capital credits for the income year exceed whichever is the

lesser of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the PDF's CGT limit for that income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the tax paid by the PDF on its <sup>*</sup>SME income component for that

income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Net venture capital credits_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>PDF's _net venture capital credits_ for the

income year is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1217.gif)</sub>

where:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_venture capital credits_ is the total <sup>*</sup>venture capital

credits of the <sup>*</sup>PDF that relate to tax in relation to taxable income

of that income year. _venture capital debits_ is the total <sup>*</sup>venture capital debits of the <sup>*</sup>PDF that relate to tax in relation to taxable income of that income year.  </dl></dl>

_CGT limit_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>PDF's _CGT limit_ for the income year is

worked out using the formula:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1218.gif)</sub>

where:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_ordinary capital gains from all SME CGT events_ means the total of

the <sup>*</sup>ordinary capital gains for the income year for <sup>*</sup>CGT

events in relation to <sup>*</sup>SME investments of the <sup>*</sup>PDF. _ordinary capital gains from venture capital CGT events_ means the total of <sup>*</sup>ordinary capital gains for the income year for <sup>*</sup>CGT events in relation to shares in companies that are <sup>*</sup>qualifying SME investments. _SME tax rate_ is the tax rate applicable to the <sup>*</sup>SME income component of the <sup>*</sup>PDF for the income year.  </dl></dl>

_Tax paid by the PDF on its SME income component_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The _tax paid by the PDF on its SME income component_ for the

income year is the tax paid by the <sup>*</sup>PDF on its <sup>*</sup>SME

income component after allowing <sup>*</sup>tax offsets referred to in

section&#160;4-10 _._

</dd> </dl></dl>

210-130  Venture capital surplus and deficit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>PDF's <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account is in

_surplus_ at a particular time if, at that time, the sum of the

<sup>*</sup>venture capital credits in the account exceeds the sum of the

<sup>*</sup>venture capital debits in the account. The amount of the

_venture capital surplus_ is the amount of the excess.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>PDF's <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account is in _deficit_ at a particular time if, at that time, the sum of the <sup>*</sup>venture capital debits in the account exceeds the sum of the <sup>*</sup>venture capital credits in the account. The amount of the _venture capital deficit_ is the amount of the excess.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>PDF's <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account may be in <sup>*</sup>deficit even though its <sup>*</sup>franking account as a whole is in <sup>*</sup>surplus. Similarly, a PDF's venture capital sub-account may be in surplus even though its franking account as a whole is in deficit. </dd> </dl></dl>

210-135  Venture capital deficit tax

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>While recognising that an entity may anticipate <sup>*</sup>venture

capital credits when <sup>*</sup>franking <sup>*</sup>distributions, the object

of this section is to prevent those credits from being anticipated indefinitely

by requiring the entity to reconcile its <sup>*</sup>venture capital

sub-account at certain times and levying tax if the account is in

<sup>*</sup>deficit.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An entity is liable to pay <sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax imposed by the _New Business Tax System (Venture Capital Deficit Tax) Act 2003_ if its <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account is in <sup>*</sup>deficit at the end of an income year.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>An entity is liable to pay <sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax imposed by the _New Business Tax System (Venture Capital Deficit Tax) Act 2003_ if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>PDF; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>immediately before it ceases to be a PDF, its <sup>*</sup>venture capital

sub-account is in <sup>*</sup>deficit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

210-140  Effect of a liability to pay venture capital deficit tax on franking deficit tax

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an entity is liable to pay <sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax

under subsection 210-135(2) because its <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account

is in <sup>*</sup>deficit at the end of an income year, the amount (if any) of

<sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax that the entity would otherwise be liable to

pay under subsection 205-45(2) because its <sup>*</sup>franking account is in

<sup>*</sup>deficit at that time is reduced by the amount of the liability for

venture capital deficit tax.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an entity is liable to pay <sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax under subsection 210-135(3) because it ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>PDF during an income year, the amount (if any) of <sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax that the entity would otherwise be liable to pay under subsection 205-45(3) because it ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>franking entity at that time is reduced by the amount of the liability for <sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax. </dd> </dl></dl>

210-145  Effect of a liability to pay venture capital deficit tax on the franking account

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an entity incurs a liability to pay <sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit

tax, a <sup>*</sup>franking credit arises for the entity immediately after the

liability arises (the _relevant day_).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The amount of the <sup>*</sup>franking credit is equal to: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if no liability to pay <sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax arises on the

relevant day&#151;the amount of the <sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if a liability to pay franking deficit tax also arises on the relevant

day&#151;the amount of the venture capital deficit tax reduced by the amount of the

franking deficit tax.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

210-150  Deferring venture capital deficit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The object of this section is to ensure that an entity does not avoid

<sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax by deferring the time at which a

<sup>*</sup>venture capital debit occurs.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>refund of income tax for an income year is taken to have been paid to an entity immediately before the end of that year for the purposes of subsection 210-135(2), if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the refund is paid within 3 months after the end of that year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity's <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account would have been in

<sup>*</sup>deficit, or in deficit to a greater extent, at the end of the

previous income year if the refund had been received in the previous income

year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If an entity ceases to be a <sup>*</sup>PDF during an income year, a

<sup>*</sup>refund of income tax is taken to have been paid to it immediately

before it ceased to be a PDF, for the purposes of subsection 210-135(3), if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the refund is attributable to a period in the year during which the entity

was a PDF; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the refund is paid within 3 months after the entity ceases to be a PDF;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account of the entity would have been

in <sup>*</sup>deficit, or in deficit to a greater extent, immediately before

it ceased to be a PDF if the refund had been received before it ceased to be a

PDF.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Subdivision&#160;210-H&#151;Effect of receiving a distribution franked

with a venture capital credit

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;210-H
 210-155  What this Subdivision is about
 A superannuation fund or other entity that deals with superannuation that receives a distribution franked with a venture capital credit is entitled to a tax offset equal to the credit.

Table of sections

210-160	The significance of a venture capital credit
 210-165	Recipients for whom the venture capital credit is not significant

Operative provisions

210-170	Tax offset for certain recipients of distributions franked with venture capital credits
 210-175	Amount of the tax offset
 210-180	Application of Division&#160;207 where the recipient is entitled to a tax offset under section&#160;210-170 

210-160  The significance of a venture capital credit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The venture capital credit on a distribution is only significant in the

hands of a relevant venture capital investor (basically a superannuation fund

or other entity that deals with superannuation).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>That investor  receives a tax offset. In most cases, this will be equal to the venture capital credit.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Under section&#160;124ZM of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_, that part of the distribution that is franked with a venture capital credit is also treated as exempt income in the hands of the entity. </dd> </dl></dl>

210-165  Recipients for whom the venture capital credit is not significant

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For other entities, the fact that all or part of the franking credit on a

distribution is also a venture capital credit can be ignored.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The franking credit will either generate a gross-up of the entity's assessable income and a corresponding tax offset under Division&#160;207 or, if the right to make an election under section&#160;124ZM of the _Income Tax Assessment 1936_ is exercised, the franked part of the distribution will be treated as exempt income.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The unfranked part of the distribution is treated as exempt income under section&#160;124ZM of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_. </dd> </dl></dl>

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

210-170  Tax offset for certain recipients of distributions franked with venture capital credits

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The recipient of a <sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with a

venture capital credit is entitled to a <sup>*</sup>tax offset for the income

year in which the distribution is made if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the recipient is a relevant venture capital investor; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the recipient is not:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>partnership; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a trustee (other than the trustee of an eligible entity within the

meaning of Part&#160;IX of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_); and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the recipient satisfies the <sup>*</sup>residency requirement for an

entity receiving a distribution; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the distribution is not <sup>*</sup>exempt income of the recipient

(ignoring section&#160;124ZM of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_);

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the recipient is not a qualified person in relation to the distribution

for the purposes of Division&#160;1A of Part&#160;IIIAA of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the distribution is not part of a <sup>*</sup>dividend stripping

operation; and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has not made a determination under paragraph 204-30(3)(c)

that no <sup>*</sup>imputation benefit is to arise for the receiving entity in

respect of the distribution; and</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has not made a determination under paragraph 177EA(5)(b)

that no imputation benefit is to arise in respect of the distribution to the

recipient.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Relevant venture capital investors_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The following entities are _relevant venture capital investors_:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the trustee of a fund that is a <sup>*</sup>complying superannuation fund

in relation to the income year in which the <sup>*</sup>distribution is made

and is not a self managed superannuation fund (within the meaning of the

_Superannuation Industry Supervision Act 1993_);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the trustee of a fund that is a <sup>*</sup>complying approved deposit

fund in relation to the income year in which the distribution is made and is

not a self managed superannuation fund (within the meaning of the

_Superannuation Industry Supervision Act 1993_);</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the trustee of a unit trust that is a <sup>*</sup>pooled superannuation

trust in relation to the income year in which the distribution is made;</dd>

	(d) a <sup>*</sup>life insurance company.

</dl></dl></dl>

210-175  Amount of the tax offset

_Where the recipient is not a life insurance company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the entity receiving the <sup>*</sup>distribution is not a

<sup>*</sup>life insurance company, the <sup>*</sup>tax offset is equal to the

<sup>*</sup>venture capital credit on the distribution.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Where the recipient is a life insurance company_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the entity receiving the <sup>*</sup>distribution is a <sup>*</sup>life

insurance company, the <sup>*</sup>tax offset is worked out using the formula:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1219.gif)</sub>

where:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_complying superannuation class of taxable income_ means the

<sup>*</sup>complying superannuation class of taxable income of the company for

the income year in which the <sup>*</sup>distribution is made. _tax offset to which the entity would otherwise be entitled_ is the <sup>*</sup>tax offset that the company would be entitled to under subsection&#160;(1) if the entity were not a life insurance company. _total income_ is the company's assessable income for the income year.  </dl></dl>

210-180  Application of Division&#160;207 where the recipient is entitled to a tax offset under section&#160;210-170

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If the recipient of a <sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with a

venture capital credit is entitled to a <sup>*</sup>tax offset under

section&#160;210-170, Division&#160;207 does not apply to that <sup>*</sup>part

of the distribution that is venture capital franked.

 </dl></dl>

Division&#160;210&#151;Venture capital franking

210-1  Order of events provision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The venture capital sub-account of a PDF under Part&#160;IIIAA of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_(the _old sub-account__)_ is closed off at the end of 30&#160;June 2002 and

an opening balance is created in the PDF's venture capital sub-account under

section&#160;210-100 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as follows:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any estimated venture capital debits in the old sub-account at the end of

30&#160;June 2002 are washed out of the account under section&#160;210-5; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>then:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>in the case of a PDF whose 2001-02 franking year ends on 30&#160;June 2002

under Part&#160;IIIAA of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_&#151;the PDF's

venture capital sub-account balance is converted under section&#160;210-10 to a

tax paid basis; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>in the case of a PDF whose 2001-02 franking year ends before 30&#160;June

2002 under Part&#160;IIIAA of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_&#151;the

PDF's venture capital sub-account balance is converted under

section&#160;210-15 to a tax paid basis.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

210-5  Washing estimated venture capital debits out of the old sub-account before conversion

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If, under Part&#160;IIIAA of the _Income Tax Assessment act 1936_, the

termination time in relation to an estimated venture capital debit of a PDF

would, but for this section, occur after the end of 30&#160;June 2002, it is

taken to have occurred at the end of 30&#160;June 2002.

 </dl></dl>

because of the surplus; and</dd>

sub-account established under section&#160;210-100 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ for the PDF.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

1  Subsections 202-75(2) and (3)

Repeal the subsections, substitute:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The statement must be given on or before the day on which the

<sup>*</sup>distribution is made, unless the entity is allowed to give the

statement at a later time under subsection&#160;(3).</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the entity is a <sup>*</sup>private company for the income year in which the <sup>*</sup>distribution is made, the statement must be given: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, the entity is not allowed to give the statement at a later time

credits allocated to other distributions made by the entity during the income

year, result in the entity having a liability for <sup>*</sup>franking deficit

tax, or an increased liability for franking deficit tax, at the end of the

income year.

</dd> </dl></dl>

3  After Division&#160;210

Insert: 

Division&#160;214&#151;Administering the imputation system

Table of Subdivisions

	Guide to Division&#160;214
 214-A	Franking returns
 214-B	Franking assessments
 214-C	Amending franking assessments
 214-D	Collection and recovery
 214-E	Records, information and tax agents 

Guide to Division&#160;214

Table of sections

214-1	Purpose of the system
 214-5	Key features 

214-1  Purpose of the system

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		These provisions:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>allow the Commissioner to gather sufficient information to determine

whether tax is payable by a corporate tax entity under the imputation system;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>provide for the Commissioner to assess the amount of tax that is payable;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>specify when the tax is payable; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>establish systems to support the assessment and collection of the tax.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-5  Key features

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Initial information about a corporate tax entity's franking activities is

provided by means of a return, called a franking return, given by the entity to

the Commissioner.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commissioner is able to require corporate tax entities to give a franking return for an income year by publishing a notice in the _Gazette_.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Commissioner is also able to require a particular corporate tax entity to give a franking return for one or more income years. The Commissioner might do this, for example, if the Commissioner wishes to audit the corporate tax entity's franking activities over a number of years.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may assess whether tax is payable under the imputation system and the amount of that tax.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>In most cases, this is done by treating the first return of a corporate tax entity for an income year as an assessment by the Commissioner. To this extent, there is self-assessment.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>An assessment by the Commissioner is conclusive evidence of a corporate tax entity's tax liabilities under the imputation system, except for the purposes of objection, review and appeal processes under Part&#160;IVC of the _Tax Administration Act 1953_(see section&#160;177 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ and sections&#160;214-50 and 214-85 of this Act).</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>Assessments can be amended by the Commissioner within certain time limits. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Subdivision&#160;214-A&#151;Franking returns

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;214-A
  214-10  What this Subdivision is about
 A franking return for an income year provides the Commissioner with information about a corporate tax entity's franking activities during that year.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

214-15	Notice to give a franking return&#151;general notice
 214-20	Notice to a specific corporate tax entity
 214-25	Content and form of a franking return
 214-30	Franking account balance
 214-35	Venture capital sub-account balance
 214-40	Meaning of _franking tax_
 214-45	Effect of a refund on franking returns
 214-50	Evidence

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

214-15  Notice to give a franking return&#151;general notice

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may publish a notice in the _Gazette_ requiring each

<sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity to which the notice applies to give the

Commissioner a <sup>*</sup>franking return for an income year specified in the

notice.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An entity to which the notice applies must comply with the requirement within the time specified in the notice, or within any further time allowed by the Commissioner. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-20  Notice to a specific corporate tax entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may give a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity a written

notice requiring the entity to give the Commissioner a <sup>*</sup>franking

return for an income year specified in the notice.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The entity must comply with the requirement within the time specified in the notice, or within any further time allowed by the Commissioner.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The entity must comply with the requirement regardless of whether the entity has given, or has been required to give, the Commissioner a return under section&#160;214-15\. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-25  Content and form of a franking return

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity must include the following information

in its <sup>*</sup>franking return for an income year:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the entity is a <sup>*</sup>franking entity at the end of the income

year&#151;its <sup>*</sup>franking account balance at the end of the income year;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the entity ceased to be a franking entity during the income year&#151;its

franking account balance immediately before it ceased to be a franking entity;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the entity is a <sup>*</sup>PDF at the end of the income year&#151;its

<sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account balance at the end of the income year;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the entity ceased to be a PDF during the income year&#151;its venture

capital sub-account balance immediately before it ceased to be a PDF; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the amounts (if any) of <sup>*</sup>franking tax which the entity is

liable to pay because of events that have occurred, or are taken to have

occurred, during the income year; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>any other information required by the Commissioner for the purposes of

administering this Part.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The return must be in writing in the approved form.

</dd> </dl></dl>

214-30  Franking account balance

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity's _franking account balance_

at a particular time is:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the entity has a <sup>*</sup>franking surplus or a <sup>*</sup>franking

deficit at that time&#151;the amount of the surplus or deficit; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the entity does not have a franking surplus or a franking deficit at

that time&#151;nil.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

214-35  Venture capital sub-account balance

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>PDF's _venture capital sub-account balance_ at a

particular time is:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the PDF has a <sup>*</sup>venture capital surplus or a

<sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit at that time&#151;the amount of the surplus or

deficit; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the entity does not have a venture capital surplus or a venture capital

deficit at that time&#151;nil.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-40  Meaning of _franking tax_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Each of the following is a _franking tax_:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>over-franking tax;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>venture capital deficit tax.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-45  Effect of a refund on franking returns

_If no franking return is outstanding_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity receives a <sup>*</sup>refund of income

tax; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the receipt of the refund gives rise to a liability, or an increased

liability, to pay <sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax because of the operation of

subsection 205-50(2) or (3); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>when the refund is received, the entity does not have a

<sup>*</sup>franking return that is <sup>*</sup>outstanding for the income year

in which the liability arose;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the entity must give the Commissioner a franking return for the income year within 14 days after the refund is received.

_Refund received within 14 days before an outstanding franking return is due_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an entity receives a <sup>*</sup>refund of income tax; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the receipt of the refund gives rise to a liability, or an increased

liability, to pay <sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax because of the operation of

subsection 205-50(2) or (3); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>when the refund is received, the entity has a <sup>*</sup>franking return

that is <sup>*</sup>outstanding for the income year in which the liability

arose; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity receives the refund within the period of 14 days ending on the

day by which the outstanding return must be given to the Commissioner;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the entity may, instead of accounting for the liability, or increased liability, in the outstanding return, account for it in a further return given to the Commissioner within 14 days after the refund is received.

_Meaning of outstanding_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>franking return for an income year is

_outstanding_ at a particular time if each of the following is true

at that time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity has been required to give a

<sup>*</sup>franking return for the income year;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the time within which the franking return must be given has not yet

passed;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the franking return has not yet been given.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

214-50  Evidence

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;177 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies as if a

reference in that section to a return included a reference to a

<sup>*</sup>franking return.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;214-B&#151;Franking assessments

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;214-B
 214-55  What this Subdivision is about
 The Commissioner may make an assessment of a corporate tax entity's liability to pay franking tax, and the franking account balance and the venture capital sub-account balance on which that liability is based. An entity's first return for an income year is treated as an assessment by the Commissioner. To this extent, there is self-assessment.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

214-60	Commissioner may make a franking assessment
 214-65	Commissioner taken to have made a franking assessment on first return
 214-70	Part-year assessment
 214-75	Validity of assessment
 214-80	Objections
 214-85	Evidence

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

214-60  Commissioner may make a franking assessment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may make an assessment of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity is a <sup>*</sup>franking entity at

the end of the income year&#151;its <sup>*</sup>franking account balance at the end

of the income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if a corporate tax entity ceased to be a franking entity during the income

year&#151;its franking account balance immediately before it ceased to be a

franking entity; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if a corporate tax entity is a <sup>*</sup>PDF at the end of the income

year&#151;its <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account balance at the end of the

income year; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if a corporate tax entity ceased to be a PDF during the income year&#151;its

venture capital sub-account balance immediately before it ceased to be a PDF;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the amounts (if any) of <sup>*</sup>franking tax which the entity is

liable to pay because of events that have occurred, or are taken to have

occurred, during the income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This is a _franking assessment_ for the entity for the income year.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commissioner must give the entity notice of the assessment as soon as

practicable after making the assessment.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The notice may be included in a notice of any other assessment under this Act. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-65  Commissioner taken to have made a franking assessment on first return

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity gives the Commissioner a

<sup>*</sup>franking return for an income year on a particular day (the

_return day_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the return is the first franking return given by the entity for the year;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has not already made a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment

for the entity for the year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner is taken to have made a franking assessment for the entity for the year on the return day, and to have assessed:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity's <sup>*</sup>franking account balance at a particular time as

that stated in the return as the balance at that time; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the entity's <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account balance (if any) at a

particular time as that stated in the return as the balance at that time; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the amounts (if any) of <sup>*</sup>franking tax payable by the entity

because of events that have occurred, or are taken to have occurred, during

that income year as those stated in the return.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The return is taken to be notice of the assessment signed by the

Commissioner and given to the entity on the return day.

</dd> </dl></dl>

214-70  Part-year assessment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may, at any time during an income year, make a

<sup>*</sup>franking assessment for a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity for a

particular period within that year as if the beginning and end of that period

were the beginning and end of an income year.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>This Part applies, for the purposes of that assessment, as if the beginning and end of the period were the beginning and end of an income year. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-75  Validity of assessment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The validity of a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment is not affected because any

of the provisions of this Act have not been complied with.

 </dl></dl>

214-80  Objections

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity is dissatisfied with a

<sup>*</sup>franking assessment made in relation to the entity, the entity may

object against the assessment in the manner set out in Part&#160;IVC of the

_Taxation Administration Act 1953_.

 </dl></dl>

214-85  Evidence

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;177 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies as if a

reference in that section to an assessment or a notice of assessment included a

reference to a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment or a notice of a franking

assessment, as required.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;214-C&#151;Amending franking assessments

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;214-C
 214-90  What this Subdivision is about
 The Commissioner may amend franking assessments within certain time limits.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

214-95	Amendments within 3 years of the original assessment
 214-100	Amended assessments are treated as franking assessments
 214-105	Further return as a result of a refund affecting a franking deficit tax liability
 214-110	Later amendments&#151;on request
 214-115	Later amendments&#151;failure to make proper disclosure
 214-120	Later amendments&#151;fraud or evasion
 214-125	Further amendment of an amended particular
 214-130	Other later amendments
 214-135	Amendment on review etc.
 214-140	Notice of amendments

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

214-95  Amendments within 3 years of the original assessment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may amend a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment for a

<sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity for an income year at any time during the

period of 3 years after the <sup>*</sup>original franking assessment day for

the entity for that year.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The _original franking assessment_ _day_ for a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity for an income year is the day on which the first <sup>*</sup>franking assessment for the entity for the income year is made. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-100  Amended assessments are treated as franking assessments

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Once an amended <sup>*</sup>franking assessment for a corporate tax entity

for an income year is made, it is taken to be a _franking assessment_ for the entity for the year.

 </dl></dl>

214-105  Further return as a result of a refund affecting a franking deficit tax liability

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment for a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity

for an income year has been made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on a particular day (the _further return day_) the entity

gives the Commissioner a further return for the income year under subsection

214-45(1) (because the entity has received a <sup>*</sup>refund of income tax

that affects its liability to pay <sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner is taken to have amended the entity's franking assessment on the further return day, and to have assessed:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity's <sup>*</sup>franking account balance at a particular time as

that stated in the further return as the balance at that time; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity's <sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account balance (if any) at a

particular time as that stated in the further return as the balance at that

time; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the amounts (if any) of <sup>*</sup>franking tax payable by the entity

because of events that have occurred, or are taken to have occurred, during

that income year as those stated in the further return.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The further return is taken to be notice of the amended assessment signed

by the Commissioner and given to the entity on the further return day.

</dd> </dl></dl>

214-110  Later amendments&#151;on request

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The Commissioner may amend a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment for a

<sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity for an income year after the end of the period

of 3 years after the <sup>*</sup>original franking assessment day for the

entity for the year if, within that 3 year period:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity applies for the amendment; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity gives the Commissioner all the information necessary for making

the amendment.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-115  Later amendments&#151;failure to make proper disclosure

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity does not make a full and true

disclosure to the Commissioner of the information necessary for a

<sup>*</sup>franking assessment for the entity for an income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in making the assessment, the Commissioner makes an

<sup>*</sup>under-assessment; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is not of the opinion that the under-assessment is due to

fraud or evasion;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner may amend the assessment at any time during the period of 6 years after the <sup>*</sup>original franking assessment day for the entity for the year.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commissioner makes an _under-assessment_ in a

<sup>*</sup>franking assessment (the _earlier assessment_) if, in

amending the earlier assessment, the Commissioner would have to do one or more

of the following for the amended assessment to be correct:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>reduce the <sup>*</sup>franking surplus (including to a nil balance);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>increase the <sup>*</sup>franking deficit (including from a nil

balance);</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>increase <sup>*</sup>franking tax payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-120  Later amendments&#151;fraud or evasion

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity does not make a full and true

disclosure to the Commissioner of the information necessary for a

<sup>*</sup>franking assessment for the entity for an income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in making the assessment, the Commissioner makes an

<sup>*</sup>under-assessment; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is of the opinion that the under-assessment is due to

fraud or evasion;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

the Commissioner may amend the assessment at any time. 

214-125  Further amendment of an amended particular

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment has been amended (the _first amendment_) in any particular; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is of the opinion that it would be just to further amend

the assessment in that particular so as to <sup>*</sup>reduce the assessment;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner may do so within a period of 3 years after the first amendment.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commissioner _reduces a franking assessment_ if the

Commissioner amends the assessment by doing one or more of the following:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>increasing the <sup>*</sup>franking surplus (including from a nil

balance);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>decreasing the <sup>*</sup>franking deficit (including to a nil

balance);</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>decreasing <sup>*</sup>franking tax payable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-130  Other later amendments

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In a case not covered by section&#160;214-110, 214-115, 214-120 or 214-125,

the Commissioner may amend the <sup>*</sup>franking assessment for a

<sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity for an income year after the period of 3 years

after the <sup>*</sup>original assessment day has expired, but not so as to

<sup>*</sup>reduce the assessment.

 </dl></dl>

214-135  Amendment on review etc.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Nothing in this Subdivision prevents the amendment of a <sup>*</sup>franking

assessment:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to give effect to a decision on a review or appeal; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to <sup>*</sup>reduce the assessment as a result of an objection made

under this Act or pending an appeal or review.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-140  Notice of amendments

 <dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the Commissioner amends an entity's <sup>*</sup>franking assessment,

the Commissioner must give the entity notice of the amendment as soon as

practicable after making the amendment.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The notice may be included in a notice of any other assessment under this Act. </dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;214-D&#151;Collection and recovery

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;214-D 214-145  What this Subdivision is about
 Franking tax is due and payable at certain times and the general interest charge applies to unpaid amounts.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

214-150	Due date for payment of franking tax
 214-155	General interest charge
 214-160	Refunds of amounts overpaid
 214-165	Security for payment of tax

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

214-150  Due date for payment of franking tax

_General rule_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Unless this section provides otherwise, <sup>*</sup>franking tax assessed

for a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity because of events that have occurred, or

are taken to have occurred, during an income year is due and payable on the

last day of the month immediately following the end of the income year.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Part-year assessments_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>Franking tax payable because of an assessment under

section&#160;214-70 (a part-year assessment) is due and payable on the day

specified in the notice of assessment as the day on which it is due and payable.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Amended assessmentsother than because of deficit deferral_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the Commissioner amends a <sup>*</sup>franking assessment (the

_earlier assessment_) other than because of the operation of

section&#160;214-105 (an amendment because of a refund of tax that affects

<sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax liability); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount of <sup>*</sup>franking tax of a particular type payable under

the amended assessment exceeds the amount of franking tax of that type payable

under the earlier assessment;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the excess amount is due and payable one month after the day on which the assessment was amended.

_Tax payable because of deficit deferral_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity receives a <sup>*</sup>refund of income

tax; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the receipt of the refund gives rise to a liability, or an increased

liability, to pay <sup>*</sup>franking deficit tax because of the operation of

subsection 205-50(2) or (3);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the franking deficit tax or, if there is an increase in an existing liability to pay franking deficit tax, the difference between the original liability and the increased liability, is due and payable on:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the entity accounts for the liability, or increased liability, in a

<sup>*</sup>franking return that is <sup>*</sup>outstanding for the income year

in which the liability arose&#151;the day on which the outstanding return is

required to be given to the Commissioner; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;14 days after the day on which the refund was received.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-155  General interest charge

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>franking tax of a particular type payable by a

<sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity remains unpaid after the time by which it is

due and payable; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has not allocated the unpaid amount to an <sup>*</sup>RBA;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the entity is liable to pay the <sup>*</sup>general interest charge on the unpaid amount for each day in the period that:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>starts at the beginning of the day on which the franking tax was due to be

paid; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>ends at the end of the last day on which, at the end of the day, any of

the following remains unpaid:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the franking tax;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>general interest charge on any of the franking tax.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The general interest charge is worked out under

Division&#160;1 of Part&#160;IIA of the _Taxation Administration Act 1953_.

 </dl></dl>

214-160  Refunds of amounts overpaid

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;172 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies for the

purposes of this Part as if references in that section to tax included

references to <sup>*</sup>franking tax.

 </dl></dl>

214-165  Security for payment of tax

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In section&#160;213 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_(under which

the Commissioner may require security for the payment of income tax), a

reference to income tax includes a reference to <sup>*</sup>franking tax.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;214-E&#151;Records, information and tax agents

 Guide to Subdivision&#160;214-E 214-170  What this Subdivision is about
 Generally applicable provisions to do with record keeping, information gathering and tax agents apply for the purposes of the imputation system.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

214-175	Record keeping
 214-180	Power of Commissioner to obtain information
 214-185	Tax agents

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions

214-175  Record keeping

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Section&#160;262A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies for

the purposes of this Part as if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the reference in that section to a person carrying on a business were a

reference to a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the reference in paragraph&#160;(2)(a) of that section to the person's

income and expenditure were a reference to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the entity's <sup>*</sup>franking account balance; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the entity's liability to pay <sup>*</sup>franking tax; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>paragraph&#160;(5)(a) of that section were omitted.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>PDF does not need to maintain records under

section&#160;262A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ in relation to a

<sup>*</sup>venture capital sub-account if the <sup>*</sup>PDF does not elect

to be a <sup>*</sup>participating PDF.

</dd> </dl></dl>

214-180  Power of Commissioner to obtain information

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;264 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies for the

purposes of this Part as if the reference in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) of that

section to a person's income or assessment were a reference to a matter

relevant to the administration or operation of this Part.

 </dl></dl>

214-185  Tax agents

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Part&#160;VIIA of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies in

relation to a return given, or objection made, for the purposes of this Part as

it applies to an income tax return or objection.

 </dl></dl>

section&#160;214-30.

 </dl></dl>

Insert:

<center>Back to Top</center>

_franking assessment_ has the meaning given by subsection 214-60(1)

and affected by section&#160;214-100.

 </dl></dl>

6  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_franking return_ means a return required under

Subdivision&#160;214-A.

 </dl></dl>

7  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_franking tax_ has the meaning given by section&#160;214-40.

 </dl></dl>

8  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_original franking assessment day_ has the meaning given by

subsection 214-95(2).

 </dl></dl>

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_outstanding_, within the context of <sup>*</sup>franking

 </dl></dl>

 </dl></dl>

 </dl></dl>
