 </dl></dl>

_Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_

13  After Division&#160;210

Insert: 

Division&#160;214&#151;Administering the imputation system

214-1  Application

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This Division  applies to a corporate tax entity if a liability to pay

franking deficit tax arises for the entity under section&#160;205-25 of this

Act because of events that occur within a period of 12 months ending on

30&#160;June in any year (the _balancing period_).

 </dl></dl>

214-5  Entity must give a franking return

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The entity must give the Commissioner a franking return for the balancing

period setting out the following information before the end of the month

immediately following the end of the period:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the entity is a franking entity at the end of the balancing period&#151;its

franking account balance at the end of the period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the entity ceases to be a franking entity during the balancing

period&#151;its franking account balance immediately before it ceased to be a

franking entity; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) of franking deficit tax that the entity is liable to

pay under section&#160;205-25 of this Act because of events that have occurred,

or are taken to have occurred, during the balancing period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The return must be in writing in the approved form.

</dd> </dl></dl>

214-10  Notice to a specific corporate tax entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may give the entity a written notice requiring the entity

to give the Commissioner a franking return for the balancing period.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The entity must comply with the requirement within the time specified in the notice, or within any further time allowed by the Commissioner.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The entity must comply with the requirement regardless of whether the entity has given, or has been required to give, the Commissioner a return under section&#160;214-5\. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-15  Effect of a refund on franking returns

_If no franking return is outstanding_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity receives a refund of income tax; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the receipt of the refund gives rise to a liability, or an increased

liability, to pay franking deficit tax because of the operation of subsection

205-30(2) or (3) of this Act; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>when the refund is received, the entity does not have a franking return

that is outstanding for the balancing period in which the liability arose;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the entity must give the Commissioner a franking return for the period within 14 days after the refund is received.

_Refund received within 14 days before an outstanding franking return is due_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity receives a refund of income tax; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the receipt of the refund gives rise to a liability, or an increased

liability, to pay franking deficit tax because of the operation of subsection

205-30(2) or (3) of this Act; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>when the refund is received, the entity does not have a franking return

that is outstanding for the balancing period in which the liability arose;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity receives the refund within the period of 14 days ending on the

day by which the outstanding return must be given to the Commissioner;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the entity may, instead of accounting for the liability, or increased liability, in the outstanding return, account for it in a further return given to the Commissioner within 14 days after the refund is received.

_Meaning of outstanding_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A franking return for a balancing period is _outstanding_ at a

particular time if each of the following is true at that time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity has been required to give a franking return for the period;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the time within which the franking return must be given has not yet

passed;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the franking return has not yet been given.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-20  Franking returns for the income year

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A franking return for a balancing period  is in addition to any

franking return that the entity is required to give to the Commissioner under

Subdivision&#160;214-A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ for the

income year in which the balancing period ends.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, if an entity is required to give a franking return for a balancing period, it is not required to include in its franking return for the income year in which that period ends anything that should have been included in the franking return for the balancing period. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-25  Commissioner may make a franking assessment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may make an assessment of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the entity is a franking entity at the end of the balancing period&#151;its

franking account balance at the end of the period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the entity ceases to be a franking entity during the balancing

period&#151;its franking account balance immediately before it ceased to be a

franking entity; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) of franking deficit tax that the entity is liable to

pay under section&#160;205-25 of this Act because of events that have occurred,

or are taken to have occurred, during the balancing period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This is a _franking assessment_ for the entity for the balancing period.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Commissioner must give the entity notice of the assessment as soon as

practicable after making the assessment.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The notice may be included in a notice of any other assessment under this Act. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-30  Commissioner taken to have made a franking assessment on first return

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity gives the Commissioner a franking return under

section&#160;214-5 or 214-10 of this Act on a particular day (the _return day_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the return is the first franking return given to the Commissioner by the

entity for the balancing period; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has not already made a franking assessment for the entity

for that period;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner is taken to have made a franking assessment for the entity for the period on the return day, and to have assessed:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity's franking account balance at a particular time as that stated

in the return as the balance at that time; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) of franking deficit tax payable by the entity because

of events that have occurred, or are taken to have occurred, during the period

as those stated in the return.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The return is taken to be notice of the assessment signed by the

Commissioner and given to the entity on the return day.

</dd> </dl></dl>

214-35  Amendments within 3 years of the original assessment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may amend a franking assessment for the entity for the

balancing period at any time during the period of 3 years after the original

assessment day for the entity for the period.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The _original assessment day_ for the entity for the balancing period is the day on which the first franking assessment for the entity for the period is made. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-40  Amended assessments are treated as franking assessments

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Once an amended franking assessment for the entity for the balancing period

is made, it is taken to be a _franking assessment_ for the entity

for the period.

 </dl></dl>

214-45  Further return as a result of a refund affecting a franking deficit tax liability

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a franking assessment for the entity for the balancing period has been

made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on a particular day (the _further return day_) the entity

gives the Commissioner a further return for the balancing period under

subsection 214-15(1) of this Act (because the entity has received a refund of

income tax that affects its liability to pay franking deficit tax);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

the Commissioner is taken to have amended the entity's franking assessment on the further return day, and to have assessed:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity's franking account balance at a particular time as that stated

in the further return as the balance at that time; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the amount of franking deficit tax payable by the entity because of events

that have occurred, or are taken to have occurred, during the period as those

stated in the further return.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The further return is taken to be notice of the amended assessment signed

by the Commissioner and given to the entity on the further return day.

</dd> </dl></dl>

214-50  Later amendments&#151;on request

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The Commissioner may amend a franking assessment for the entity for the

balancing period after the end of a period of 3 years after the original

franking assessment day if, within that 3 year period:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity applies for the amendment; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity gives the Commissioner all the information necessary for making

the amendment.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-55  Later amendments&#151;failure to make proper disclosure

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity does not make a full and true disclosure to the Commissioner of

the information necessary for a franking assessment for the entity for the

balancing period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in making the assessment, the Commissioner makes an under-assessment;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is not of the opinion that the under-assessment is due to

fraud or evasion;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner may amend the assessment at any time during the period of 6 years after the original franking assessment day. 

214-60  Later amendments&#151;fraud or evasion

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity does not make a full and true disclosure to the Commissioner of

the information necessary for a franking assessment for the entity for the

balancing period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in making the assessment, the Commissioner makes an under-assessment;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is of the opinion that the under-assessment is due to

fraud or evasion;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner may amend the assessment at any time. 

214-65  Further amendment of an amended particular

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a franking assessment for the entity for the balancing period has been

amended (the _first amendment_) in any particular; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Commissioner is of the opinion that it would be just to further amend

the assessment in that particular so as to reduce the assessment;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Commissioner may do so within a period of 3 years after the first amendment. 

214-70  Other later amendments

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In a case not covered by sections&#160;214-50, 214-55, 214-60 or 214-65, the

Commissioner may amend the franking assessment for the entity for the balancing

period after the period of 3 years after the original assessment day has

expired, but not so as to reduce the assessment.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

214-75  Amendment on review etc.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Nothing in this Division prevents the amendment of a franking assessment for

the entity for the balancing period:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to give effect to a decision on a review or appeal; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to reduce the assessment as a result of an objection made under this Act

or pending an appeal or review.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-80  Notice of amendments

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the Commissioner amends the entity's franking assessment for the

balancing period, the Commissioner must give the entity notice of the amendment

as soon as practicable after making the amendment.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The notice may be included in a notice of any other assessment under this Act. </dd> </dl></dl>

214-85  Validity of assessment

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The validity of a franking assessment for the entity for the balancing period

is not affected because any of the provisions of this Act (as defined in the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_) have not been complied with.

 </dl></dl>

214-90  Objections

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If a corporate tax entity is dissatisfied with a franking assessment made in

relation to the entity under this Division, the entity may object against the

assessment in the manner set out in Part&#160;IVC of the _Taxation Administration Act 1953_.

 </dl></dl>

214-95  Evidence

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;177 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies as if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a reference in that section to a return included a reference to a franking

return under this Division; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a reference in that section to an assessment or a notice of assessment

included a reference to a franking assessment or a notice of a franking

assessment (as required) under this Division.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-100  Due date for payment of franking tax

_General rule_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Unless this section provides otherwise, franking deficit tax assessed for

the entity because of events that have occurred, or are taken to have occurred,

during the balancing period is due and payable on the last day of the month

immediately following the end of the balancing period.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Amended assessmentsother than because of deficit deferral_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the Commissioner amends a franking assessment for the entity for the

balancing period (the _earlier assessment_) other than because of

the operation of section&#160;214-30 (an amendment because of a refund of tax

that affects franking deficit tax liability); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount of franking deficit tax payable under the amended assessment

exceeds the amount of franking deficit tax payable under the earlier assessment;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the excess amount is due and payable one month after the day on which the assessment was amended.

_Tax payable because of deficit deferral_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity receives a refund of income tax; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the receipt of the refund gives rise to a liability, or an increased

liability, to pay franking deficit tax because of the operation of subsection

205-30(2) or (3);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

the franking deficit tax or, if there is an increase in an existing liability to pay franking deficit tax, the difference between the original liability and the increased liability, is due and payable on:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the entity accounts for the liability, or increased liability, in a

franking return that is outstanding for the balancing period in which the

liability arose&#151;the day on which the outstanding return is required to be

given to the Commissioner; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;14 days after the day on which the refund was received.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-105  General interest charge

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>franking deficit tax that is payable by the entity remains unpaid after

the time by which it is due and payable; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has not allocated the unpaid amount to an RBA;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the entity is liable to pay the general interest charge on the unpaid amount for each day in the period that:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>starts at the beginning of the day on which the franking deficit tax was

due to be paid; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>ends at the end of the last day on which, at the end of the day, any of

the following remains unpaid:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the franking deficit tax;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>general interest charge on any of the franking deficit tax.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The general interest charge is worked out under

Division&#160;1 of Part&#160;IIA of the _Taxation Administration Act 1953_.

 </dl></dl>

214-110  Refunds of amounts overpaid

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;172 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies for the

purposes of this Division as if references in that section to tax included

references to franking deficit tax.

 </dl></dl>

214-115  Security for payment of tax

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		In section&#160;213 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_(under which

the Commissioner may require security for the payment of income tax), a

reference to income tax includes a reference to franking tax.

 </dl></dl>

214-120  Record keeping

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;262A of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies for

the purposes of this Division as if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the reference in that section to a person carrying on a business were a

reference to a corporate tax entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the reference in paragraph&#160;(2)(a) of that section to the person's

income and expenditure were a reference to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the entity's franking account balance; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the entity's liability to pay franking tax; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>paragraph&#160;(5)(a) of that section were omitted.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

214-125  Power of Commissioner to obtain information

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Section&#160;264 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies for the

purposes of this Division as if the reference in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) of that

section to a person's income or assessment were a reference to a matter

relevant to the administration or operation of this Division.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

214-130  Tax agents

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Part&#160;VIIA of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies in

relation to a return given, or objection made, for the purposes of this

Division as it applies to an income tax return or objection.

 </dl></dl>

214-135  Interpretation

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If an expression is defined in this Division, it has the meaning given in

that definition, and not the meaning given in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

_Taxation Administration Act 1953_

 </dl></dl>

19  Application

(1)	The amendment made by item&#160;1 of this Schedule applies to distributions made after 30&#160;June 2002.
 (2)	The amendment made by item&#160;2 of this Schedule applies where the franking periods to which the notice relates occur after 30&#160;June 2002.
 (3)	The amendments made by items&#160;3 to 12 and item&#160;16 of this Schedule apply to income years ending after 30&#160;June 2002.

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;29&#151;Consequential amendments relating to the simplified imputation system

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_

1  Subsection 6(1)

_franked part_ of a distribution has the same meaning as in the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

2  Subsection 6(1)

Insert:

<center>Back to Top</center>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_part of a distribution that is franked with an exempting credit_ has the same meaning as in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

3  Subsection 6(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_part of a distribution that is franked with a venture capital credit_ has the same meaning as in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

4  Subsection 6(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_unfranked part_ of a distribution has the same meaning as in the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

5  Subsection 46AA(2)

Repeal the subsection.

6  Section&#160;46AD

 Repeal the section.

7  Subsection 46F(1) (definition of _unfranked part_)

Repeal the definition, substitute:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_unfranked part_ of a dividend includes a dividend that is

unfrankable under the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_.

 </dl></dl>

8  Paragraph 128B(3)(aaa)

Repeal the paragraph, substitute:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(aaa)</dt><dd>income that consists of a non-share dividend that is unfrankable under

section&#160;215-10 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

9  Paragraph 128B(3)(ga)

Repeal the paragraph, substitute:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(ga)</dt><dd>income that consists of the franked part of a dividend, or the part of a

dividend that is franked with an exempting credit (other than a dividend in

respect of which a determination is made under paragraph 204-30(3)(c) of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ or a dividend or a part of a dividend in

respect of which a determination is made under paragraph 177EA(5)(b)); or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

respect of the distribution under section&#160;128TC; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

11  Section&#160;177EA

 Repeal the section, substitute: 

177EA  Creation of franking debit or cancellation of franking credits

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>In this section, unless the contrary intention appears:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_relevant circumstances_ has a meaning affected by

subsection&#160;(17). _relevant taxpayer_ has the meaning given by subsection&#160;(3). _scheme for a disposition_, in relation to membership interests or an interest in membership interests, has a meaning affected by subsection&#160;(14).  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An expression used in this section that is defined in the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ has the same meaning as in that Act, except to the

extent that its meaning is extended by subsection&#160;(16), (18) or (19), or

affected by subsection&#160;(15).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Application of section_

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>This section applies if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>there is a scheme for a disposition of membership interests, or an

interest in membership interests, in a corporate tax entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a frankable distribution has been paid, or is payable or expected to be

payable, to a person in respect of the membership interests; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a frankable distribution has flowed indirectly, or flows indirectly or is

expected to flow indirectly, to a person in respect of the interest in

membership interests, as the case may be; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the distribution was, or is expected to be, a franked distribution or a

distribution franked with an exempting credit; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>except for this section, the person (the _relevant_

_taxpayer_) would receive, or could reasonably be expected to

receive, imputation benefits as a result of the distribution; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>having regard to the relevant circumstances of the scheme, it would be

concluded that the person, or one of the persons, who entered into or carried

out the scheme or any part of the scheme did so for a purpose (whether or not

the dominant purpose but not including an incidental purpose) of enabling the

relevant taxpayer to obtain an imputation benefit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Bare acquisition of membership interests or interest in membership interests_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>It is not to be concluded for the purposes of paragraph&#160;(3)(e) that a

person entered into or carried out a scheme for a purpose mentioned in that

paragraph merely because the person acquired membership interests, or an

interest in membership interests, in the entity.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Commissioner to determine franking debit or deny franking credit_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may make, in writing, either of the following

determinations:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the corporate tax entity is a party to the scheme, a determination that

a franking debit or exempting debit of the entity arises in respect of each

distribution made to the relevant taxpayer or that flows indirectly to the

relevant taxpayer;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a determination that no imputation benefit is to arise in respect of a

distribution or a specified part of a distribution that is made, or that flows

indirectly, to the relevant taxpayer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A determination does not form part of an assessment.

_Notice of determination_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the Commissioner makes a determination under subsection&#160;(5), the

Commissioner must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in respect of a determination made under paragraph&#160;(5)(a)&#151;serve

notice in writing of the determination on the corporate tax entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in respect of a determination made under paragraph&#160;(5)(b)&#151;serve

notice in writing of the determination on the relevant taxpayer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The notice may be included in a notice of assessment.

_Publication in national newspaper of determination in relation to listed public company denying imputation benefit_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>If the Commissioner makes a determination under paragraph&#160;(5)(b), in

respect of a distribution made by a listed public company, the Commissioner is

taken to have served notice in writing of the determination on the relevant

taxpayer if the Commissioner causes the notice to be published in a daily

newspaper that circulates generally in each State, the Australian Capital

Territory and the Northern Territory. The notice is taken to have been served

on the day on which the publication takes place.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Evidence of determination_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>The production of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a notice of a determination; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a document signed by the Commissioner, a Second Commissioner or a Deputy

Commissioner purporting to be a copy of a determination;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is conclusive evidence:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>of the due making of the determination; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>except in proceedings under Part&#160;IVC of the _Taxation Administration Act 1953_ on an appeal or review relating to the

determination, that the determination is correct.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Objections_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>If a taxpayer to whom a determination relates is dissatisfied with the

determination, the taxpayer may object against it in the manner set out in

Part&#160;IVC of the _Taxation Administration Act 1953_.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Effect of determination of franking debit or exempting debit_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(10)</dt><dd>If the Commissioner makes a determination under paragraph&#160;(5)(a):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>on the day on which notice in writing of the determination is served on

the entity, a franking debit or exempting debit of the corporate tax entity

arises in respect of the distribution; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount of the franking debit or exempting debit is such amount as is

stated in the Commissioner's determination, being an amount that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the Commissioner considers reasonable in the circumstances; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>does not exceed the amount of the franking debit or exempting debit of

the entity arising under item&#160;1 of the table in section&#160;205-30 of the

_Income Tax Assessment 1997_ or item&#160;2 of the table in

section&#160;208-120 of that Act in respect of the distribution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Effect of determination that no imputation benefit is to arise_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(11)</dt><dd>If the Commissioner makes a determination under paragraph&#160;(5)(b),

the determination has effect according to its terms.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Application of section to non-share dividends_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(12)</dt><dd>This section:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>applies to a non-share equity interest in the same way as it applies to a

membership interest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>applies to an equity holder in the same way as it applies to a member;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>applies to a non-share dividend in the same way as it applies to a

distribution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Meaning of interest in membership interests_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(13)</dt><dd>A person has an interest in membership interests if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has any legal or equitable interest in the membership

interests; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person is a partner in a partnership and:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the assets of the partnership include, or will include, the membership

interests; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the partnership derives, or will derive, income indirectly through

interposed companies, trusts or partnerships, from distributions made on the

membership interests; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person is a beneficiary of a trust (including a potential beneficiary

of a discretionary trust) and:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the membership interests form, or will form, part of the trust estate;

or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the trust derives, or will derive, income indirectly through interposed

companies, trusts or partnerships, from distributions made on the membership

interests.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Meaning of scheme for a disposition_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(14)</dt><dd>A scheme for a disposition of membership interests or an interest in

membership interests includes, but is not limited to, a scheme that involves

any of the following:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>issuing the membership interests or creating the interest in membership

interests;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>entering into any contract, arrangement, transaction or dealing that

changes or otherwise affects the legal or equitable ownership of the membership

interests or interest in membership interests;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>creating, varying or revoking a trust in relation to the membership

interests or interest in membership interests;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>creating, altering or extinguishing a right, power or liability attaching

to, or otherwise relating to, the membership interests or interest in

membership interests;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>substantially altering any of the risks of loss, or opportunities for

profit or gain, involved in holding or owning the membership interests or

having the interest in membership interests;</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the membership interests or interest in membership interests beginning to

be included, or ceasing to be included, in any of the insurance funds of a life

assurance company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(15)</dt><dd>In determining whether a distribution flows indirectly to a person,

assume that the following provisions had not been enacted:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;282B, 283 or 297B of this Act (certain income derived by an

eligible entity within the meaning of Part&#160;IX of that Act); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>paragraph 320-35(1)(b) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

(segregated exempt assets) or subparagraph 320-35(1)(f)(ii) of that Act (income

bonds, funeral policies and scholarship plans).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_When imputation benefit is received_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(16)</dt><dd>A taxpayer to whom a distribution flows indirectly receives an

_imputation benefit_ as a result of the distribution if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the taxpayer is entitled to a tax offset under Division&#160;207 of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as a result of the distribution; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>where the taxpayer is a corporate tax entity&#151;a franking credit would

arise in the franking account of the taxpayer as a result of the distribution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Where the distribution is made directly to the taxpayer,

see subsection 204-30(6) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ for a

definition of _imputation benefit_.

 </dl></dl>

_Meaning of relevant circumstances of scheme_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(17)</dt><dd>The _relevant circumstances_ of a scheme include the

following:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the extent and duration of the risks of loss, and the opportunities for

profit or gain, from holding membership interests, or having interests in

membership interests, in the corporate tax entity that are respectively borne

by or accrue to the parties to the scheme, and whether there has been any

change in those risks and opportunities for the relevant taxpayer or any other

party to the scheme (for example, a change resulting from the making of any

contract, the granting of any option or the entering into of any arrangement

with respect to any membership interests, or interests in membership interests,

in the corporate tax entity);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>whether the relevant taxpayer would, in the year of income in which the

distribution is made, or if the distribution flows indirectly to the relevant

taxpayer, in the year in which the distribution flows indirectly to the

relevant taxpayer, derive a greater benefit from franking credits than other

entities who hold membership interests, or have interests in membership

interests, in the corporate tax entity;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>whether, apart from the scheme, the corporate tax entity would have

retained the franking credits or exempting credits or would have used the

franking credits or exempting credits to pay a franked distribution to another

entity referred to in paragraph&#160;(b);</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>whether, apart from the scheme, a franked distribution would have flowed

indirectly to another entity referred to in paragraph&#160;(b);</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>if the scheme involves the issue of a non-share equity interest to which

section&#160;215-10 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ applies&#151;whether the corporate tax entity has issued, or is likely to

issue, equity interests in the corporate tax entity:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that are similar, from a commercial point of view, to the non-share equity

interest; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>distributions in respect of which are frankable;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>whether any consideration paid or given by or on behalf of, or received by

or on behalf of, the relevant taxpayer in connection with the scheme (for

example, the amount of any interest on a loan) was calculated by reference to

the imputation benefits to be received by the relevant taxpayer;</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>whether a deduction is allowable or a capital loss is incurred in

connection with a distribution that is made or that flows indirectly under the

scheme;</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>whether a distribution that is made or that flows indirectly under the

scheme to the relevant taxpayer is equivalent to the receipt by the relevant

taxpayer of interest or of an amount in the nature of, or similar to,

interest;</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period for which the relevant taxpayer held membership interests, or

had an interest in membership interests, in the corporate tax entity;</dd>

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>any of the matters referred to in subparagraphs 177D(b)(i) to (viii).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Meaning of greater benefit from franking credits_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(18)</dt><dd>The following subsection lists some of the cases in which a taxpayer to

whom a distribution flows indirectly receives a _greater benefit from franking credits_ than an entity referred to in paragraph&#160;(17)(b).

It is not an exhaustive list.</dd> <dt>(19)</dt><dd>A taxpayer to whom a distribution flows indirectly receives a _greater benefit from franking credits_ than an entity referred to in paragraph&#160;(17)(b) if any of the following circumstances exist in relation to that entity in the income year in which the distribution giving rise to the benefit is made, and not in relation to the taxpayer if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity is not an Australian resident; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity  would not be entitled to any tax offset under

Division&#160;207 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ because of the

distribution; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the amount of income tax that would be payable by the entity because of

the distribution is less than the tax offset to which the entity would be

entitled; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity  is a corporate tax entity at the time the distribution

is made, but no franking credit arises for the entity as a result of the

distribution; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the entity  is a corporate tax entity at the time the distribution

is made, but cannot use franking credits received on the distribution to frank

distributions to its own members because:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>it is not a franking entity; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>it is unable to make frankable distributions.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Where the distribution is made directly to the taxpayer,

see subsections 204-30(7), (8), (9) and (10) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ for a list of circumstances in which the taxpayer will be treated

as deriving a greater benefit from franking credits than another entity.

 </dl></dl>

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

12  Section&#160;975-505 (link note)

Repeal the link note.

13  After Division&#160;975

Insert: 

Division&#160;976&#151;Imputation

Table of sections

976-1	Franked part of a distribution
 976-5	Unfranked part of a distribution
 976-10	The part of a distribution that is franked with an exempting credit
 976-15	The part of a distribution that is franked with a venture capital credit 

976-1  Franked part of a distribution

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The _franked part_ of a <sup>*</sup>distribution is an amount

worked out using the formula:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1223.gif)</sub>

976-5  Unfranked part of a distribution

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The _unfranked part_ of a <sup>*</sup>distribution is the amount

that is left after deducting the <sup>*</sup>franked part of the distribution

from the total distribution.

 </dl></dl>

976-10  The part of a distribution that is franked with an exempting credit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The _part of a distribution that is franked with an exempting credit_ is worked out using the formula:

 </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1224.gif)</sub>

976-15  The part of a distribution that is franked with a venture capital credit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The _part of a distribution that is franked with a venture capital credit_ is worked out using the formula:

 </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01305/Html/E57874EEABE1E617CA256F710056FCBC/$FILE/1225.gif)</sub>

14  Application

 (1)	The amendments made by items&#160;8 to 10 of this Schedule apply to income derived after 30&#160;June 2002.
 (2)	The amendment made by item&#160;11 of this Schedule applies to distributions that are made or that flow indirectly after 30&#160;June 2002.

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2003Schedule&#160;30&#151;The effect of a cum dividend sale or securities lending arrangement under the simplified imputation system 
**</center>

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

1  After Division&#160;215

 Insert: 

Division&#160;216&#151;Cum dividend sales and securities lending

arrangements

Table of Subdivisions

216-A	Circumstances where a distribution to a member of a corporate tax entity is treated as having been made to someone else
 216-B	Statements to be made where there is a cum dividend sale or securities lending arrangement 

Subdivision&#160;216-A&#151;Circumstances where a distribution to a

member of a corporate tax entity is treated as having been made to someone

else

Table of sections

216-1	When a distribution made to a member of a corporate tax entity is treated as having been made to someone else
 216-5	First situation (cum dividend sales)
 216-10	Second situation (securities lending arrangements)
 216-15	Distribution closing time 

216-1  When a distribution made to a member of a corporate tax entity is treated as having been made to someone else

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		There are 2 situations in which a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution, or a

distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting credit, that is made to a

<sup>*</sup>member of a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity is taken to have been

made to another entity.

 </dl></dl>

216-5  First situation (cum dividend sales)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The first situation is one in which:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity makes a <sup>*</sup>franked

distribution, or a <sup>*</sup>distribution franked with an exempting credit,

to a <sup>*</sup>member of the entity in respect of a <sup>*</sup>membership

interest in the entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the <sup>*</sup>distribution closing time, the member is under an

obligation to transfer the membership interest to another person under a

contract for the sale of the membership interest; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the contract:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>requires that the distribution be paid on to the other person; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is entered into in the ordinary course of trading on an

<sup>*</sup>approved stock exchange in Australia or elsewhere.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>distribution is taken to have been made to the other

person as a <sup>*</sup>member of the entity (and not to the member).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	As the other person is the entity receiving the

distribution, there may be tax effects for the other person under

Division&#160;207 or 208.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>distribution referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a) includes

a distribution that is taken to be made as a result of one or more previous

applications of this section or section&#160;216-10.

</dd> </dl></dl>

216-10  Second situation (securities lending arrangements)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The second situation is one in which:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity makes a <sup>*</sup>franked

distribution, or a <sup>*</sup>distribution franked with an exempting credit,

to a <sup>*</sup>member of the entity in respect of a <sup>*</sup>membership

interest in the entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the time the distribution was made, the member was under an obligation

to pay the distribution to another person under a <sup>*</sup>securities

lending arrangement; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the obligation was incurred in the member's capacity as the borrower under

the securities lending arrangement; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>distribution closing time occurred during the borrowing

period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>distribution is taken to have been made to the other

person as a <sup>*</sup>member of the entity (and not to the member).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	As the other person is the entity receiving the

distribution, there may be tax effects for the other person under

Division&#160;207 or 208.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The distribution referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a) includes a

distribution that is taken to be made as a result of one or more previous

applications of this section or section&#160;216-5.

</dd> </dl></dl>

216-15  Distribution closing time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If <sup>*</sup>distributions by a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity are made

to those <sup>*</sup>members who were members as at a particular time at or

before the distribution is made, that time is the _distribution closing time_ in relation to those distributions.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;216-B&#151;Statements to be made where there is a cum

dividend sale or securities lending arrangement

Table of sections

216-20	Cum dividend sale&#151;statement by securities dealer
 216-25	Cum dividend sale&#151;statement by party
 216-30	Securities lending arrangements&#151;statement by borrower 

216-20  Cum dividend sale&#151;statement by securities dealer

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;216-5 applies in relation to a <sup>*</sup>franked

distribution or a <sup>*</sup>distribution franked with an exempting credit

(cum dividend sales); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>securities dealer has acted for a particular party to the

contract concerned;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the securities dealer must, as soon as practicable after the making of the distribution, give to the other party to the contract a statement in the <sup>*</sup>approved form setting out such information in relation to the distribution as is required by the approved form. 

216-25  Cum dividend sale&#151;statement by party

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;216-5 applies in relation to a <sup>*</sup>franked

distribution or a <sup>*</sup>distribution franked with an exempting credit

(cum dividend sales); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a particular party to the contract concerned has not had a

<sup>*</sup>securities dealer acting for him or her;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

that party must, as soon as practicable after the making of the distribution, give to the other party to the contract a statement in the <sup>*</sup>approved form setting out such information in relation to the distribution as is required by the approved form. 

216-30  Securities lending arrangements&#151;statement by borrower

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If section&#160;216-10 (<sup>*</sup>securities lending arrangements) applies

in relation to a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution, or a

<sup>*</sup>distribution franked with an exempting credit, the borrower must,

as soon as practicable after the making of the distribution, give to the lender

a statement in the <sup>*</sup>approved form setting out such information in

relation to the distribution as is required by the approved form.

 </dl></dl>

2  Application

The amendments made by this Schedule apply to distributions made after 30&#160;June 2002.
